================================================================================
MAYA AI Assistant - Comprehensive Technical Report
================================================================================

Generated on: 2026-06-21 16:38:51.282070

1. Executive Summary
--------------------
MAYA is an extensible, multi-agent AI assistant designed to automate complex workflows,
fetch data from external APIs, and provide hands-free voice interaction. This technical
report outlines the system architecture, the purpose of each specialized agent, and
provides an in-depth source code review and API reference for the entire platform.

2. System Architecture Overview
-------------------------------
The system relies on a plugin-based architecture. A central 'Brain' coordinates requests
and delegates them to individual 'Agents'. Each agent is self-contained and exposes
a standard `execute` method that takes JSON input and returns JSON output.

3. Detailed Module Analysis
---------------------------

================================================================================
Module: build_registry.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
build_registry.py — Scan agents/ and generate the complete registry system.

Produces:
    system/agent_registry.json        — per-agent metadata + actions
    system/action_registry.json       — flat action→agent lookup
    system/agent_capabilities.json    — capability matrix
    system/planner_context.json       — LLM-planner-optimised metadata
    system/generated_docs/            — one Markdown file per agent

Run from the project root:

    python build_registry.py

Re-run any time a new agent is added or an existing one changes.


Functions:
  - _load_agent_module
    Docstring: Import an agent module by file path without executing its CLI....
  - _discover_agents
    Docstring: Scan agents/ and extract metadata from each agent module....
  - _build_agent_registry
  - _build_action_registry
  - _build_capabilities
  - _build_planner_context
  - _generate_agent_doc
    Docstring: Generate a Markdown documentation file for one agent....
  - _write_json
  - _write_text
  - _validate
    Docstring: Return a list of validation warnings (empty = all good)....
  - main

0433 | # ── agent loader ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0434 | def _load_agent_module(path: Path) -> Any:
0435 |     """Import an agent module by file path without executing its CLI."""
0436 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(path.stem, str(path))
0437 |     if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
0438 |         raise ImportError(f"Cannot load {path}")
0439 |     module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
0440 |     sys.modules[path.stem] = module
0441 |     spec.loader.exec_module(module)
0442 |     return module
0443 | 
0444 | 
0445 | def _discover_agents() -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0446 |     """Scan agents/ and extract metadata from each agent module."""
0447 |     agents: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0448 | 
0449 |     for py_file in sorted(AGENTS_DIR.glob("*.py")):
0450 |         if py_file.name.startswith("_"):
0451 |             continue
0452 | 
0453 |         try:
0454 |             module = _load_agent_module(py_file)
0455 |         except Exception as exc:
0456 |             print(f"  WARN: could not import {py_file.name}: {exc}")
0457 |             continue
0458 | 
0459 |         plugin_info = getattr(module, "PLUGIN_INFO", None)
0460 |         if plugin_info is None:
0461 |             print(f"  SKIP: {py_file.name} has no PLUGIN_INFO")
0462 |             continue
0463 | 
0464 |         actions_dict = getattr(module, "_ACTIONS", {})
0465 |         required_params = getattr(module, "_REQUIRED_PARAMS", {})
0466 |         agent_name = plugin_info.get("name", py_file.stem)
0467 | 
0468 |         optional_params = _OPTIONAL_PARAMS.get(agent_name, {})
0469 |         extra_meta = _AGENT_META.get(agent_name, {})
0470 |         examples = _EXAMPLES.get(agent_name, {})
0471 | 
0472 |         action_list: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0473 |         for action_name in sorted(actions_dict.keys()):
0474 |             handler = actions_dict[action_name]
0475 |             doc = (handler.__doc__ or "").strip().split("\n")[0]
0476 | 
0477 |             action_entry: dict[str, Any] = {
0478 |                 "name": action_name,
0479 |                 "description": doc,
0480 |                 "required_params": required_params.get(action_name, []),
0481 |                 "optional_params": optional_params.get(action_name, []),
0482 |             }
0483 | 
0484 |             if action_name in examples:
0485 |                 action_entry["example_input"] = examples[action_name]["input"]
0486 |                 action_entry["example_output_summary"] = examples[action_name]["output_summary"]
0487 | 
0488 |             action_list.append(action_entry)
0489 | 
0490 |         agent_entry: dict[str, Any] = {
0491 |             "name": agent_name,
0492 |             "agent_name": plugin_info.get("agent_name", agent_name),
0493 |             "version": plugin_info.get("version", "0.0.0"),
0494 |             "type": plugin_info.get("type", "tool"),
0495 |             "description": plugin_info.get("description", ""),

0563 | def _build_planner_context(agents: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0564 |     entries: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0565 |     for agent in agents:
0566 |         compact_actions: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0567 |         for action in agent["actions"]:
0568 |             entry: dict[str, Any] = {
0569 |                 "name": action["name"],
0570 |                 "required_params": action["required_params"],
0571 |             }
0572 |             if action["optional_params"]:
0573 |                 entry["optional_params"] = action["optional_params"]
0574 |             if action["description"]:
0575 |                 entry["description"] = action["description"]
0576 |             compact_actions.append(entry)
0577 | 
0578 |         entries.append({
0579 |             "agent": agent["name"],
0580 |             "purpose": agent["description"],
0581 |             "type": agent["type"],
0582 |             "keywords": agent["keywords"],
0583 |             "actions": compact_actions,
0584 |         })
0585 |     return {
0586 |         "version": "1.0.0",
0587 |         "generated_at": datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc).isoformat(),
0588 |         "instruction": (
0589 |             "Use this context to decide which agent and action to invoke. "
0590 |             "Match user intent against keywords, then select the action whose "
0591 |             "required_params you can fill from the user's request. "
0592 |             "For project_tracker_agent: you can pass 'project_name' instead of "
0593 |             "'project_id' — the agent will resolve the name to an ID automatically."
0594 |         ),
0595 |         "agents": entries,
0596 |     }
0597 |

0599 | def _generate_agent_doc(agent: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
0600 |     """Generate a Markdown documentation file for one agent."""
0601 |     lines: list[str] = []
0602 |     lines.append(f"# {agent['agent_name']}")

0604 |     lines.append(f"**Module:** `{agent['file']}`  ")
0605 |     lines.append(f"**Version:** {agent['version']}  ")
0606 |     lines.append(f"**Type:** {agent['type']}  ")
0607 |     lines.append(f"**Entrypoint:** `{agent['entrypoint']}`  ")
0608 |     lines.append("")
0609 |

0611 |         lines.append(f"## Purpose")
0612 |         lines.append("")

0617 |         lines.append("## Keywords")

0623 |         lines.append("## Suggested Use Cases")
0624 |         lines.append("")
0625 |         for uc in agent["suggested_use_cases"]:
0626 |             lines.append(f"- {uc}")
0627 |         lines.append("")
0628 | 
0629 |     if agent["avoid_use_cases"]:
0630 |         lines.append("## Avoid Use Cases")
0631 |         lines.append("")
0632 |         for uc in agent["avoid_use_cases"]:
0633 |             lines.append(f"- {uc}")
0634 |         lines.append("")
0635 |

0637 |     lines.append("")
0638 | 
0639 |     for action in agent["actions"]:
0640 |         lines.append(f"### `{action['name']}`")
0641 |         lines.append("")
0642 |         if action["description"]:
0643 |             lines.append(action["description"])
0644 |             lines.append("")
0645 |

0647 |             lines.append("**Required parameters:**")

0677 | 
0678 | def _write_json(path: Path, data: Any) -> None:
0679 |     path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
0680 |     path.write_text(
0681 |         json.dumps(data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
0682 |         encoding="utf-8",
0683 |     )
0684 |     print(f"  wrote {path.relative_to(PROJECT_ROOT)}")
0685 | 
0686 | 
0687 | def _write_text(path: Path, content: str) -> None:
0688 |     path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
0689 |     path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
0690 |     print(f"  wrote {path.relative_to(PROJECT_ROOT)}")
0691 | 
0692 | 
0693 | # ── validation ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0694 | def _validate(agents: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> list[str]:
0695 |     """Return a list of validation warnings (empty = all good)."""
0696 |     warnings: list[str] = []
0697 | 
0698 |     for agent in agents:
0699 |         if not agent["description"]:
0700 |             warnings.append(f"{agent['name']}: missing description in PLUGIN_INFO")
0701 |         if not agent["keywords"]:
0702 |             warnings.append(f"{agent['name']}: no keywords defined")
0703 |         if agent["action_count"] == 0:
0704 |             warnings.append(f"{agent['name']}: no actions discovered")
0705 |         for action in agent["actions"]:
0706 |             if not action["description"]:
0707 |                 warnings.append(f"{agent['name']}.{action['name']}: missing docstring")
0708 | 
0709 |     return warnings
0710 | 
0711 | 
0712 | # ── main ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0713 | def main() -> int:
0714 |     print("build_registry: scanning agents/\n")
0715 | 
0716 |     if not AGENTS_DIR.is_dir():
0717 |         print(f"ERROR: agents/ directory not found at {AGENTS_DIR}")
0718 |         return 1
0719 | 
0720 |     agents = _discover_agents()
0721 | 
0722 |     if not agents:
0723 |         print("\nERROR: no agents discovered")
0724 |         return 1
0725 | 
0726 |     print(f"\nDiscovered {len(agents)} agents, generating registry files...\n")
0727 | 
0728 |     agent_registry = _build_agent_registry(agents)
0729 |     action_registry = _build_action_registry(agents)
0730 |     capabilities = _build_capabilities(agents)
0731 |     planner_context = _build_planner_context(agents)
0732 | 
0733 |     _write_json(SYSTEM_DIR / "agent_registry.json", agent_registry)
0734 |     _write_json(SYSTEM_DIR / "action_registry.json", action_registry)
0735 |     _write_json(SYSTEM_DIR / "agent_capabilities.json", capabilities)
0736 |     _write_json(SYSTEM_DIR / "planner_context.json", planner_context)
0737 | 
0738 |     print()
0739 |     for agent in agents:
0740 |         doc = _generate_agent_doc(agent)
0741 |         doc_path = DOCS_DIR / f"{agent['name']}.md"
0742 |         _write_text(doc_path, doc)
0743 | 
0744 |     warnings = _validate(agents)
0745 |     if warnings:
0746 |         print(f"\nValidation warnings ({len(warnings)}):")
0747 |         for w in warnings:
0748 |             print(f"  ! {w}")
0749 |     else:
0750 |         print("\nValidation: all checks passed")
0751 | 
0752 |     total_actions = sum(a["action_count"] for a in agents)
0753 |     print(f"\nDone. {len(agents)} agents, {total_actions} actions registered.")
0754 |     return 0
0755 | 
0756 | 
0757 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0758 |     raise SystemExit(main())

0008 |

0010 |     print('='*40)
0011 |     print(os.path.basename(path))
0012 |     for node in tree.body:
0013 |         if isinstance(node, ast.AnnAssign):

0016 |                 if target.id == 'PLUGIN_INFO':
0017 |                     try:
0018 |                         val = ast.literal_eval(node.value)

0009 | def get_python_files(root_dir):
0010 |     py_files = []
0011 |     for dirpath, _, filenames in os.walk(root_dir):
0012 |         if '__pycache__' in dirpath or '.pytest_cache' in dirpath:
0013 |             continue
0014 |         for f in filenames:
0015 |             if f.endswith('.py'):

0130 |                     models.add(name.split(":")[0])
0131 |         return models
0132 |     except Exception:
0133 |         return set()
0134 | 
0135 | 
0136 | def _check_model(model_name: str, available: set[str]) -> bool:
0137 |     base = model_name.split(":")[0]
0138 |     if model_name in available or base in available:
0139 |         _ok(f"Model: {model_name}")
0140 |         return True
0141 |     _fail(f"Model: {model_name} — not found")
0142 |     return False
0143 | 
0144 | 
0145 | def _check_registry() -> bool:
0146 |     reg = PROJECT_ROOT / "system" / "agent_registry.json"
0147 |     if reg.exists():
0148 |         with open(reg) as f:
0149 |             data = json.load(f)
0150 |         count = len(data) if isinstance(data, (list, dict)) else 0
0151 |         _ok(f"Agent registry ({count} agents)")
0152 |         return True
0153 |     _fail("Agent registry missing — run: python build_registry.py")
0154 |     return False
0155 | 
0156 | 
0157 | def _check_agents() -> int:
0158 |     agents_dir = PROJECT_ROOT / "agents"
0159 |     if not agents_dir.is_dir():
0160 |         _fail("agents/ directory not found")
0161 |         return 0
0162 |     agents = list(agents_dir.glob("*_agent.py"))
0163 |     _ok(f"{len(agents)} agents found")
0164 |     return len(agents)
0165 |

0167 | def _check_directories() -> None:
0168 |     dirs = [
0169 |         PROJECT_ROOT / "brain" / "logs",
0170 |         PROJECT_ROOT / "memory" / "active_chat",
0171 |         PROJECT_ROOT / "memory" / "archive",
0172 |         PROJECT_ROOT / "memory" / "chat_summaries",
0173 |         PROJECT_ROOT / "memory" / "vector_db",

0179 |             created += 1

0183 |         _ok("All directories exist")

0185 | 
0186 | def run_checks(*, voice: bool = True) -> dict:
0187 |     """Run all prerequisite checks. Returns a status dict."""
0188 |     results = {
0189 |         "python": False,
0190 |         "packages": False,
0191 |         "voice_packages": False,
0192 |         "ollama": False,
0193 |         "models": False,
0194 |         "registry": False,
0195 |         "agents": 0,
0196 |     }
0197 | 
0198 |     _header("Python")
0199 |     results["python"] = _check_python_version()
0200 | 
0201 |     _header("Core Packages")
0202 |     pkg_ok = all(_check_package(mod, pip) for mod, pip in _REQUIRED_PACKAGES)
0203 |     results["packages"] = pkg_ok
0204 | 
0205 |     if voice:
0206 |         _header("Voice Packages")
0207 |         vpkg_ok = all(_check_package(mod, pip) for mod, pip in _VOICE_PACKAGES)
0208 |         results["voice_packages"] = vpkg_ok
0209 | 
0210 |     _header("Ollama")
0211 |     results["ollama"] = _check_ollama_running()
0212 | 
0213 |     if results["ollama"]:
0214 |         _header("LLM Models")
0215 |         available = _get_ollama_models()
0216 |         from brain.utils.config import PLANNER_MODEL, RESPONSE_MODEL
0217 |         p = _check_model(PLANNER_MODEL, available)
0218 |         r = _check_model(RESPONSE_MODEL, available)
0219 |         results["models"] = p and r
0220 |         if not p:
0221 |             _info(f"Pull with: ollama pull {PLANNER_MODEL}")
0222 |         if not r:
0223 |             _info(f"Pull with: ollama pull {RESPONSE_MODEL}")
0224 | 
0225 |     _header("Agent System")
0226 |     results["registry"] = _check_registry()
0227 |     results["agents"] = _check_agents()
0228 | 
0229 |     _header("Directories")
0230 |     _check_directories()
0231 | 
0232 |     return results

0235 | # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
0236 | # Install missing packages
0237 | # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
0238 | 
0239 | def install_packages(include_voice: bool = True) -> bool:
0240 |     _header("Installing Dependencies")
0241 |     packages = [pip for _, pip in _REQUIRED_PACKAGES]
0242 |     if include_voice:
0243 |         packages += [pip for _, pip in _VOICE_PACKAGES]
0244 | 
0245 |     missing = []
0246 |     for mod, pip_name in _REQUIRED_PACKAGES + (_VOICE_PACKAGES if include_voice else []):
0247 |         try:
0248 |             importlib.import_module(mod)
0249 |         except ImportError:
0250 |             missing.append(pip_name)
0251 | 
0252 |     if not missing:
0253 |         _ok("All packages already installed")
0254 |         return True
0255 | 
0256 |     _info(f"Installing {len(missing)} packages: {', '.join(missing)}")
0257 |     try:
0258 |         subprocess.check_call(
0259 |             [sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "install"] + missing,
0260 |             stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL,
0261 |             stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
0262 |         )
0263 |         _ok("Installation complete")
0264 |         return True
0265 |     except subprocess.CalledProcessError:
0266 |         _fail("pip install failed — check errors above")
0267 |         return False
0268 | 
0269 | 
0270 | # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
0271 | # Pull missing models
0272 | # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
0273 | 
0274 | def pull_models() -> bool:
0275 |     _header("Pulling LLM Models")
0276 |     try:
0277 |         from brain.utils.config import PLANNER_MODEL, RESPONSE_MODEL
0278 |         available = _get_ollama_models()
0279 |         models_needed = []
0280 | 
0281 |         for model in [PLANNER_MODEL, RESPONSE_MODEL]:
0282 |             base = model.split(":")[0]
0283 |             if model not in available and base not in available:
0284 |                 models_needed.append(model)
0285 | 
0286 |         if not models_needed:
0287 |             _ok("All models already available")
0288 |             return True
0289 | 
0290 |         for model in models_needed:
0291 |             _info(f"Pulling {model}... (this may take a while)")
0292 |             try:
0293 |                 subprocess.check_call(
0294 |                     ["ollama", "pull", model],
0295 |                     timeout=1800,  # 30 min max
0296 |                 )
0297 |                 _ok(f"Pulled {model}")
0298 |             except subprocess.CalledProcessError:
0299 |                 _fail(f"Failed to pull {model}")
0300 |                 return False
0301 |             except FileNotFoundError:
0302 |                 _fail("ollama command not found — install from https://ollama.com")
0303 |                 return False
0304 | 
0305 |         return True
0306 |     except Exception as exc:
0307 |         _fail(f"Error: {exc}")
0308 |         return False

0394 |     """Text input with voice output — type commands, hear responses."""
0395 |     _header("Starting MAYA — Text + Voice Mode")
0396 |     print(f"  {_DIM}Type your commands. MAYA speaks the responses. 'quit' to stop.{_RESET}\n")
0397 | 
0398 |     from brain.brain import Brain
0399 |     import maya_tts
0400 |

0402 |     _ok("Brain initialized with memory\n")
0403 | 
0404 |     while True:
0405 |         try:
0406 |             command = input(f"{_CYAN}You:{_RESET} ").strip()
0407 |         except (KeyboardInterrupt, EOFError):
0408 |             print(f"\n{_DIM}Goodbye.{_RESET}")
0409 |             break
0410 |         if not command:
0411 |             continue
0412 |         if command.lower() in ("quit", "exit", "bye", "q"):
0413 |             maya_tts.speak("Goodbye.")
0414 |             break
0415 |         try:
0416 |             start = time.perf_counter()
0417 |             response = brain.process(command)
0418 |             elapsed = time.perf_counter() - start
0419 |             print(f"{_GREEN}MAYA:{_RESET} {response}")
0420 |             print(f"{_DIM}  [{elapsed:.1f}s]{_RESET}")
0421 |             maya_tts.speak(response)
0422 |             print()
0423 |         except KeyboardInterrupt:
0424 |             maya_tts.request_stop()
0425 |             print(f"\n{_YELLOW}  Cancelled.{_RESET}\n")
0426 |         except Exception as exc:
0427 |             print(f"{_RED}  Error: {exc}{_RESET}\n")

0430 | def start_voice_text_mode() -> None:
0431 |     """Voice input with text output — speak commands, read responses on screen."""
0432 |     _header("Starting MAYA — Voice In + Text Out")
0433 |     print(f"  {_DIM}Say 'Maya' then your command. Responses shown as text. Ctrl+C to quit.{_RESET}\n")
0434 | 
0435 |     import numpy as np
0436 |     from voice.voice_orchestrator import (
0437 |         _ensure_loaded, _sr, _recog, _transcribe_fast, _transcribe_accurate,
0438 |         has_wake, strip_wake, _is_real_command, END_SILENCE,
0439 |     )
0440 |     from brain.brain import Brain
0441 | 
0442 |     _ensure_loaded()
0443 |     brain = Brain(enable_memory=True)
0444 |     _ok("Brain initialized with memory\n")
0445 | 
0446 |     with _sr.Microphone(sample_rate=16000) as src:
0447 |         print(f"  {_DIM}Adjusting for ambient noise...{_RESET}")
0448 |         _recog.adjust_for_ambient_noise(src, duration=1.0)
0449 |         _recog.energy_threshold = max(_recog.energy_threshold, 200)
0450 |         print(f"  {_GREEN}Ready!{_RESET} Say 'Maya' followed by your command.\n")
0451 | 
0452 |         while True:
0453 |             try:
0454 |                 audio = _recog.listen(src, phrase_time_limit=15)
0455 |             except KeyboardInterrupt:
0456 |                 print(f"\n{_DIM}Goodbye.{_RESET}")
0457 |                 break
0458 |             except Exception:
0459 |                 continue
0460 | 
0461 |             gist = _transcribe_fast(audio)
0462 |             if not gist:
0463 |                 continue
0464 |             if not has_wake(gist):
0465 |                 print(f"\r{_DIM}[idle] {gist[:60]:<60}{_RESET}", end="", flush=True)
0466 |                 continue
0467 | 
0468 |             accurate = _transcribe_accurate(audio) or gist
0469 |             command = strip_wake(accurate)
0470 |             if not command:
0471 |                 print(f"\n{_CYAN}You:{_RESET} (just the wake word)")
0472 |                 # Listen once more for the actual command
0473 |                 try:
0474 |                     follow = _recog.listen(src, timeout=8, phrase_time_limit=15)
0475 |                     command = (_transcribe_accurate(follow) or "").strip()
0476 |                 except Exception:
0477 |                     command = ""
0478 |                 if not _is_real_command(command):
0479 |                     print(f"  {_DIM}Didn't catch a command.{_RESET}\n")
0480 |                     continue
0481 | 
0482 |             print(f"\n{_CYAN}You:{_RESET} {command}")
0483 | 
0484 |             try:
0485 |                 start = time.perf_counter()
0486 |                 response = brain.process(command)
0487 |                 elapsed = time.perf_counter() - start
0488 |                 print(f"{_GREEN}MAYA:{_RESET} {response}")
0489 |                 print(f"{_DIM}  [{elapsed:.1f}s]{_RESET}\n")
0490 |             except KeyboardInterrupt:
0491 |                 print(f"\n{_YELLOW}  Cancelled.{_RESET}\n")
0492 |             except Exception as exc:
0493 |                 print(f"{_RED}  Error: {exc}{_RESET}\n")
0494 |

0635 | def main() -> None:
0636 |     if len(sys.argv) < 2:
0637 |         interactive_menu()
0638 |         return
0639 |

0641 | 
0642 |     if cmd == "voice":
0643 |         run_checks(voice=True)
0644 |         start_voice_mode()
0645 |     elif cmd == "text":
0646 |         run_checks(voice=False)
0647 |         start_text_mode()
0648 |     elif cmd in ("text-voice", "tv"):
0649 |         run_checks(voice=False)
0650 |         start_text_voice_mode()
0651 |     elif cmd in ("voice-text", "vt"):
0652 |         run_checks(voice=True)
0653 |         start_voice_text_mode()
0654 |     elif cmd == "check":
0655 |         run_checks(voice=True)
0656 |     elif cmd == "test":
0657 |         run_tests()
0658 |     elif cmd == "setup":
0659 |         setup()
0660 |     elif cmd in ("help", "--help", "-h"):
0661 |         print(__doc__)
0662 |     else:
0663 |         print(f"{_RED}Unknown command: {cmd}{_RESET}")
0664 |         print(__doc__)
0665 | 
0666 | 
0667 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0668 |     main()

================================================================================
Module: maya_tts.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
maya_tts.py
===========
Interruptible text-to-speech for MAYA.

Backends (set JARVIS_TTS_BACKEND in .env):
  * "piper"   - LOCAL neural voices (natural, fully offline once downloaded).
  * "pyttsx3" - Windows SAPI (robotic, but zero setup).
  * "sapi"    - dependency-free PowerShell SAPI fallback.

Speech is chunked by sentence and a stop flag is checked between chunks,
so barge-in halts MAYA almost immediately.

CLI:
    python maya_tts.py --list
    python maya_tts.py --download en_US-amy-medium
    python maya_tts.py "Hello, I am Maya."


Functions:
  - clean_for_speech
  - _sentences
  - request_stop
  - is_speaking

0003 | ===========
0004 | Interruptible text-to-speech for MAYA.
0005 | 
0006 | Backends (set JARVIS_TTS_BACKEND in .env):

0116 | def download_voice(name: str, dest: Path | None = None) -> Path:
0117 |     import requests
0118 |     dest = dest or VOICE_DIR
0119 |     dest.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
0120 |     sub = _hf_subpath(name)
0121 |     for ext in (".onnx", ".onnx.json"):
0122 |         path = dest / (name + ext)
0123 |         if path.exists() and path.stat().st_size > 1000:
0124 |             print(f"[tts] have {path.name}")
0125 |             continue
0126 |         url = f"{_HF}/{sub}/{name}{ext}"
0127 |         print(f"[tts] downloading {name}{ext} ...")
0128 |         r = requests.get(url, stream=True, timeout=600)
0129 |         r.raise_for_status()
0130 |         total = 0
0131 |         with open(path, "wb") as f:
0132 |             for chunk in r.iter_content(1 << 16):
0133 |                 f.write(chunk)
0134 |                 total += len(chunk)
0135 |         print(f"[tts]   saved {path.name}  ({total / 1e6:.1f} MB)")
0136 |     return dest / (name + ".onnx")

0204 | def _speak_sapi(text: str) -> None:
0205 |     safe = text.replace("'", "''")
0206 |     rate = max(-10, min(10, round((RATE - 200) / 20)))

0208 |                     f"$v=New-Object -ComObject SAPI.SpVoice; $v.Rate={rate}; $v.Speak('{safe}') | Out-Null"],
0209 |                    check=False, capture_output=True)

0213 | _ORDER = {"piper": ["piper", "sapi"], "sapi": ["sapi", "pyttsx3"], "pyttsx3": ["pyttsx3", "sapi"]}
0214 |

0216 | def _speak_one(text: str) -> None:
0217 |     for b in _ORDER.get(BACKEND, ["pyttsx3", "sapi"]):
0218 |         try:
0219 |             _FUNCS[b](text)
0220 |             return
0221 |         except Exception as exc:
0222 |             print(f"[tts:{b} failed: {exc}]", file=sys.stderr)
0223 |     print(f"[tts unavailable] {text}", file=sys.stderr)

0226 | def speak(text: str, allow_interrupt: bool = True) -> None:
0227 |     text = clean_for_speech(text)
0228 |     if not text:
0229 |         return
0230 |     with _lock:
0231 |         _stop.clear()
0232 |         _speaking.set()
0233 |         try:
0234 |             for sentence in _sentences(text):
0235 |                 if allow_interrupt and _stop.is_set():
0236 |                     break
0237 |                 _speak_one(sentence)
0238 |         finally:
0239 |             _speaking.clear()

0243 |     t = threading.Thread(target=speak, args=(text, allow_interrupt), daemon=True)

================================================================================
Module: voice_text.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
voice_text.py
=============
Speech-to-text for commands, with a LOCAL fallback.

  * Primary:  Groq Whisper (cloud, very accurate/fast) — used when reachable.
  * Backup:   a local faster-whisper model (default "small.en") — used
              automatically if Groq fails (no network, no key, error, timeout).

Set JARVIS_STT_BACKEND=local in .env to run fully offline (skip Groq entirely).
The local model loads lazily (only when first needed) and is then cached.

Entry points:
  * transcribe_array(audio_int16, sample_rate) — used by the always-on listener
  * listen_and_transcribe() — record from the mic until you stop talking, then
    transcribe. RMS is float (int16**2 overflows) and the end-of-speech timer
    only starts AFTER you actually begin speaking, so it won't clip you.


Functions:
  - _groq
  - _transcribe_groq
  - transcribe_local
  - transcribe_array
  - listen_and_transcribe

----------------------------------------
Source Code Dump
----------------------------------------
0001 | """
0002 | voice_text.py
0003 | =============
0004 | Speech-to-text for commands, with a LOCAL fallback.
0005 | 
0006 |   * Primary:  Groq Whisper (cloud, very accurate/fast) — used when reachable.
0007 |   * Backup:   a local faster-whisper model (default "small.en") — used
0008 |               automatically if Groq fails (no network, no key, error, timeout).
0009 | 
0010 | Set JARVIS_STT_BACKEND=local in .env to run fully offline (skip Groq entirely).
0011 | The local model loads lazily (only when first needed) and is then cached.
0012 | 
0013 | Entry points:
0014 |   * transcribe_array(audio_int16, sample_rate) — used by the always-on listener
0015 |   * listen_and_transcribe() — record from the mic until you stop talking, then
0016 |     transcribe. RMS is float (int16**2 overflows) and the end-of-speech timer
0017 |     only starts AFTER you actually begin speaking, so it won't clip you.
0018 | """
0019 | 
0020 | import os
0021 | import time
0022 | 
0023 | import numpy as np
0024 | import scipy.io.wavfile as wavfile
0025 | import sounddevice as sd
0026 | from dotenv import load_dotenv
0027 | 
0028 | load_dotenv()
0029 | 
0030 | SAMPLE_RATE = 16000
0031 | SILENCE_THRESHOLD = int(os.getenv("JARVIS_MIC_THRESHOLD", "350"))
0032 | END_SILENCE = float(os.getenv("JARVIS_END_SILENCE", "2.5"))
0033 | MAX_DURATION = 15.0
0034 | 
0035 | GROQ_KEY = os.environ.get("GROQ_API_KEY")
0036 | STT_BACKEND = os.getenv("JARVIS_STT_BACKEND", "groq").lower()        # "groq" | "local"
0037 | LOCAL_STT_MODEL = os.getenv("JARVIS_LOCAL_STT_MODEL", "small.en")    # tiny.en/base.en/small.en/medium.en
0038 | 
0039 | _client = None       # Groq client (lazy)
0040 | _local = None        # faster-whisper model (lazy)
0041 | 
0042 | 
0043 | # ── Groq (primary) ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0044 | def _groq():
0045 |     global _client
0046 |     if _client is None:
0047 |         from groq import Groq
0048 |         _client = Groq(api_key=GROQ_KEY)
0049 |     return _client
0050 | 
0051 | 
0052 | def _transcribe_groq(audio_int16: np.ndarray, sample_rate: int) -> str:
0053 |     tmp = "temp_recording.wav"
0054 |     try:
0055 |         wavfile.write(tmp, sample_rate, audio_int16)
0056 |         with open(tmp, "rb") as f:
0057 |             tr = _groq().audio.transcriptions.create(
0058 |                 file=("recording.wav", f.read()),
0059 |                 model="whisper-large-v3",
0060 |                 response_format="text",
0061 |             )
0062 |         return (tr or "").strip()
0063 |     finally:
0064 |         try:
0065 |             os.remove(tmp)
0066 |         except OSError:
0067 |             pass
0068 | 
0069 | 
0070 | # ── Local faster-whisper (backup / offline) ──────────────────────────────
0071 | def transcribe_local(audio_int16: np.ndarray, sample_rate: int = SAMPLE_RATE) -> str:
0072 |     global _local
0073 |     if _local is None:
0074 |         from faster_whisper import WhisperModel
0075 |         print(f"[stt] loading local model '{LOCAL_STT_MODEL}' (one-time)...")
0076 |         _local = WhisperModel(LOCAL_STT_MODEL, device="auto", compute_type="int8")
0077 |     samples = audio_int16.astype(np.float32) / 32768.0
0078 |     segments, _ = _local.transcribe(
0079 |         samples, beam_size=1, language="en", vad_filter=True,   # drop silence/noise -> fewer hallucinations
0080 |         condition_on_previous_text=False, without_timestamps=True)
0081 |     return " ".join(s.text for s in segments).strip()
0082 | 
0083 | 
0084 | # ── Unified entry point: Groq first, local fallback ──────────────────────
0085 | def transcribe_array(audio_int16: np.ndarray, sample_rate: int = SAMPLE_RATE) -> str:
0086 |     if audio_int16 is None or len(audio_int16) < sample_rate * 0.3:
0087 |         return ""
0088 |     if STT_BACKEND != "local" and GROQ_KEY:
0089 |         try:
0090 |             return _transcribe_groq(audio_int16, sample_rate)
0091 |         except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — network/api/timeout -> fall back local
0092 |             print(f"[stt] Groq unavailable ({str(exc).splitlines()[0]}); using local model.")
0093 |     return transcribe_local(audio_int16, sample_rate)
0094 | 
0095 | 
0096 | # ── Standalone recorder ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
0097 | def listen_and_transcribe() -> str:
0098 |     chunk = 0.1
0099 |     chunk_samples = int(SAMPLE_RATE * chunk)
0100 |     max_silent = max(1, int(END_SILENCE / chunk))
0101 | 
0102 |     data: list[np.ndarray] = []
0103 |     started = False        # only count trailing silence once speech has begun
0104 |     silent = 0
0105 |     recording = True
0106 | 
0107 |     def cb(indata, frames, time_info, status):
0108 |         nonlocal started, silent, recording
0109 |         if not recording:
0110 |             return
0111 |         data.append(indata.copy())
0112 |         rms = np.sqrt(np.mean(indata.astype(np.float32) ** 2))  # float -> no overflow
0113 |         if rms >= SILENCE_THRESHOLD:
0114 |             started = True
0115 |             silent = 0
0116 |         elif started:
0117 |             silent += 1
0118 |             if silent >= max_silent:
0119 |                 recording = False
0120 |                 raise sd.CallbackStop()
0121 | 
0122 |     try:
0123 |         with sd.InputStream(samplerate=SAMPLE_RATE, channels=1, dtype="int16",
0124 |                             blocksize=chunk_samples, callback=cb):
0125 |             t0 = time.time()
0126 |             while recording and time.time() - t0 < MAX_DURATION:
0127 |                 time.sleep(0.05)
0128 |     except sd.CallbackStop:
0129 |         pass
0130 |     except Exception:
0131 |         return ""
0132 | 
0133 |     if not data:
0134 |         return ""
0135 |     audio = np.concatenate(data, axis=0).flatten()
0136 |     return transcribe_array(audio, SAMPLE_RATE)
0137 | 
0138 | 
0139 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0140 |     text = listen_and_transcribe()
0141 |     if text:
0142 |         print(text)
0143 | 


================================================================================
Module: agents\browser_agent.py

Module Docstring:
browser_agent.py — DuckDuckGo search and webpage retrieval plugin (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, summarization,
reasoning, classification, decision making, intent detection, opinion
generation, or content interpretation. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Searches DuckDuckGo or fetches/crawls webpages.
    3. Extracts raw content and metadata.
    4. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

Dependencies (install once)::

    pip install ddgs requests beautifulsoup4 lxml

No API keys required.

CLI usage::

    python browser_agent.py request.json
    python browser_agent.py '{"action": "web_search", "parameters": {"query": "AI news"}}'

Classes:
  - BrowserAgentError
    Docstring: Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return....

Functions:
  - _get_session
    Docstring: Return a cached :class:`requests.Session` with a realistic UA....
  - _fetch_url
    Docstring: GET *url* with retry/backoff....
  - _make_soup
    Docstring: Parse HTML with lxml (fast) falling back to html.parser....
  - _extract_title
    Docstring: Return the page <title> text or empty string....
  - _extract_text
    Docstring: Return visible text from the page, stripping scripts/styles....
  - _extract_links
    Docstring: Return all <a> links with resolved absolute URLs....
  - _extract_images
    Docstring: Return all <img> sources with resolved absolute URLs....
  - _extract_metadata
    Docstring: Return standard page metadata from <meta> tags....
  - _fetch_and_parse
    Docstring: Fetch a URL and return a full page dict (url, title, text, html, links, images)....
  - _ddg_search
    Docstring: Run a DuckDuckGo text search and normalise the result keys....
  - _clamp_max_results
    Docstring: Parse and clamp a max_results parameter....
  - _action_web_search
  - _action_multi_search
  - _action_fetch_page
  - _action_fetch_multiple_pages
  - _action_extract_text
  - _action_extract_links
  - _action_extract_images
  - _action_get_page_metadata
  - _action_crawl_website
  - _action_check_url
  - _action_research_bundle
  - _action_get_raw_html
  - execute
    Docstring: Execute a browser/search action....
  - _cli_main
    Docstring: Handle command-line invocation: file arg, inline JSON arg, or piped stdin....

0066 | MAX_RETRIES: int = 3
0067 | RETRY_BACKOFF: float = 1.0
0068 | DEFAULT_MAX_RESULTS: int = 10
0069 | MAX_RESULTS_CAP: int = 50
0070 | DEFAULT_MAX_PAGES: int = 10
0071 | MAX_PAGES_CAP: int = 50
0072 | MAX_HTML_SIZE: int = 10 * 1024 * 1024  # 10 MB
0073 | 
0074 | USER_AGENT: str = (
0075 |     "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) "
0076 |     "AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) "
0077 |     "Chrome/125.0.0.0 Safari/537.36"
0078 | )
0079 | 
0080 | 
0081 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0082 | # Exceptions
0083 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0084 | class BrowserAgentError(Exception):
0085 |     """Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return."""
0086 | 
0087 | 
0088 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0089 | # HTTP layer (with retry/backoff)
0090 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0091 | _SESSION: Optional[requests.Session] = None
0092 | 
0093 | 
0094 | def _get_session() -> requests.Session:
0095 |     """Return a cached :class:`requests.Session` with a realistic UA."""
0096 |     global _SESSION
0097 |     if _SESSION is None:
0098 |         _SESSION = requests.Session()
0099 |         _SESSION.headers.update({"User-Agent": USER_AGENT})
0100 |     return _SESSION
0101 | 
0102 | 
0103 | def _fetch_url(url: str, *, timeout: int = REQUEST_TIMEOUT) -> requests.Response:
0104 |     """GET *url* with retry/backoff.
0105 | 
0106 |     Retries on network errors and HTTP 5xx. Client errors (4xx) are
0107 |     surfaced immediately.
0108 |     """
0109 |     session = _get_session()
0110 |     last_error: str = "unknown error"
0111 | 
0112 |     for attempt in range(MAX_RETRIES):
0113 |         try:
0114 |             resp = session.get(url, timeout=timeout, allow_redirects=True)
0115 |         except requests.RequestException as exc:
0116 |             last_error = f"network error ({exc})"
0117 |         else:
0118 |             if resp.status_code >= 500:
0119 |                 last_error = f"server error (HTTP {resp.status_code})"
0120 |             elif resp.status_code >= 400:
0121 |                 raise BrowserAgentError(
0122 |                     f"HTTP {resp.status_code} for {url}"
0123 |                 )
0124 |             else:
0125 |                 content_length = len(resp.content)
0126 |                 if content_length > MAX_HTML_SIZE:
0127 |                     raise BrowserAgentError(
0128 |                         f"Page too large ({content_length:,} bytes, limit {MAX_HTML_SIZE:,})"
0129 |                     )
0130 |                 return resp
0131 | 
0132 |         if attempt < MAX_RETRIES - 1:
0133 |             time.sleep(RETRY_BACKOFF * (2 ** attempt))
0134 | 
0135 |     raise BrowserAgentError(f"Failed after {MAX_RETRIES} attempts: {last_error}")
0136 | 
0137 | 
0138 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0139 | # HTML parsing helpers
0140 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0141 | def _make_soup(html: str) -> BeautifulSoup:
0142 |     """Parse HTML with lxml (fast) falling back to html.parser."""
0143 |     try:
0144 |         return BeautifulSoup(html, "lxml")
0145 |     except Exception:
0146 |         return BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")
0147 | 
0148 | 
0149 | def _extract_title(soup: BeautifulSoup) -> str:
0150 |     """Return the page <title> text or empty string."""
0151 |     tag = soup.find("title")
0152 |     return tag.get_text(strip=True) if tag else ""
0153 | 
0154 | 
0155 | def _extract_text(soup: BeautifulSoup) -> str:
0156 |     """Return visible text from the page, stripping scripts/styles."""
0157 |     for tag in soup(["script", "style", "noscript", "header", "footer", "nav"]):
0158 |         tag.decompose()
0159 |     return soup.get_text(separator="\n", strip=True)
0160 | 
0161 | 
0162 | def _extract_links(soup: BeautifulSoup, base_url: str) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
0163 |     """Return all <a> links with resolved absolute URLs."""
0164 |     links: list[dict[str, str]] = []
0165 |     seen: set[str] = set()
0166 |     for a in soup.find_all("a", href=True):
0167 |         href = urljoin(base_url, a["href"])
0168 |         if href in seen:
0169 |             continue
0170 |         seen.add(href)
0171 |         text = a.get_text(strip=True)
0172 |         links.append({"url": href, "text": text})
0173 |     return links
0174 | 
0175 | 
0176 | def _extract_images(soup: BeautifulSoup, base_url: str) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
0177 |     """Return all <img> sources with resolved absolute URLs."""
0178 |     images: list[dict[str, str]] = []
0179 |     seen: set[str] = set()
0180 |     for img in soup.find_all("img", src=True):
0181 |         src = urljoin(base_url, img["src"])
0182 |         if src in seen:
0183 |             continue
0184 |         seen.add(src)
0185 |         alt = img.get("alt", "")
0186 |         images.append({"url": src, "alt": alt})
0187 |     return images
0188 | 
0189 | 
0190 | def _extract_metadata(soup: BeautifulSoup, url: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0191 |     """Return standard page metadata from <meta> tags."""
0192 |     title = _extract_title(soup)
0193 | 
0194 |     description = ""
0195 |     desc_tag = soup.find("meta", attrs={"name": "description"})
0196 |     if desc_tag and desc_tag.get("content"):
0197 |         description = desc_tag["content"]
0198 |     if not description:
0199 |         og_desc = soup.find("meta", attrs={"property": "og:description"})
0200 |         if og_desc and og_desc.get("content"):
0201 |             description = og_desc["content"]
0202 | 
0203 |     keywords: list[str] = []
0204 |     kw_tag = soup.find("meta", attrs={"name": "keywords"})
0205 |     if kw_tag and kw_tag.get("content"):
0206 |         keywords = [k.strip() for k in kw_tag["content"].split(",") if k.strip()]
0207 | 
0208 |     canonical = ""
0209 |     canon_tag = soup.find("link", attrs={"rel": "canonical"})
0210 |     if canon_tag and canon_tag.get("href"):
0211 |         canonical = canon_tag["href"]
0212 | 
0213 |     return {
0214 |         "title": title,
0215 |         "description": description,
0216 |         "keywords": keywords,
0217 |         "canonical_url": canonical or url,
0218 |     }
0219 | 
0220 | 
0221 | def _fetch_and_parse(url: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0222 |     """Fetch a URL and return a full page dict (url, title, text, html, links, images)."""
0223 |     resp = _fetch_url(url)
0224 |     html = resp.text
0225 |     soup = _make_soup(html)
0226 |     return {
0227 |         "url": resp.url,
0228 |         "title": _extract_title(soup),
0229 |         "text": _extract_text(soup),
0230 |         "html": html,
0231 |         "links": _extract_links(soup, resp.url),
0232 |         "images": _extract_images(soup, resp.url),
0233 |     }
0234 | 
0235 | 
0236 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0237 | # DuckDuckGo search helper
0238 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0239 | def _ddg_search(query: str, max_results: int) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
0240 |     """Run a DuckDuckGo text search and normalise the result keys."""
0241 |     try:
0242 |         ddgs = DDGS()
0243 |         raw = ddgs.text(query, max_results=max_results, backend="html")
0244 |         if not raw:
0245 |             raw = ddgs.text(query, max_results=max_results, backend="lite")
0246 |     except Exception as exc:
0247 |         raise BrowserAgentError(f"DuckDuckGo search failed: {exc}")
0248 | 
0249 |     results: list[dict[str, str]] = []
0250 |     for item in raw:
0251 |         results.append({
0252 |             "title": item.get("title", ""),
0253 |             "url": item.get("href", ""),
0254 |             "snippet": item.get("body", ""),
0255 |         })
0256 |     return results
0257 | 
0258 | 
0259 | def _clamp_max_results(params: dict[str, Any], key: str = "max_results") -> int:
0260 |     """Parse and clamp a max_results parameter."""
0261 |     raw = params.get(key, DEFAULT_MAX_RESULTS)
0262 |     try:
0263 |         n = int(raw)
0264 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0265 |         raise BrowserAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be an integer")
0266 |     if n < 1:
0267 |         n = 1
0268 |     if n > MAX_RESULTS_CAP:
0269 |         n = MAX_RESULTS_CAP
0270 |     return n
0271 | 
0272 | 
0273 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0274 | # Action handlers
0275 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0276 | def _action_web_search(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0277 |     query = params.get("query", "")
0278 |     max_results = _clamp_max_results(params)
0279 |     results = _ddg_search(query, max_results)
0280 |     return {"count": len(results), "results": results}
0281 | 
0282 | 
0283 | def _action_multi_search(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0284 |     queries = params.get("queries")
0285 |     if not queries or not isinstance(queries, list):
0286 |         raise BrowserAgentError("Missing or invalid queries parameter (expected a list)")
0287 |     if not all(isinstance(q, str) and q.strip() for q in queries):
0288 |         raise BrowserAgentError("All queries must be non-empty strings")
0289 |     max_results = _clamp_max_results(params)
0290 | 
0291 |     results: dict[str, Any] = {}
0292 |     for query in queries:
0293 |         try:
0294 |             results[query] = _ddg_search(query.strip(), max_results)
0295 |         except BrowserAgentError as exc:
0296 |             results[query] = {"error": str(exc)}
0297 |     return {"results": results}
0298 | 
0299 | 
0300 | def _action_fetch_page(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0301 |     url = params.get("url", "")
0302 |     return _fetch_and_parse(url)
0303 | 
0304 | 
0305 | def _action_fetch_multiple_pages(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0306 |     urls = params.get("urls")
0307 |     if not urls or not isinstance(urls, list):
0308 |         raise BrowserAgentError("Missing or invalid urls parameter (expected a list)")
0309 |     if not all(isinstance(u, str) and u.strip() for u in urls):
0310 |         raise BrowserAgentError("All urls must be non-empty strings")
0311 | 
0312 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0313 |     for url in urls:
0314 |         try:
0315 |             page = _fetch_and_parse(url.strip())
0316 |             results.append({"status": "success", "url": url, "data": page})
0317 |         except (BrowserAgentError, Exception) as exc:
0318 |             results.append({"status": "error", "url": url, "message": str(exc)})
0319 |     return {"count": len(results), "results": results}
0320 | 
0321 | 
0322 | def _action_extract_text(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0323 |     url = params.get("url", "")
0324 |     resp = _fetch_url(url)
0325 |     soup = _make_soup(resp.text)
0326 |     return {"url": resp.url, "text": _extract_text(soup)}
0327 | 
0328 | 
0329 | def _action_extract_links(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0330 |     url = params.get("url", "")
0331 |     resp = _fetch_url(url)
0332 |     soup = _make_soup(resp.text)
0333 |     links = _extract_links(soup, resp.url)
0334 |     return {"url": resp.url, "count": len(links), "links": links}
0335 | 
0336 | 
0337 | def _action_extract_images(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0338 |     url = params.get("url", "")
0339 |     resp = _fetch_url(url)
0340 |     soup = _make_soup(resp.text)
0341 |     images = _extract_images(soup, resp.url)
0342 |     return {"url": resp.url, "count": len(images), "images": images}
0343 | 
0344 | 
0345 | def _action_get_page_metadata(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0346 |     url = params.get("url", "")
0347 |     resp = _fetch_url(url)
0348 |     soup = _make_soup(resp.text)
0349 |     return _extract_metadata(soup, resp.url)
0350 | 
0351 | 
0352 | def _action_crawl_website(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0353 |     start_url = params.get("url", "")
0354 |     max_pages_raw = params.get("max_pages", DEFAULT_MAX_PAGES)
0355 |     try:
0356 |         max_pages = int(max_pages_raw)
0357 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0358 |         raise BrowserAgentError("max_pages must be an integer")
0359 |     if max_pages < 1:
0360 |         max_pages = 1
0361 |     if max_pages > MAX_PAGES_CAP:
0362 |         max_pages = MAX_PAGES_CAP
0363 | 
0364 |     parsed_start = urlparse(start_url)
0365 |     domain = parsed_start.netloc
0366 | 
0367 |     visited: set[str] = set()
0368 |     queue: list[str] = [start_url]
0369 |     pages: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0370 | 
0371 |     while queue and len(pages) < max_pages:
0372 |         url = queue.pop(0)
0373 |         normalised = urlparse(url)._replace(fragment="").geturl()
0374 |         if normalised in visited:
0375 |             continue
0376 |         visited.add(normalised)
0377 | 
0378 |         try:
0379 |             resp = _fetch_url(url)
0380 |             soup = _make_soup(resp.text)
0381 |             text = _extract_text(soup)
0382 |             title = _extract_title(soup)
0383 |             pages.append({
0384 |                 "url": resp.url,
0385 |                 "title": title,
0386 |                 "text": text,
0387 |             })
0388 |             for a in soup.find_all("a", href=True):
0389 |                 link = urljoin(resp.url, a["href"])
0390 |                 link_parsed = urlparse(link)
0391 |                 link_clean = link_parsed._replace(fragment="").geturl()
0392 |                 if link_parsed.netloc == domain and link_clean not in visited:
0393 |                     queue.append(link_clean)
0394 |         except (BrowserAgentError, Exception):
0395 |             continue
0396 | 
0397 |     return {"domain": domain, "pages_crawled": len(pages), "pages": pages}
0398 | 
0399 | 
0400 | def _action_check_url(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0401 |     url = params.get("url", "")
0402 |     session = _get_session()
0403 |     try:
0404 |         resp = session.head(url, timeout=REQUEST_TIMEOUT, allow_redirects=True)
0405 |         return {
0406 |             "url": url,
0407 |             "final_url": resp.url,
0408 |             "exists": resp.status_code < 400,
0409 |             "status_code": resp.status_code,
0410 |         }
0411 |     except requests.RequestException as exc:
0412 |         return {
0413 |             "url": url,
0414 |             "exists": False,
0415 |             "status_code": None,
0416 |             "error": str(exc),
0417 |         }
0418 | 
0419 | 
0420 | def _action_research_bundle(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0421 |     queries = params.get("queries")
0422 |     if not queries or not isinstance(queries, list):
0423 |         raise BrowserAgentError("Missing or invalid queries parameter (expected a list)")
0424 |     if not all(isinstance(q, str) and q.strip() for q in queries):
0425 |         raise BrowserAgentError("All queries must be non-empty strings")
0426 | 
0427 |     max_per_query_raw = params.get("max_results_per_query", 5)
0428 |     try:
0429 |         max_per_query = int(max_per_query_raw)
0430 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0431 |         raise BrowserAgentError("max_results_per_query must be an integer")
0432 |     if max_per_query < 1:
0433 |         max_per_query = 1
0434 |     if max_per_query > MAX_RESULTS_CAP:
0435 |         max_per_query = MAX_RESULTS_CAP
0436 | 
0437 |     fetch_top = bool(params.get("fetch_top_pages", False))
0438 | 
0439 |     results: dict[str, Any] = {}
0440 |     for query in queries:
0441 |         q = query.strip()
0442 |         entry: dict[str, Any] = {}
0443 |         try:
0444 |             search_results = _ddg_search(q, max_per_query)
0445 |             entry["search_results"] = search_results
0446 |         except BrowserAgentError as exc:
0447 |             entry["search_results"] = []
0448 |             entry["search_error"] = str(exc)
0449 | 
0450 |         if fetch_top and entry.get("search_results"):
0451 |             top_url = entry["search_results"][0].get("url", "")
0452 |             if top_url:
0453 |                 try:
0454 |                     page = _fetch_and_parse(top_url)
0455 |                     entry["top_page"] = {
0456 |                         "url": page["url"],
0457 |                         "title": page["title"],
0458 |                         "text": page["text"],
0459 |                     }
0460 |                 except (BrowserAgentError, Exception) as exc:
0461 |                     entry["top_page"] = {"url": top_url, "error": str(exc)}
0462 | 
0463 |         results[q] = entry
0464 | 
0465 |     return {"results": results}
0466 | 
0467 | 
0468 | def _action_get_raw_html(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0469 |     url = params.get("url", "")
0470 |     resp = _fetch_url(url)
0471 |     return {"url": resp.url, "status_code": resp.status_code, "html": resp.text}

0481 |     "fetch_multiple_pages": ["urls"],

0492 | _ACTIONS: dict[str, Callable[[dict[str, Any]], dict[str, Any]]] = {
0493 |     "web_search": _action_web_search,
0494 |     "multi_search": _action_multi_search,
0495 |     "fetch_page": _action_fetch_page,
0496 |     "fetch_multiple_pages": _action_fetch_multiple_pages,

0507 | 
0508 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0509 | # Public entry point
0510 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0511 | def execute(request_json: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0512 |     """Execute a browser/search action.
0513 | 
0514 |     Args:
0515 |         request_json: A dict with ``"action"`` (str) and ``"parameters"`` (dict).
0516 | 
0517 |     Returns:
0518 |         A JSON-compatible dict with ``"status"`` (``"success"`` | ``"error"``),
0519 |         ``"action"``, and either ``"data"`` or ``"message"``.
0520 |     """
0521 |     if isinstance(request_json, str):
0522 |         request_json = request_json.lstrip("﻿")
0523 |         try:
0524 |             request_json = json.loads(request_json)
0525 |         except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0526 |             return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON: {exc}"}
0527 | 
0528 |     if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0529 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Request must be a JSON object"}
0530 | 
0531 |     action = request_json.get("action", "")
0532 |     if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0533 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Missing or invalid action field"}
0534 | 
0535 |     if action not in _ACTIONS:
0536 |         return {
0537 |             "status": "error",
0538 |             "action": action,
0539 |             "message": f"Unknown action: {action}. Available: {', '.join(sorted(_ACTIONS))}",
0540 |         }
0541 | 
0542 |     parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0543 |     if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0544 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": "parameters must be a JSON object"}
0545 | 
0546 |     required = _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, [])
0547 |     for key in required:
0548 |         value = parameters.get(key)
0549 |         if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
0550 |             return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Missing required parameter: {key}"}
0551 | 
0552 |     try:
0553 |         data = _ACTIONS[action](parameters)
0554 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, "data": data}
0555 |     except BrowserAgentError as exc:
0556 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": str(exc)}
0557 |     except Exception as exc:
0558 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Unexpected error: {exc}"}
0559 | 
0560 | 
0561 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0562 | # CLI entry point
0563 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0564 | def _cli_main() -> None:
0565 |     """Handle command-line invocation: file arg, inline JSON arg, or piped stdin."""
0566 |     raw: Optional[str] = None
0567 | 
0568 |     if len(sys.argv) > 1:
0569 |         arg = sys.argv[1]
0570 |         if os.path.isfile(arg):
0571 |             with open(arg, "rb") as fh:
0572 |                 raw = fh.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
0573 |         else:
0574 |             raw = arg
0575 |     elif not sys.stdin.isatty():
0576 |         raw = sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
0577 |     else:
0578 |         print(
0579 |             "Usage:\n"
0580 |             '  python browser_agent.py request.json\n'
0581 |             '  python browser_agent.py \'{"action":"web_search","parameters":{"query":"AI news"}}\'\n'
0582 |             '  echo \'{"action":"check_url","parameters":{"url":"https://example.com"}}\' '
0583 |             "| python browser_agent.py",
0584 |             file=sys.stderr,
0585 |         )
0586 |         sys.exit(2)
0587 | 
0588 |     raw = raw.strip().lstrip("﻿")
0589 |     try:
0590 |         request_data = json.loads(raw)
0591 |     except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0592 |         result = {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}"}
0593 |         print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
0594 |         sys.exit(1)
0595 | 
0596 |     result = execute(request_data)
0597 |     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
0598 |     sys.exit(0 if result.get("status") == "success" else 1)
0599 | 
0600 | 
0601 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0602 |     _cli_main()

================================================================================
Module: agents\file_agent.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
file_agent.py — File system and document access plugin (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, summarization,
classification, reasoning, decision making, intent detection, or content
interpretation. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Performs file system operations or reads documents.
    3. Extracts raw content and metadata.
    4. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

Dependencies (install once)::

    pip install PyPDF2 python-docx openpyxl python-pptx pandas

CLI usage::

    python file_agent.py request.json
    python file_agent.py '{"action": "list_directory", "parameters": {"path": "."}}'

Classes:
  - FileAgentError
    Docstring: Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return....

0001 | """file_agent.py — File system and document access plugin (TOOL ONLY).
0002 | 
0003 | This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, summarization,
0004 | classification, reasoning, decision making, intent detection, or content
0005 | interpretation. It only:
0006 | 
0007 |     1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
0008 |     2. Performs file system operations or reads documents.
0009 |     3. Extracts raw content and metadata.
0010 |     4. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.
0011 | 
0012 | All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
0013 | entry point is :func:`execute`.
0014 | 
0015 | Dependencies (install once)::
0016 | 
0017 |     pip install PyPDF2 python-docx openpyxl python-pptx pandas
0018 | 
0019 | CLI usage::
0020 | 
0021 |     python file_agent.py request.json
0022 |     python file_agent.py '{"action": "list_directory", "parameters": {"path": "."}}'
0023 | """
0024 |

0046 |     "type": "tool",
0047 |     "input_format": "json",
0048 |     "output_format": "json",
0049 |     "entrypoint": "execute",

0051 | }

0054 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0055 | # Supported extensions
0056 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0057 | TEXT_EXTENSIONS: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
0058 |     ".txt", ".md", ".csv", ".json", ".py", ".js", ".ts",
0059 |     ".html", ".css", ".xml", ".yaml", ".yml",
0060 | })
0061 |

0063 |     ".pdf", ".doc", ".docx", ".ppt", ".pptx", ".xls", ".xlsx",

0066 | ALL_SUPPORTED_EXTENSIONS: frozenset[str] = TEXT_EXTENSIONS | DOCUMENT_EXTENSIONS
0067 | 
0068 | DEFAULT_MAX_DEPTH: int = 5
0069 | DEFAULT_LIMIT: int = 20
0070 | MAX_TEXT_SIZE: int = 50 * 1024 * 1024  # 50 MB safety cap for text files
0071 | MAX_RECURSIVE_ENTRIES: int = 10_000

0074 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0075 | # Exceptions
0076 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0077 | class FileAgentError(Exception):
0078 |     """Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return.
0079 | 
0080 |     Covers parameter validation, missing files, permission errors, and
0081 |     corrupt documents. These map to a structured ``status: error`` response
0082 |     instead of crashing the tool.
0083 |     """

0086 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0087 | # Path helpers
0088 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0089 | def _resolve_path(raw: str) -> Path:
0090 |     """Resolve and validate a user-supplied path string.
0091 | 
0092 |     Raises:
0093 |         FileAgentError: On empty input.
0094 |     """
0095 |     if not raw or not raw.strip():
0096 |         raise FileAgentError("Path parameter is empty")
0097 |     return Path(raw).resolve()
0098 | 
0099 | 
0100 | def _require_file(path: Path) -> None:
0101 |     """Assert that *path* exists and is a file."""
0102 |     if not path.exists():
0103 |         raise FileAgentError(f"File not found: {path}")
0104 |     if not path.is_file():
0105 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Path is not a file: {path}")
0106 | 
0107 | 
0108 | def _require_directory(path: Path) -> None:
0109 |     """Assert that *path* exists and is a directory."""
0110 |     if not path.exists():
0111 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Directory not found: {path}")
0112 |     if not path.is_dir():
0113 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Path is not a directory: {path}")
0114 | 
0115 | 
0116 | def _iso_timestamp(epoch: float) -> str:
0117 |     """Convert an epoch timestamp to an ISO-8601 UTC string."""
0118 |     return datetime.fromtimestamp(epoch, tz=timezone.utc).isoformat()
0119 | 
0120 | 
0121 | def _file_meta(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
0122 |     """Return a standard metadata dict for a single file."""
0123 |     stat = path.stat()
0124 |     return {
0125 |         "name": path.name,
0126 |         "extension": path.suffix.lower(),
0127 |         "size_bytes": stat.st_size,
0128 |         "created_time": _iso_timestamp(stat.st_ctime),
0129 |         "modified_time": _iso_timestamp(stat.st_mtime),
0130 |         "absolute_path": str(path),
0131 |     }
0132 | 
0133 | 
0134 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0135 | # Directory listing helpers
0136 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0137 | def _list_entries(directory: Path) -> dict[str, list[dict[str, Any]]]:
0138 |     """List immediate children of *directory* split into folders and files."""
0139 |     folders: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0140 |     files: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0141 |     try:
0142 |         entries = sorted(directory.iterdir(), key=lambda p: p.name.lower())
0143 |     except PermissionError:
0144 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Permission denied: {directory}")
0145 | 
0146 |     for entry in entries:
0147 |         try:
0148 |             if entry.is_dir():
0149 |                 folders.append({"name": entry.name, "path": str(entry)})
0150 |             elif entry.is_file():
0151 |                 stat = entry.stat()
0152 |                 files.append({
0153 |                     "name": entry.name,
0154 |                     "extension": entry.suffix.lower(),
0155 |                     "size_bytes": stat.st_size,
0156 |                     "modified_time": _iso_timestamp(stat.st_mtime),
0157 |                     "path": str(entry),
0158 |                 })
0159 |         except (PermissionError, OSError):
0160 |             continue
0161 |     return {"folders": folders, "files": files}
0162 | 
0163 | 
0164 | def _walk_recursive(
0165 |     directory: Path, max_depth: int, _current_depth: int = 0
0166 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
0167 |     """Build a recursive directory tree up to *max_depth* levels."""
0168 |     node: dict[str, Any] = {
0169 |         "name": directory.name,
0170 |         "path": str(directory),
0171 |         "folders": [],
0172 |         "files": [],
0173 |     }
0174 |     if _current_depth >= max_depth:
0175 |         return node
0176 | 
0177 |     try:
0178 |         entries = sorted(directory.iterdir(), key=lambda p: p.name.lower())
0179 |     except PermissionError:
0180 |         node["error"] = "permission denied"
0181 |         return node
0182 | 
0183 |     for entry in entries:
0184 |         try:
0185 |             if entry.is_dir():
0186 |                 child = _walk_recursive(entry, max_depth, _current_depth + 1)
0187 |                 node["folders"].append(child)
0188 |             elif entry.is_file():
0189 |                 stat = entry.stat()
0190 |                 node["files"].append({
0191 |                     "name": entry.name,
0192 |                     "extension": entry.suffix.lower(),
0193 |                     "size_bytes": stat.st_size,
0194 |                     "modified_time": _iso_timestamp(stat.st_mtime),
0195 |                     "path": str(entry),
0196 |                 })
0197 |         except (PermissionError, OSError):
0198 |             continue
0199 |     return node
0200 | 
0201 | 
0202 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0203 | # Document readers
0204 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0205 | def _read_text(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
0206 |     """Read a text-based file and return its content."""
0207 |     stat = path.stat()
0208 |     if stat.st_size > MAX_TEXT_SIZE:
0209 |         raise FileAgentError(
0210 |             f"File too large ({stat.st_size:,} bytes, limit {MAX_TEXT_SIZE:,})"
0211 |         )
0212 |     try:
0213 |         content = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
0214 |     except UnicodeDecodeError:
0215 |         try:
0216 |             content = path.read_text(encoding="latin-1")
0217 |         except Exception as exc:
0218 |             raise FileAgentError(f"Unable to decode file: {exc}")
0219 |     except PermissionError:
0220 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Permission denied: {path}")
0221 |     return {"content": content}
0222 | 
0223 | 
0224 | def _read_pdf(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
0225 |     """Read a PDF and return per-page text."""
0226 |     try:
0227 |         from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
0228 |     except ImportError:
0229 |         raise FileAgentError(
0230 |             "PyPDF2 is not installed. Run: pip install PyPDF2"
0231 |         )
0232 |     try:
0233 |         reader = PdfReader(str(path))
0234 |     except Exception as exc:
0235 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Failed to open PDF: {exc}")
0236 | 
0237 |     pages: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0238 |     for i, page in enumerate(reader.pages, start=1):
0239 |         try:
0240 |             text = page.extract_text() or ""
0241 |         except Exception:
0242 |             text = ""
0243 |         pages.append({"page": i, "text": text})
0244 |     return {"page_count": len(pages), "pages": pages}
0245 | 
0246 | 
0247 | def _read_excel(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
0248 |     """Read an Excel workbook and return per-sheet rows."""
0249 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0250 |     try:
0251 |         import pandas as pd
0252 |     except ImportError:
0253 |         raise FileAgentError(
0254 |             "pandas is not installed. Run: pip install pandas"
0255 |         )
0256 | 
0257 |     engine: Optional[str] = None
0258 |     if ext == ".xlsx":
0259 |         try:
0260 |             import openpyxl  # noqa: F401
0261 |             engine = "openpyxl"
0262 |         except ImportError:
0263 |             raise FileAgentError(
0264 |                 "openpyxl is not installed. Run: pip install openpyxl"
0265 |             )
0266 |     elif ext == ".xls":
0267 |         try:
0268 |             import xlrd  # noqa: F401
0269 |             engine = "xlrd"
0270 |         except ImportError:
0271 |             raise FileAgentError(
0272 |                 "xlrd is not installed. Run: pip install xlrd"
0273 |             )
0274 |     else:
0275 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Unsupported Excel extension: {ext}")
0276 | 
0277 |     try:
0278 |         sheets_dict = pd.read_excel(str(path), sheet_name=None, engine=engine)
0279 |     except Exception as exc:
0280 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Failed to read Excel file: {exc}")
0281 | 
0282 |     sheets: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0283 |     for sheet_name, df in sheets_dict.items():
0284 |         df = df.fillna("")
0285 |         rows = df.values.tolist()
0286 |         columns = df.columns.tolist()
0287 |         sheets.append({
0288 |             "sheet_name": str(sheet_name),
0289 |             "columns": [str(c) for c in columns],
0290 |             "row_count": len(rows),
0291 |             "rows": rows,
0292 |         })
0293 |     return {"sheet_count": len(sheets), "sheets": sheets}
0294 | 
0295 | 
0296 | def _read_word(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
0297 |     """Read a Word document and return its paragraphs."""
0298 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0299 |     if ext == ".doc":
0300 |         raise FileAgentError(
0301 |             "Legacy .doc format is not supported. Convert to .docx first."
0302 |         )
0303 |     try:
0304 |         from docx import Document
0305 |     except ImportError:
0306 |         raise FileAgentError(
0307 |             "python-docx is not installed. Run: pip install python-docx"
0308 |         )
0309 |     try:
0310 |         doc = Document(str(path))
0311 |     except Exception as exc:
0312 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Failed to open Word document: {exc}")
0313 | 
0314 |     paragraphs: list[str] = [p.text for p in doc.paragraphs]
0315 |     return {"paragraph_count": len(paragraphs), "paragraphs": paragraphs}
0316 | 
0317 | 
0318 | def _read_powerpoint(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
0319 |     """Read a PowerPoint presentation and return per-slide text."""
0320 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0321 |     if ext == ".ppt":
0322 |         raise FileAgentError(
0323 |             "Legacy .ppt format is not supported. Convert to .pptx first."
0324 |         )
0325 |     try:
0326 |         from pptx import Presentation
0327 |     except ImportError:
0328 |         raise FileAgentError(
0329 |             "python-pptx is not installed. Run: pip install python-pptx"
0330 |         )
0331 |     try:
0332 |         prs = Presentation(str(path))
0333 |     except Exception as exc:
0334 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Failed to open PowerPoint file: {exc}")
0335 | 
0336 |     slides: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0337 |     for i, slide in enumerate(prs.slides, start=1):
0338 |         texts: list[str] = []
0339 |         for shape in slide.shapes:
0340 |             if shape.has_text_frame:
0341 |                 for paragraph in shape.text_frame.paragraphs:
0342 |                     text = paragraph.text.strip()
0343 |                     if text:
0344 |                         texts.append(text)
0345 |         slides.append({"slide_number": i, "text": "\n".join(texts)})
0346 |     return {"slide_count": len(slides), "slides": slides}
0347 | 
0348 | 
0349 | def _read_any_file(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
0350 |     """Read a file based on its extension, returning structured content."""
0351 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0352 |     if ext in TEXT_EXTENSIONS:
0353 |         return _read_text(path)
0354 |     if ext == ".pdf":
0355 |         return _read_pdf(path)
0356 |     if ext in (".xlsx", ".xls"):
0357 |         return _read_excel(path)
0358 |     if ext in (".docx", ".doc"):
0359 |         return _read_word(path)
0360 |     if ext in (".pptx", ".ppt"):
0361 |         return _read_powerpoint(path)
0362 |     raise FileAgentError(f"Unsupported file type: {ext}")
0363 |

0369 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0370 |     _require_directory(path)
0371 |     return _list_entries(path)

0374 | def _action_list_directory_recursive(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0375 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0376 |     _require_directory(path)
0377 |     max_depth = int(params.get("max_depth", DEFAULT_MAX_DEPTH))
0378 |     if max_depth < 1:
0379 |         raise FileAgentError("max_depth must be at least 1")
0380 |     return _walk_recursive(path, max_depth)

0383 | def _action_search_files(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0384 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0385 |     _require_directory(path)
0386 |     pattern = params.get("pattern", "")
0387 |     if not pattern or not pattern.strip():
0388 |         raise FileAgentError("Missing pattern parameter")
0389 | 
0390 |     matches: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0391 |     count = 0
0392 |     for root, _dirs, files in os.walk(str(path)):
0393 |         for name in files:
0394 |             if fnmatch.fnmatch(name.lower(), pattern.lower()):
0395 |                 fp = Path(root) / name
0396 |                 try:
0397 |                     stat = fp.stat()
0398 |                     matches.append({
0399 |                         "name": name,
0400 |                         "extension": fp.suffix.lower(),
0401 |                         "size_bytes": stat.st_size,
0402 |                         "modified_time": _iso_timestamp(stat.st_mtime),
0403 |                         "path": str(fp),
0404 |                     })
0405 |                 except (PermissionError, OSError):
0406 |                     continue
0407 |                 count += 1
0408 |                 if count >= MAX_RECURSIVE_ENTRIES:
0409 |                     break
0410 |         if count >= MAX_RECURSIVE_ENTRIES:
0411 |             break
0412 |     return {"count": len(matches), "matches": matches}
0413 |

0415 | def _action_get_file_info(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0416 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0417 |     _require_file(path)
0418 |     return _file_meta(path)

0421 | def _action_read_text_file(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0422 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0423 |     _require_file(path)
0424 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0425 |     if ext not in TEXT_EXTENSIONS:
0426 |         raise FileAgentError(
0427 |             f"Unsupported text file type: {ext}. "
0428 |             f"Supported: {', '.join(sorted(TEXT_EXTENSIONS))}"
0429 |         )
0430 |     return _read_text(path)
0431 |

0433 | def _action_read_pdf(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0434 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0435 |     _require_file(path)
0436 |     if path.suffix.lower() != ".pdf":
0437 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Not a PDF file: {path.suffix}")
0438 |     return _read_pdf(path)

0441 | def _action_read_excel(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0442 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0443 |     _require_file(path)
0444 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0445 |     if ext not in (".xlsx", ".xls"):
0446 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Not an Excel file: {ext}")
0447 |     return _read_excel(path)

0450 | def _action_read_word(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0451 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0452 |     _require_file(path)
0453 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0454 |     if ext not in (".docx", ".doc"):
0455 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Not a Word document: {ext}")
0456 |     return _read_word(path)

0459 | def _action_read_powerpoint(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0460 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0461 |     _require_file(path)
0462 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0463 |     if ext not in (".pptx", ".ppt"):
0464 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Not a PowerPoint file: {ext}")
0465 |     return _read_powerpoint(path)

0468 | def _action_read_multiple_files(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0469 |     paths = params.get("paths")
0470 |     if not paths or not isinstance(paths, list):
0471 |         raise FileAgentError("Missing or invalid paths parameter (expected a list)")
0472 |     if not all(isinstance(p, str) and p.strip() for p in paths):
0473 |         raise FileAgentError("All items in paths must be non-empty strings")
0474 | 
0475 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0476 |     for raw in paths:
0477 |         try:
0478 |             path = _resolve_path(raw)
0479 |             _require_file(path)
0480 |             content = _read_any_file(path)
0481 |             results.append({
0482 |                 "status": "success",
0483 |                 "path": str(path),
0484 |                 "name": path.name,
0485 |                 "extension": path.suffix.lower(),
0486 |                 "data": content,
0487 |             })
0488 |         except (FileAgentError, Exception) as exc:
0489 |             results.append({
0490 |                 "status": "error",
0491 |                 "path": raw,
0492 |                 "message": str(exc),
0493 |             })
0494 |     return {"count": len(results), "results": results}
0495 |
