0497 | def _action_get_folder_tree(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0498 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0499 |     _require_directory(path)
0500 |     max_depth = int(params.get("max_depth", DEFAULT_MAX_DEPTH))
0501 |     if max_depth < 1:
0502 |         raise FileAgentError("max_depth must be at least 1")
0503 |     return _walk_recursive(path, max_depth)

0506 | def _action_file_exists(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0507 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0508 |     exists = path.is_file()
0509 |     result: dict[str, Any] = {"exists": exists, "path": str(path)}
0510 |     if exists:
0511 |         result["name"] = path.name
0512 |         result["extension"] = path.suffix.lower()
0513 |         result["size_bytes"] = path.stat().st_size
0514 |     return result
0515 | 
0516 | 
0517 | def _action_directory_exists(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0518 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0519 |     exists = path.is_dir()
0520 |     return {"exists": exists, "path": str(path)}
0521 | 
0522 | 
0523 | def _action_get_supported_files(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0524 |     return {
0525 |         "text_extensions": sorted(TEXT_EXTENSIONS),
0526 |         "document_extensions": sorted(DOCUMENT_EXTENSIONS),
0527 |         "all_extensions": sorted(ALL_SUPPORTED_EXTENSIONS),
0528 |     }

0531 | def _action_get_recent_files(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0532 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0533 |     _require_directory(path)
0534 |     limit = int(params.get("limit", DEFAULT_LIMIT))
0535 |     if limit < 1:
0536 |         raise FileAgentError("limit must be at least 1")
0537 | 
0538 |     all_files: list[tuple[float, Path]] = []
0539 |     count = 0
0540 |     for root, _dirs, files in os.walk(str(path)):
0541 |         for name in files:
0542 |             fp = Path(root) / name
0543 |             try:
0544 |                 mtime = fp.stat().st_mtime
0545 |                 all_files.append((mtime, fp))
0546 |             except (PermissionError, OSError):
0547 |                 continue
0548 |             count += 1
0549 |             if count >= MAX_RECURSIVE_ENTRIES:
0550 |                 break
0551 |         if count >= MAX_RECURSIVE_ENTRIES:
0552 |             break
0553 | 
0554 |     all_files.sort(key=lambda t: t[0], reverse=True)
0555 |     recent = all_files[:limit]
0556 | 
0557 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0558 |     for mtime, fp in recent:
0559 |         try:
0560 |             stat = fp.stat()
0561 |             results.append({
0562 |                 "name": fp.name,
0563 |                 "extension": fp.suffix.lower(),
0564 |                 "size_bytes": stat.st_size,
0565 |                 "modified_time": _iso_timestamp(stat.st_mtime),
0566 |                 "path": str(fp),
0567 |             })
0568 |         except (PermissionError, OSError):
0569 |             continue
0570 |     return {"count": len(results), "files": results}
0571 | 
0572 | 
0573 | def _action_read_folder_contents(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0574 |     path = _resolve_path(params.get("path", ""))
0575 |     _require_directory(path)
0576 |     limit = int(params.get("limit", 50))
0577 | 
0578 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0579 |     try:
0580 |         entries = sorted(path.iterdir(), key=lambda p: p.name.lower())
0581 |     except PermissionError:
0582 |         raise FileAgentError(f"Permission denied: {path}")
0583 | 
0584 |     for entry in entries:
0585 |         if not entry.is_file():
0586 |             continue
0587 |         ext = entry.suffix.lower()
0588 |         if ext not in ALL_SUPPORTED_EXTENSIONS:
0589 |             continue
0590 |         try:
0591 |             content = _read_any_file(entry)
0592 |             results.append({
0593 |                 "status": "success",
0594 |                 "path": str(entry),
0595 |                 "name": entry.name,
0596 |                 "extension": ext,
0597 |                 "data": content,
0598 |             })
0599 |         except (FileAgentError, Exception) as exc:
0600 |             results.append({
0601 |                 "status": "error",
0602 |                 "path": str(entry),
0603 |                 "name": entry.name,
0604 |                 "message": str(exc),
0605 |             })
0606 |         if len(results) >= limit:
0607 |             break
0608 |     return {"count": len(results), "results": results}

0656 | def execute(request_json: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0657 |     """Execute a file system or document-reading action.
0658 | 
0659 |     Args:
0660 |         request_json: A dict with ``"action"`` (str) and ``"parameters"`` (dict).
0661 | 
0662 |     Returns:
0663 |         A JSON-compatible dict with ``"status"`` (``"success"`` | ``"error"``),
0664 |         ``"action"``, and either ``"data"`` or ``"message"``.
0665 |     """
0666 |     if isinstance(request_json, str):
0667 |         request_json = request_json.lstrip("﻿")
0668 |         try:
0669 |             request_json = json.loads(request_json)
0670 |         except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0671 |             return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON: {exc}"}
0672 | 
0673 |     if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0674 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Request must be a JSON object"}
0675 | 
0676 |     action = request_json.get("action", "")
0677 |     if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0678 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Missing or invalid action field"}
0679 | 
0680 |     if action not in _ACTIONS:
0681 |         return {
0682 |             "status": "error",
0683 |             "action": action,
0684 |             "message": f"Unknown action: {action}. Available: {', '.join(sorted(_ACTIONS))}",
0685 |         }
0686 | 
0687 |     parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0688 |     if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0689 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": "parameters must be a JSON object"}
0690 | 
0691 |     required = _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, [])
0692 |     for key in required:
0693 |         value = parameters.get(key)
0694 |         if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
0695 |             return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Missing required parameter: {key}"}
0696 | 
0697 |     try:
0698 |         data = _ACTIONS[action](parameters)
0699 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, "data": data}
0700 |     except FileAgentError as exc:
0701 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": str(exc)}
0702 |     except PermissionError as exc:
0703 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Permission denied: {exc}"}
0704 |     except Exception as exc:
0705 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Unexpected error: {exc}"}

================================================================================
Module: agents\gmail_agent.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
gmail_agent.py — Gmail retrieval and search plugin (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, reasoning,
summarization, classification, intent detection, or decision making. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Performs read-only Gmail API operations.
    3. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

Dependencies (install once)::

    pip install google-api-python-client google-auth google-auth-oauthlib

Authentication:
    * Expects an OAuth *installed app* ``credentials.json`` in the working dir.
    * On first run a browser window opens for consent and ``token.json`` is
      written. Subsequent runs reuse ``token.json`` and refresh it silently.

CLI usage (handy for the Brain Agent to call as a subprocess)::

    python gmail_agent.py '{"action": "get_latest_emails", "parameters": {"limit": 5}}'
    echo '{"action": "count_emails", "parameters": {"query": "is:unread"}}' | python gmail_agent.py

  - GmailAgentError
    Docstring: Raised for request-validation problems (bad/missing parameters)....

0101 | def _save_token(creds: Credentials) -> None:
0102 |     """Persist OAuth credentials to :data:`TOKEN_FILE` as JSON."""
0103 |     with open(TOKEN_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
0104 |         handle.write(creds.to_json())
0105 | 
0106 | 
0107 | def _get_credentials() -> Credentials:
0108 |     """Load, refresh, or interactively obtain OAuth2 credentials.
0109 | 
0110 |     Order of operations:
0111 |         1. Reuse ``token.json`` if present and valid.
0112 |         2. Silently refresh it if expired but a refresh token exists.
0113 |         3. Otherwise run the installed-app consent flow and store a new token.
0114 | 
0115 |     Returns:
0116 |         Valid :class:`google.oauth2.credentials.Credentials`.
0117 | 
0118 |     Raises:
0119 |         FileNotFoundError: ``credentials.json`` is missing when a fresh
0120 |             interactive login is required.
0121 |         RefreshError / GoogleAuthError: The OAuth flow itself failed.
0122 |     """
0123 |     creds: Optional[Credentials] = None
0124 | 
0125 |     if os.path.exists(TOKEN_FILE):
0126 |         try:
0127 |             creds = Credentials.from_authorized_user_file(TOKEN_FILE, SCOPES)
0128 |         except (ValueError, json.JSONDecodeError):
0129 |             # Corrupt/incompatible token file — discard and re-authenticate.
0130 |             creds = None
0131 | 
0132 |     if creds and creds.valid:
0133 |         return creds
0134 | 
0135 |     if creds and creds.expired and creds.refresh_token:
0136 |         try:
0137 |             creds.refresh(Request())
0138 |             _save_token(creds)
0139 |             return creds
0140 |         except RefreshError:
0141 |             # Refresh token revoked/expired — fall through to full re-auth.
0142 |             creds = None
0143 | 
0144 |     if not os.path.exists(CREDENTIALS_FILE):
0145 |         raise FileNotFoundError(
0146 |             f"OAuth client file not found: {CREDENTIALS_FILE}"
0147 |         )
0148 | 
0149 |     flow = InstalledAppFlow.from_client_secrets_file(CREDENTIALS_FILE, SCOPES)
0150 |     creds = flow.run_local_server(port=0)
0151 |     _save_token(creds)
0152 |     return creds
0153 |

0200 | def _to_gmail_date(date_str: str, add_day: bool = False) -> str:
0201 |     """Convert ``YYYY-MM-DD`` to Gmail's ``YYYY/MM/DD`` query format.
0202 | 
0203 |     Args:
0204 |         date_str: Date in ISO ``YYYY-MM-DD`` form.
0205 |         add_day: If ``True``, add one day. Used to make ``before:`` ranges
0206 |             inclusive of the end date (Gmail's ``before:`` is exclusive).
0207 | 
0208 |     Raises:
0209 |         GmailAgentError: ``date_str`` is not a valid ``YYYY-MM-DD`` date.
0210 |     """
0211 |     try:
0212 |         parsed = datetime.strptime(date_str, "%Y-%m-%d")
0213 |     except (ValueError, TypeError):
0214 |         raise GmailAgentError(
0215 |             f"Invalid date '{date_str}', expected format YYYY-MM-DD"
0216 |         )
0217 |     if add_day:
0218 |         parsed += timedelta(days=1)
0219 |     return parsed.strftime("%Y/%m/%d")

0225 | def _get_header(headers: list[dict[str, str]], name: str) -> str:
0226 |     """Return the value of header ``name`` (case-insensitive), or ``""``."""
0227 |     target = name.lower()

0234 | def _decode_base64url(data: str) -> str:
0235 |     """Decode a Gmail base64url body part to a UTF-8 string."""
0236 |     if not data:
0237 |         return ""
0238 |     decoded = base64.urlsafe_b64decode(data.encode("utf-8"))
0239 |     return decoded.decode("utf-8", errors="replace")

0242 | def _find_part_body(payload: dict[str, Any], mime_type: str) -> str:
0243 |     """Recursively find the first body part matching ``mime_type``."""
0244 |     if payload.get("mimeType") == mime_type:
0245 |         data = payload.get("body", {}).get("data")
0246 |         if data:
0247 |             return _decode_base64url(data)
0248 |     for part in payload.get("parts", []) or []:
0249 |         found = _find_part_body(part, mime_type)
0250 |         if found:
0251 |             return found
0252 |     return ""

0255 | def _extract_body(payload: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
0256 |     """Extract the message body, preferring ``text/plain`` over ``text/html``."""
0257 |     plain = _find_part_body(payload, "text/plain")
0258 |     if plain:
0259 |         return plain
0260 |     return _find_part_body(payload, "text/html")

0263 | def _extract_attachments(payload: dict[str, Any]) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0264 |     """Collect attachment metadata (filename, mime type, id, size)."""
0265 |     attachments: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0266 | 
0267 |     def walk(part: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
0268 |         filename = part.get("filename")
0269 |         body = part.get("body", {})
0270 |         if filename:
0271 |             attachments.append(
0272 |                 {
0273 |                     "filename": filename,
0274 |                     "mime_type": part.get("mimeType", ""),
0275 |                     "attachment_id": body.get("attachmentId", ""),
0276 |                     "size": body.get("size", 0),
0277 |                 }
0278 |             )
0279 |         for child in part.get("parts", []) or []:
0280 |             walk(child)
0281 | 
0282 |     walk(payload)
0283 |     return attachments

0293 |     Args:
0294 |         message: Raw message resource from the Gmail API.
0295 |         include_body: Include the decoded ``body`` field (needs full format).
0296 |         include_attachments: Include an ``attachments`` list (needs full format).
0297 |     """
0298 |     payload = message.get("payload", {}) or {}
0299 |     headers = payload.get("headers", []) or []
0300 | 
0301 |     email: dict[str, Any] = {
0302 |         "id": message.get("id", ""),
0303 |         "thread_id": message.get("threadId", ""),
0304 |         "from": _get_header(headers, "From"),
0305 |         "to": _get_header(headers, "To"),
0306 |         "subject": _get_header(headers, "Subject"),
0307 |         "date": _get_header(headers, "Date"),
0308 |         "snippet": message.get("snippet", ""),
0309 |         "label_ids": message.get("labelIds", []) or [],
0310 |     }
0311 |     if include_body:
0312 |         email["body"] = _extract_body(payload)
0313 |     if include_attachments:
0314 |         email["attachments"] = _extract_attachments(payload)
0315 |     return email
0316 | 
0317 | 
0318 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0319 | # Gmail API access helpers
0320 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0321 | def _list_message_ids(
0322 |     service: Any,
0323 |     query: Optional[str] = None,
0324 |     label_ids: Optional[list[str]] = None,
0325 |     limit: Optional[int] = None,
0326 | ) -> list[str]:
0327 |     """List message IDs matching a query/labels, honoring an optional limit.
0328 | 
0329 |     When ``limit`` is ``None`` every matching message is paginated (used for an
0330 |     accurate ``count_emails``); otherwise pagination stops once ``limit`` IDs
0331 |     are collected. Results preserve Gmail's newest-first ordering.
0332 |     """
0333 |     ids: list[str] = []
0334 |     page_token: Optional[str] = None
0335 | 
0336 |     while True:
0337 |         page_size = GMAIL_PAGE_SIZE
0338 |         if limit is not None:
0339 |             remaining = limit - len(ids)
0340 |             if remaining <= 0:
0341 |                 break
0342 |             page_size = min(GMAIL_PAGE_SIZE, remaining)
0343 | 
0344 |         response = (
0345 |             service.users()
0346 |             .messages()
0347 |             .list(
0348 |                 userId=USER_ID,
0349 |                 q=query or "",
0350 |                 labelIds=label_ids or [],
0351 |                 maxResults=page_size,
0352 |                 pageToken=page_token,
0353 |             )
0354 |             .execute()
0355 |         )
0356 | 
0357 |         ids.extend(item["id"] for item in response.get("messages", []))
0358 |         page_token = response.get("nextPageToken")
0359 |         if not page_token:
0360 |             break
0361 |         if limit is not None and len(ids) >= limit:
0362 |             break
0363 | 
0364 |     return ids
0365 | 
0366 | 
0367 | def _get_message(service: Any, message_id: str, full: bool = False) -> dict[str, Any]:
0368 |     """Fetch a single message in ``metadata`` (default) or ``full`` format."""
0369 |     if full:
0370 |         return (
0371 |             service.users()
0372 |             .messages()
0373 |             .get(userId=USER_ID, id=message_id, format="full")
0374 |             .execute()
0375 |         )
0376 |     return (
0377 |         service.users()
0378 |         .messages()
0379 |         .get(
0380 |             userId=USER_ID,
0381 |             id=message_id,
0382 |             format="metadata",
0383 |             metadataHeaders=METADATA_HEADERS,
0384 |         )
0385 |         .execute()
0386 |     )

0389 | def _fetch_emails(
0390 |     service: Any,
0391 |     message_ids: list[str],
0392 |     include_body: bool = False,
0393 |     include_attachments: bool = False,
0394 | ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0395 |     """Fetch and parse a list of message IDs into standard email dicts."""
0396 |     need_full = include_body or include_attachments
0397 |     emails: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0398 |     for message_id in message_ids:
0399 |         raw = _get_message(service, message_id, full=need_full)
0400 |         emails.append(_parse_message(raw, include_body, include_attachments))
0401 |     return emails

0531 | # Required parameters per action, validated *before* authentication so that a
0532 | # malformed request fails fast without triggering an OAuth/network round-trip.
0533 | # Handlers also re-check via ``_require`` so they remain safe if called directly.
0534 | _REQUIRED_PARAMS: dict[str, list[str]] = {
0535 |     "search_sender": ["sender"],
0536 |     "search_subject": ["subject"],
0537 |     "search_date_range": ["start_date", "end_date"],
0538 |     "search_gmail_query": ["query"],
0539 |     "get_email_by_id": ["message_id"],
0540 |     "count_emails": ["query"],
0541 | }
0542 | 
0543 | 
0544 | # Action registry: maps an action name to its handler. The handler signature is
0545 | # ``(service, parameters) -> list[dict] | int``.
0546 | _ACTIONS: dict[str, Callable[[Any, dict[str, Any]], Any]] = {
0547 |     "get_latest_emails": _action_get_latest_emails,
0548 |     "get_unread_emails": _action_get_unread_emails,
0549 |     "search_sender": _action_search_sender,

0556 |     "get_starred_emails": _action_get_starred_emails,
0557 |     "get_sent_emails": _action_get_sent_emails,

0563 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0564 | # Response builders
0565 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0566 | def _error(action: Optional[str], message: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0567 |     """Build a structured error response."""
0568 |     return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": message}
0569 | 
0570 | 
0571 | def _success(action: str, result: Any) -> dict[str, Any]:
0572 |     """Build a structured success response from a handler result."""
0573 |     if isinstance(result, int):  # count_emails
0574 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, "count": result, "data": []}
0575 |     return {
0576 |         "status": "success",
0577 |         "action": action,
0578 |         "count": len(result),
0579 |         "data": result,
0580 |     }
0581 | 
0582 | 
0583 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0584 | # Public interface
0585 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0586 | def execute(request_json: dict) -> dict:
0587 |     """Single public entry point — route a JSON request to a Gmail operation.
0588 | 
0589 |     The function validates input, dispatches to the matching read-only handler,
0590 |     and always returns a JSON-compatible ``dict``. It never raises; every error
0591 |     is reported as ``{"status": "error", ...}``.
0592 | 
0593 |     Args:
0594 |         request_json: A request dict (a JSON string is also accepted and parsed)
0595 |             of the form ``{"action": <str>, "parameters": <dict>}``.
0596 | 
0597 |     Returns:
0598 |         On success::
0599 | 
0600 |             {"status": "success", "action": <str>, "count": <int>, "data": [...]}
0601 | 
0602 |         On failure::
0603 | 
0604 |             {"status": "error", "action": <str|None>, "message": <str>}
0605 |     """
0606 |     action: Optional[str] = None
0607 |     try:
0608 |         # Accept a raw JSON string for convenience, though dict is the contract.
0609 |         # ``lstrip`` drops a leading BOM that some shells (PowerShell) prepend.
0610 |         if isinstance(request_json, str):
0611 |             try:
0612 |                 request_json = json.loads(request_json.lstrip("\ufeff"))
0613 |             except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0614 |                 return _error(None, f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}")
0615 | 
0616 |         if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0617 |             return _error(None, "Request must be a JSON object (dict)")
0618 | 
0619 |         action = request_json.get("action")
0620 |         if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0621 |             return _error(action, "Missing or invalid 'action' field")
0622 | 
0623 |         handler = _ACTIONS.get(action)
0624 |         if handler is None:
0625 |             return _error(action, "Unsupported action")
0626 | 
0627 |         parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0628 |         if parameters is None:
0629 |             parameters = {}
0630 |         if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0631 |             return _error(action, "'parameters' must be a JSON object")
0632 | 
0633 |         # Validate required parameters before authenticating (router step 3).
0634 |         for required_key in _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, []):
0635 |             _require(parameters, required_key)
0636 | 
0637 |         service = _get_service()
0638 |         result = handler(service, parameters)
0639 |         return _success(action, result)
0640 | 
0641 |     except GmailAgentError as exc:
0642 |         return _error(action, str(exc))
0643 |     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
0644 |         return _error(action, f"Authentication failed: {exc}")
0645 |     except (RefreshError, GoogleAuthError) as exc:
0646 |         return _error(action, f"Authentication failed: {exc}")
0647 |     except HttpError as exc:
0648 |         return _error(action, f"Gmail API error: {exc}")
0649 |     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - tool must never crash the Brain.
0650 |         return _error(action, f"Unexpected error: {exc}")
0651 | 
0652 | 
0653 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0654 | # CLI shim — accept a JSON request from a file, an argument, or stdin.
0655 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0656 | def _read_stdin() -> str:
0657 |     """Read stdin as bytes and decode with ``utf-8-sig`` to strip any BOM.
0658 | 
0659 |     PowerShell prepends a UTF-8 BOM when piping to a native process, which
0660 |     would otherwise make the JSON unparseable; ``utf-8-sig`` removes it.
0661 |     """
0662 |     return sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig", errors="replace")
0663 | 
0664 | 
0665 | def _print_usage() -> None:
0666 |     """Print CLI usage to stderr (shown when run on a TTY with no input)."""
0667 |     sys.stderr.write(
0668 |         "gmail_agent - Gmail retrieval/search tool (JSON in, JSON out)\n\n"
0669 |         "Provide a JSON request one of these ways:\n\n"
0670 |         "  1) From a file (most reliable on Windows/PowerShell):\n"
0671 |         "       python gmail_agent.py request.json\n\n"
0672 |         "  2) Piped via stdin:\n"
0673 |         "       '{\"action\":\"get_unread_emails\",\"parameters\":{\"limit\":5}}'"
0674 |         " | python gmail_agent.py\n\n"
0675 |         "  3) As one argument with escaped quotes (PowerShell):\n"
0676 |         "       python gmail_agent.py '{\\\"action\\\":\\\"get_unread_emails\\\","
0677 |         "\\\"parameters\\\":{\\\"limit\\\":5}}'\n\n"
0678 |         "Actions: " + ", ".join(sorted(_ACTIONS)) + "\n"
0679 |     )
0680 | 
0681 | 
0682 | def _main(argv: list[str]) -> int:
0683 |     """Run a single request from the command line and print the JSON result.
0684 | 
0685 |     Input source (first match wins):
0686 |         1. ``argv[1]`` naming an existing file -> read JSON from that file.
0687 |         2. ``argv[1]`` otherwise -> treat it as a JSON string.
0688 |         3. Piped stdin -> read the request from stdin.
0689 |         4. Interactive terminal with no input -> print usage and exit.
0690 |     """
0691 |     if len(argv) > 1:
0692 |         arg = argv[1]
0693 |         if os.path.isfile(arg):
0694 |             with open(arg, "r", encoding="utf-8-sig") as handle:
0695 |                 raw = handle.read()
0696 |         else:
0697 |             raw = arg
0698 |     elif not sys.stdin.isatty():
0699 |         raw = _read_stdin()
0700 |     else:
0701 |         _print_usage()
0702 |         return 2
0703 | 
0704 |     if not raw or not raw.strip():
0705 |         print(json.dumps(_error(None, "No JSON request provided")))
0706 |         return 1
0707 | 
0708 |     response = execute(raw)
0709 |     print(json.dumps(response, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
0710 |     return 0 if response.get("status") == "success" else 1
0711 | 
0712 | 
0713 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0714 |     raise SystemExit(_main(sys.argv))
0715 |

memory_agent.py — Memory management plugin for the MAYA Brain.

0128 | def _update_memory(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0129 |     mgr = _get_manager()
0130 |     success = mgr.update_memory(
0131 |         memory_id=params["memory_id"],
0132 |         content=params.get("content"),
0133 |         importance=params.get("importance"),
0134 |         tags=params.get("tags"),
0135 |     )
0136 |     if success:
0137 |         return {"status": "success", "message": "Memory updated"}
0138 |     return {"status": "error", "message": "Memory not found"}
0139 | 
0140 | 
0141 | def _delete_memory(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0142 |     mgr = _get_manager()
0143 |     success = mgr.delete_memory(params["memory_id"])
0144 |     if success:
0145 |         return {"status": "success", "message": "Memory deleted"}
0146 |     return {"status": "error", "message": "Memory not found"}
0147 | 
0148 | 
0149 | def _get_status(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0150 |     mgr = _get_manager()
0151 |     return {"status": "success", "memory_status": mgr.get_status()}
0152 |

0154 | # ── action registry ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0155 | 
0156 | _ACTIONS: dict[str, Callable] = {
0157 |     "store_memory": _store_memory,

0178 | # ── public entry point ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0179 | 
0180 | 
0181 | def execute(request_json: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0182 |     """Standard MAYA agent entry point."""
0183 |     action = request_json.get("action", "")
0184 |     params = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0185 | 
0186 |     handler = _ACTIONS.get(action)
0187 |     if handler is None:
0188 |         return {
0189 |             "status": "error",
0190 |             "message": f"Unknown action: {action}",
0191 |             "available_actions": list(_ACTIONS.keys()),
0192 |         }
0193 | 
0194 |     required = _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, [])
0195 |     missing = [p for p in required if p not in params]
0196 |     if missing:
0197 |         return {
0198 |             "status": "error",
0199 |             "message": f"Missing required parameters: {missing}",
0200 |         }
0201 | 
0202 |     try:
0203 |         return handler(params)
0204 |     except Exception as exc:
0205 |         return {
0206 |             "status": "error",
0207 |             "message": str(exc),
0208 |             "traceback": traceback.format_exc(),
0209 |         }
0210 | 
0211 | 
0212 | # ── CLI shim ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0213 | 
0214 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0215 |     if len(sys.argv) < 2:
0216 |         print("Usage: python memory_agent.py '<json_request>'")
0217 |         sys.exit(1)
0218 |     arg = sys.argv[1]
0219 |     if Path(arg).exists():
0220 |         request = json.loads(Path(arg).read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
0221 |     else:
0222 |         request = json.loads(arg)
0223 |     result = execute(request)
0224 |     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))

================================================================================
Module: agents\news_agent.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
news_agent.py — News retrieval plugin using NewsAPI (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, summarization,
opinion generation, classification, sentiment analysis, ranking, reasoning,
or decision making. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Calls NewsAPI (https://newsapi.org/v2).
    3. Collects the requested news data.
    4. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

Dependencies (install once)::

    pip install requests python-dotenv

Configuration:
    * ``NEWS_API_KEY`` is read from the environment / a ``.env`` file
      (loaded automatically via python-dotenv). The key is never hardcoded.

CLI usage (handy for the Brain Agent to call as a subprocess)::

    python news_agent.py request.json
    python news_agent.py '{"action": "top_headlines", "parameters": {"country": "us"}}'
    '{"action":"get_sources","parameters":{}}' | python news_agent.py

  - NewsAgentError
    Docstring: Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return....

0100 | def _get_api_key() -> str:
0101 |     """Return the NewsAPI key from the environment.
0102 | 
0103 |     Raises:
0104 |         NewsAgentError: ``NEWS_API_KEY`` is not set.
0105 |     """
0106 |     global _API_KEY_CACHE
0107 |     if _API_KEY_CACHE is None:
0108 |         key = os.getenv("NEWS_API_KEY")
0109 |         if not key or not key.strip():
0110 |             raise NewsAgentError(
0111 |                 "NEWS_API_KEY not found. Add it to your .env file."
0112 |             )
0113 |         _API_KEY_CACHE = key.strip()
0114 |     return _API_KEY_CACHE

0117 | def _get_session() -> requests.Session:
0118 |     """Return a cached :class:`requests.Session` with the API key header set."""
0119 |     global _SESSION
0120 |     if _SESSION is None:
0121 |         session = requests.Session()
0122 |         session.headers.update({"X-Api-Key": _get_api_key()})
0123 |         _SESSION = session

0126 | 
0127 | def _request(endpoint: str, params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0128 |     """Perform a GET against a NewsAPI endpoint and return the parsed JSON.
0129 | 
0130 |     ``None``-valued params are dropped. NewsAPI/network errors are converted
0131 |     into :class:`NewsAgentError` with a safe, human-readable message.
0132 | 
0133 |     Args:
0134 |         endpoint: Endpoint path, e.g. ``"top-headlines"`` or ``"everything"``.
0135 |         params: Query parameters (``None`` values are omitted).
0136 | 
0137 |     Raises:
0138 |         NewsAgentError: On network failure or a NewsAPI error response.
0139 |     """
0140 |     clean_params = {key: value for key, value in params.items() if value is not None}
0141 |     try:
0142 |         response = _get_session().get(
0143 |             f"{NEWSAPI_BASE}/{endpoint}",
0144 |             params=clean_params,
0145 |             timeout=REQUEST_TIMEOUT,
0146 |         )
0147 |     except requests.RequestException as exc:
0148 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Network error contacting NewsAPI: {exc}")
0149 | 
0150 |     try:
0151 |         payload = response.json()
0152 |     except ValueError:
0153 |         raise NewsAgentError(
0154 |             f"NewsAPI returned a non-JSON response (HTTP {response.status_code})"
0155 |         )
0156 | 
0157 |     if response.status_code != 200 or payload.get("status") == "error":
0158 |         message = payload.get("message") or (
0159 |             f"NewsAPI request failed (HTTP {response.status_code})"
0160 |         )
0161 |         raise NewsAgentError(message)
0162 | 
0163 |     return payload
0164 |

0169 | def _require(parameters: dict[str, Any], key: str) -> Any:
0170 |     """Return ``parameters[key]`` or raise if missing/blank."""
0171 |     value = parameters.get(key)
0172 |     if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
0173 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Missing {key} parameter")
0174 |     return value
0175 | 
0176 | 
0177 | def _require_list(parameters: dict[str, Any], key: str) -> list[str]:
0178 |     """Return a validated non-empty list of non-blank strings."""
0179 |     value = parameters.get(key)
0180 |     if value is None:
0181 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Missing {key} parameter")
0182 |     if not isinstance(value, list) or not value:
0183 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be a non-empty list")
0184 |     if not all(isinstance(item, str) and item.strip() for item in value):
0185 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must contain non-empty strings")
0186 |     return value
0187 | 
0188 | 
0189 | def _optional_list(parameters: dict[str, Any], key: str) -> list[str]:
0190 |     """Return a validated list (possibly empty) of non-blank strings."""
0191 |     value = parameters.get(key)
0192 |     if value is None:
0193 |         return []
0194 |     if not isinstance(value, list):
0195 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be a list")
0196 |     if not all(isinstance(item, str) and item.strip() for item in value):
0197 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must contain non-empty strings")
0198 |     return value

0202 |     parameters: dict[str, Any], key: str = "limit", default: int = DEFAULT_LIMIT
0203 | ) -> int:
0204 |     """Parse and clamp an integer ``limit``-style parameter to ``MAX_PAGE_SIZE``."""
0205 |     raw = parameters.get(key, default)
0206 |     try:
0207 |         limit = int(raw)
0208 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0209 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be an integer")
0210 |     if limit <= 0:
0211 |         raise NewsAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be a positive integer")
0212 |     return min(limit, MAX_PAGE_SIZE)

0309 | def _fetch_top_headlines(
0310 |     country: Optional[str] = None,
0311 |     category: Optional[str] = None,
0312 |     sources: Optional[str] = None,
0313 |     query: Optional[str] = None,
0314 |     limit: int = DEFAULT_LIMIT,
0315 | ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0316 |     """Fetch articles from the ``/top-headlines`` endpoint.
0317 | 
0318 |     NewsAPI forbids combining ``sources`` with ``country``/``category``; when
0319 |     ``sources`` is supplied the country/category filters are omitted.
0320 |     """
0321 |     params: dict[str, Any] = {"pageSize": min(limit, MAX_PAGE_SIZE), "q": query}
0322 |     if sources:
0323 |         params["sources"] = sources
0324 |     else:

0327 |     payload = _request("top-headlines", params)
0328 |     articles = [_parse_article(item) for item in payload.get("articles", [])]
0329 |     return articles[:limit]

0336 | def _action_top_headlines(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:

0341 |         _validate_category(category)

0401 | def _action_get_source_news(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0402 |     """Top headlines from a specific source (e.g. ``bbc-news``)."""
0403 |     source = _require(parameters, "source")
0404 |     limit = _get_limit(parameters)
0405 |     articles = _fetch_top_headlines(sources=source, limit=limit)
0406 |     return _data_response(articles)
0407 | 
0408 | 
0409 | def _action_get_sources(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0410 |     """List available NewsAPI sources (optionally filtered)."""
0411 |     category = parameters.get("category")
0412 |     if category is not None:
0413 |         _validate_category(category)
0414 |     payload = _request(
0415 |         "top-headlines/sources",
0416 |         {
0417 |             "category": category,
0418 |             "language": parameters.get("language"),
0419 |             "country": parameters.get("country"),
0420 |         },
0421 |     )
0422 |     sources = [_parse_source(item) for item in payload.get("sources", [])]
0423 |     return _data_response(sources)
0424 | 
0425 | 
0426 | def _action_search_date_range(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0427 |     """Search articles for a query within a date range (``YYYY-MM-DD``)."""
0428 |     query = _require(parameters, "query")
0429 |     from_date = parameters.get("from_date")
0430 |     to_date = parameters.get("to_date")
0431 |     if from_date is not None:
0432 |         _validate_date(from_date)
0433 |     if to_date is not None:
0434 |         _validate_date(to_date)
0435 |     limit = _get_limit(parameters)
0436 |     sort_by = _validate_sort_by(parameters.get("sort_by", "publishedAt"))
0437 |     articles = _fetch_everything(
0438 |         query,
0439 |         limit,
0440 |         sort_by=sort_by,
0441 |         from_date=from_date,
0442 |         to_date=to_date,
0443 |         language=parameters.get("language"),
0444 |     )
0445 |     return _data_response(articles)
0446 | 
0447 | 
0448 | def _action_search_combined(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0449 |     """Aggregate news across topics, categories, and sources in one request."""
0450 |     topics = _optional_list(parameters, "topics")
0451 |     categories = _optional_list(parameters, "categories")
0452 |     sources = _optional_list(parameters, "sources")
0453 |     if not (topics or categories or sources):
0454 |         raise NewsAgentError(
0455 |             "Provide at least one of: topics, categories, sources"
0456 |         )
0457 |     country = parameters.get("country", DEFAULT_COUNTRY)
0458 |     limit = _get_limit(parameters)
0459 | 
0460 |     results: dict[str, dict[str, list[dict[str, Any]]]] = {
0461 |         "topics": {},
0462 |         "categories": {},
0463 |         "sources": {},
0464 |     }
0465 |     for topic in topics:
0466 |         results["topics"][topic] = _fetch_everything(topic, limit)
0467 |     for category in categories:
0468 |         _validate_category(category)
0469 |         results["categories"][category] = _fetch_top_headlines(
0470 |             country=country, category=category, limit=limit
0471 |         )
0472 |     for source in sources:
0473 |         results["sources"][source] = _fetch_top_headlines(sources=source, limit=limit)
0474 | 
0475 |     return {"results": results}
0476 | 
0477 | 
0478 | # Required parameters per action, validated *before* any network call so a
0479 | # malformed request fails fast. Handlers re-validate (and do deeper checks) so
0480 | # they remain safe if called directly.
0481 | _REQUIRED_PARAMS: dict[str, list[str]] = {
0482 |     "search_news": ["query"],
0483 |     "search_multiple_topics": ["topics"],
0484 |     "search_multiple_queries": ["queries"],
0485 |     "get_category_news": ["category"],
0486 |     "get_source_news": ["source"],
0487 |     "search_date_range": ["query"],
0488 | }
0489 | 
0490 | 
0491 | # Action registry: maps an action name to its handler.
0492 | _ACTIONS: dict[str, Callable[[dict[str, Any]], dict[str, Any]]] = {
0493 |     "top_headlines": _action_top_headlines,
0494 |     "search_news": _action_search_news,
0495 |     "search_multiple_topics": _action_search_multiple_topics,
0496 |     "search_multiple_queries": _action_search_multiple_queries,
0497 |     "get_latest_news": _action_get_latest_news,
0498 |     "get_category_news": _action_get_category_news,
0499 |     "get_source_news": _action_get_source_news,
0500 |     "get_sources": _action_get_sources,
0501 |     "search_date_range": _action_search_date_range,
0502 |     "search_combined": _action_search_combined,
0503 | }
0504 | 
0505 | 
0506 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0507 | # Response builder
0508 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0509 | def _error(action: Optional[str], message: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0510 |     """Build a structured error response."""
0511 |     return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": message}
0512 | 
0513 | 
0514 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0515 | # Public interface
0516 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0517 | def execute(request_json: dict) -> dict:
0518 |     """Single public entry point — route a JSON request to a NewsAPI operation.
0519 | 
0520 |     Validates input, dispatches to the matching read-only handler, and always
0521 |     returns a JSON-compatible ``dict``. It never raises; every error becomes a
0522 |     ``{"status": "error", ...}`` response.
0523 | 
0524 |     Args:
0525 |         request_json: A request dict (a JSON string is also accepted and parsed)
0526 |             of the form ``{"action": <str>, "parameters": <dict>}``.
0527 | 
0528 |     Returns:
0529 |         On success a ``{"status": "success", "action": <str>, ...}`` envelope
0530 |         whose remaining keys depend on the action (``count``/``data``,
0531 |         ``total_articles``/``topics``, ``results``, ...). On failure,
0532 |         ``{"status": "error", "action": <str|None>, "message": <str>}``.
0533 |     """
0534 |     action: Optional[str] = None
0535 |     try:
0536 |         # Accept a raw JSON string for convenience, though dict is the contract.
0537 |         # ``lstrip`` drops a leading BOM that some shells (PowerShell) prepend.
0538 |         if isinstance(request_json, str):
0539 |             try:
0540 |                 request_json = json.loads(request_json.lstrip("\ufeff"))
0541 |             except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0542 |                 return _error(None, f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}")
0543 | 
0544 |         if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0545 |             return _error(None, "Request must be a JSON object (dict)")
0546 | 
0547 |         action = request_json.get("action")
0548 |         if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0549 |             return _error(action, "Missing or invalid 'action' field")
0550 | 
0551 |         handler = _ACTIONS.get(action)
0552 |         if handler is None:
0553 |             return _error(action, "Unsupported action")
0554 | 
0555 |         parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0556 |         if parameters is None:
0557 |             parameters = {}
0558 |         if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0559 |             return _error(action, "'parameters' must be a JSON object")
0560 | 
0561 |         # Validate required parameters before any network call (router step 3).
0562 |         for required_key in _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, []):
0563 |             _require(parameters, required_key)
0564 | 
0565 |         result = handler(parameters)
0566 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, **result}
0567 | 
0568 |     except NewsAgentError as exc:
0569 |         return _error(action, str(exc))
0570 |     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - tool must never crash the Brain.
0571 |         return _error(action, f"Unexpected error: {exc}")
0572 | 
0573 | 
0574 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0575 | # CLI shim — accept a JSON request from a file, an argument, or stdin.
0576 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0577 | def _read_stdin() -> str:
0578 |     """Read stdin as bytes and decode with ``utf-8-sig`` to strip any BOM.
0579 | 
0580 |     PowerShell prepends a UTF-8 BOM when piping to a native process, which
0581 |     would otherwise make the JSON unparseable; ``utf-8-sig`` removes it.
0582 |     """
0583 |     return sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig", errors="replace")
0584 | 
0585 | 
0586 | def _print_usage() -> None:
0587 |     """Print CLI usage to stderr (shown when run on a TTY with no input)."""
0588 |     sys.stderr.write(
0589 |         "news_agent - News retrieval tool using NewsAPI (JSON in, JSON out)\n\n"
0590 |         "Provide a JSON request one of these ways:\n\n"
0591 |         "  1) From a file (most reliable on Windows/PowerShell):\n"
0592 |         "       python news_agent.py request.json\n\n"
0593 |         "  2) Piped via stdin:\n"
0594 |         "       '{\"action\":\"top_headlines\",\"parameters\":{\"country\":\"us\"}}'"
0595 |         " | python news_agent.py\n\n"
0596 |         "  3) As one argument with escaped quotes (PowerShell):\n"
0597 |         "       python news_agent.py '{\\\"action\\\":\\\"get_sources\\\","
0598 |         "\\\"parameters\\\":{}}'\n\n"
0599 |         "Actions: " + ", ".join(sorted(_ACTIONS)) + "\n"
0600 |     )
0601 | 
0602 | 
0603 | def _main(argv: list[str]) -> int:
0604 |     """Run a single request from the command line and print the JSON result.
0605 | 
0606 |     Input source (first match wins):
0607 |         1. ``argv[1]`` naming an existing file -> read JSON from that file.
0608 |         2. ``argv[1]`` otherwise -> treat it as a JSON string.
0609 |         3. Piped stdin -> read the request from stdin.
0610 |         4. Interactive terminal with no input -> print usage and exit.
0611 |     """
0612 |     if len(argv) > 1:
0613 |         arg = argv[1]
0614 |         if os.path.isfile(arg):
0615 |             with open(arg, "r", encoding="utf-8-sig") as handle:
0616 |                 raw = handle.read()
0617 |         else:
0618 |             raw = arg
0619 |     elif not sys.stdin.isatty():
0620 |         raw = _read_stdin()
0621 |     else:
0622 |         _print_usage()
0623 |         return 2
0624 | 
0625 |     if not raw or not raw.strip():
0626 |         print(json.dumps(_error(None, "No JSON request provided")))
0627 |         return 1
0628 | 
0629 |     response = execute(raw)
0630 |     print(json.dumps(response, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
0631 |     return 0 if response.get("status") == "success" else 1
0632 | 
0633 | 
0634 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0635 |     raise SystemExit(_main(sys.argv))
0636 | 


================================================================================
Module: agents\notes_generator_agent.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
notes_generator_agent.py — LLM-powered notes and document generation plugin.

Unlike tool-only agents, this agent **uses LLMs** (via Ollama / OpenAI-compatible
APIs) to generate educational, technical, academic, professional, and
documentation content. The Brain Agent decides *when* notes are needed and
*what* topic / structure to request; this agent handles content creation and
document formatting.

Dependencies (install once)::

    pip install ollama python-docx reportlab python-pptx PyPDF2 python-dotenv

Environment variables (read from ``.env`` via python-dotenv)::

    NOTES_MODEL         — Ollama model name  (default: ``gpt-oss:120b``)
    OLLAMA_BASE_URL     — Ollama server URL  (default: ``http://localhost:11434``)
    DEFAULT_OUTPUT_DIR  — output folder      (default: ``generated_notes``)

CLI usage::

    python notes_generator_agent.py request.json
    python notes_generator_agent.py '{"action":"generate_notes","parameters":{"topic":"Docker"}}'

Classes:
  - NotesGeneratorError
    Docstring: Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return....

0100 | def _llm_generate(prompt: str, *, model: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
0101 |     """Send *prompt* to the Ollama chat API and return the assistant reply."""
0102 |     import ollama as _ollama
0103 | 
0104 |     target_model = model or NOTES_MODEL
0105 |     try:
0106 |         client = _ollama.Client(host=OLLAMA_BASE_URL)
0107 |         response = client.chat(
0108 |             model=target_model,
0109 |             messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
0110 |             options={"num_ctx": 16384},
0111 |         )
0112 |         return response.message.content or ""
0113 |     except Exception as exc:
0114 |         raise NotesGeneratorError(f"LLM generation failed ({target_model}): {exc}")

0116 | 
0117 | def _llm_generate_long(prompt: str, word_target: int, *, model: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
0118 |     """Generate content, requesting continuations until *word_target* is met."""
0119 |     accumulated = _llm_generate(prompt, model=model)
0120 |     iteration = 0
0121 |     max_iterations = 15
0122 | 
0123 |     while len(accumulated.split()) < word_target * 0.85 and iteration < max_iterations:
0124 |         iteration += 1
0125 |         cont_prompt = (
0126 |             f"Continue writing from where you left off. "
0127 |             f"You have written {len(accumulated.split())} words so far. "
0128 |             f"Target is {word_target} words. Continue the content seamlessly:\n\n"
0129 |             f"...{accumulated[-1500:]}"
0130 |         )
0131 |         chunk = _llm_generate(cont_prompt, model=model)
0132 |         if not chunk.strip():
0133 |             break
0134 |         accumulated += "\n\n" + chunk
0135 | 
0136 |     return accumulated

0266 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0267 | # Source file reading
0268 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0269 | def _read_source_file(path_str: str) -> str:
0270 |     """Read and extract text from a source file for note generation."""
0271 |     path = Path(path_str).resolve()
0272 |     if not path.exists():
0273 |         raise NotesGeneratorError(f"Source file not found: {path}")
0274 |     if not path.is_file():
0275 |         raise NotesGeneratorError(f"Path is not a file: {path}")
0276 | 
0277 |     ext = path.suffix.lower()
0278 | 
0279 |     if ext in TEXT_EXTENSIONS:
0280 |         try:
0281 |             return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
0282 |         except UnicodeDecodeError:
0283 |             return path.read_text(encoding="latin-1")
0284 | 
0285 |     if ext == ".pdf":
0286 |         try:
0287 |             from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
0288 |         except ImportError:
0289 |             raise NotesGeneratorError("PyPDF2 not installed. Run: pip install PyPDF2")
0290 |         reader = PdfReader(str(path))
0291 |         pages = []
0292 |         for page in reader.pages:
0293 |             text = page.extract_text()
0294 |             if text:
0295 |                 pages.append(text)
0296 |         if not pages:
0297 |             raise NotesGeneratorError("No text could be extracted from PDF")
0298 |         return "\n\n".join(pages)
0299 | 
0300 |     if ext == ".docx":
0301 |         try:
0302 |             from docx import Document
0303 |         except ImportError:
0304 |             raise NotesGeneratorError("python-docx not installed. Run: pip install python-docx")
0305 |         doc = Document(str(path))
0306 |         return "\n".join(p.text for p in doc.paragraphs if p.text.strip())
0307 | 
0308 |     if ext == ".pptx":
0309 |         try:
0310 |             from pptx import Presentation
0311 |         except ImportError:
0312 |             raise NotesGeneratorError("python-pptx not installed. Run: pip install python-pptx")
0313 |         prs = Presentation(str(path))
0314 |         texts = []
0315 |         for slide in prs.slides:
0316 |             for shape in slide.shapes:
0317 |                 if shape.has_text_frame:
0318 |                     for para in shape.text_frame.paragraphs:
0319 |                         t = para.text.strip()
0320 |                         if t:
0321 |                             texts.append(t)
0322 |         if not texts:
0323 |             raise NotesGeneratorError("No text could be extracted from PPTX")
0324 |         return "\n".join(texts)
0325 | 
0326 |     raise NotesGeneratorError(f"Unsupported source file type: {ext}")
0327 | 
0328 | 
0329 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0330 | # Document writers
0331 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0332 | def _output_dir() -> Path:
0333 |     d = _BASE_DIR / DEFAULT_OUTPUT_DIR
0334 |     d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
0335 |     return d
0336 | 
0337 | 
0338 | def _safe_filename(topic: str) -> str:
0339 |     """Convert a topic into a filesystem-safe slug."""
0340 |     slug = re.sub(r"[^\w\s-]", "", topic.lower())
0341 |     slug = re.sub(r"[\s_-]+", "_", slug).strip("_")
0342 |     return slug[:80] or "notes"
0343 | 
0344 | 
0345 | def _write_md(content: str, topic: str) -> Path:
0346 |     name = _safe_filename(topic) + ".md"
0347 |     path = _output_dir() / name
0348 |     path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
0349 |     return path
0350 | 
0351 | 
0352 | def _write_txt(content: str, topic: str) -> Path:
0353 |     plain = content
0354 |     name = _safe_filename(topic) + ".txt"
0355 |     path = _output_dir() / name
0356 |     path.write_text(plain, encoding="utf-8")
0357 |     return path
0358 | 
0359 | 
0360 | def _write_docx(content: str, topic: str) -> Path:
0361 |     try:
0362 |         from docx import Document
0363 |         from docx.shared import Pt
0364 |     except ImportError:
0365 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("python-docx not installed. Run: pip install python-docx")
0366 | 
0367 |     doc = Document()
0368 |     style = doc.styles["Normal"]
0369 |     style.font.name = "Calibri"
0370 |     style.font.size = Pt(11)
0371 | 
0372 |     lines = content.split("\n")
0373 |     for line in lines:
0374 |         stripped = line.strip()
0375 |         if not stripped:
0376 |             continue
0377 |         if stripped.startswith("# "):
0378 |             doc.add_heading(stripped[2:], level=1)
0379 |         elif stripped.startswith("## "):
0380 |             doc.add_heading(stripped[3:], level=2)
0381 |         elif stripped.startswith("### "):
0382 |             doc.add_heading(stripped[4:], level=3)
0383 |         elif stripped.startswith("#### "):
0384 |             doc.add_heading(stripped[5:], level=4)
0385 |         elif stripped.startswith("- ") or stripped.startswith("* "):
0386 |             doc.add_paragraph(stripped[2:], style="List Bullet")
0387 |         elif re.match(r"^\d+\.\s", stripped):
0388 |             text = re.sub(r"^\d+\.\s*", "", stripped)
0389 |             doc.add_paragraph(text, style="List Number")
0390 |         elif stripped.startswith("|") and stripped.endswith("|"):
0391 |             doc.add_paragraph(stripped)
0392 |         else:
0393 |             doc.add_paragraph(stripped)
0394 | 
0395 |     name = _safe_filename(topic) + ".docx"
0396 |     path = _output_dir() / name
0397 |     doc.save(str(path))
0398 |     return path
0399 | 
0400 | 
0401 | def _write_pdf(content: str, topic: str) -> Path:
0402 |     try:
0403 |         from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import A4
0404 |         from reportlab.lib.styles import ParagraphStyle, getSampleStyleSheet
0405 |         from reportlab.lib.units import inch
0406 |         from reportlab.platypus import (
0407 |             Paragraph,
0408 |             SimpleDocTemplate,
0409 |             Spacer,
0410 |         )
0411 |     except ImportError:
0412 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("reportlab not installed. Run: pip install reportlab")
0413 | 
0414 |     name = _safe_filename(topic) + ".pdf"
0415 |     path = _output_dir() / name
0416 |     doc = SimpleDocTemplate(
0417 |         str(path), pagesize=A4,
0418 |         leftMargin=inch, rightMargin=inch,
0419 |         topMargin=inch, bottomMargin=inch,
0420 |     )
0421 | 
0422 |     styles = getSampleStyleSheet()
0423 |     body_style = styles["BodyText"]
0424 |     body_style.fontSize = 11
0425 |     body_style.leading = 15
0426 | 
0427 |     h1 = ParagraphStyle("H1", parent=styles["Heading1"], fontSize=18, spaceAfter=12)
0428 |     h2 = ParagraphStyle("H2", parent=styles["Heading2"], fontSize=15, spaceAfter=10)
0429 |     h3 = ParagraphStyle("H3", parent=styles["Heading3"], fontSize=13, spaceAfter=8)
0430 |     bullet_style = ParagraphStyle("Bullet", parent=body_style, leftIndent=20, bulletIndent=10)
0431 | 
0432 |     story: list[Any] = []
0433 |     lines = content.split("\n")
0434 | 
0435 |     def _esc(text: str) -> str:
0436 |         return text.replace("&", "&amp;").replace("<", "&lt;").replace(">", "&gt;")
0437 | 
0438 |     for line in lines:
0439 |         stripped = line.strip()
0440 |         if not stripped:
0441 |             story.append(Spacer(1, 6))
0442 |             continue
0443 |         if stripped.startswith("# "):
0444 |             story.append(Paragraph(_esc(stripped[2:]), h1))
0445 |         elif stripped.startswith("## "):
0446 |             story.append(Paragraph(_esc(stripped[3:]), h2))
0447 |         elif stripped.startswith("### ") or stripped.startswith("#### "):
0448 |             text = re.sub(r"^#{3,4}\s*", "", stripped)
0449 |             story.append(Paragraph(_esc(text), h3))
0450 |         elif stripped.startswith("- ") or stripped.startswith("* "):
0451 |             story.append(Paragraph(f"• {_esc(stripped[2:])}", bullet_style))
0452 |         elif re.match(r"^\d+\.\s", stripped):
0453 |             story.append(Paragraph(_esc(stripped), body_style))
0454 |         else:
0455 |             story.append(Paragraph(_esc(stripped), body_style))
0456 | 
0457 |     doc.build(story)
0458 |     return path
0459 | 
0460 | 
0461 | def _parse_slides(content: str) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0462 |     """Parse LLM output into slide dicts with title, bullets, speaker_notes.
0463 | 
0464 |     Handles two formats:
0465 |     - Explicit ``SLIDE N: Title`` format (preferred)
0466 |     - Markdown headings (``# Title`` / ``## Title``) as fallback
0467 |     """
0468 |     slides: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0469 |     current: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None
0470 | 
0471 |     section = "bullets"
0472 |     for line in content.split("\n"):
0473 |         stripped = line.strip()
0474 | 
0475 |         slide_match = re.match(r"^SLIDE\s+\d+\s*:\s*(.+)", stripped, re.IGNORECASE)
0476 |         if not slide_match:
0477 |             slide_match = re.match(r"^#{1,2}\s+(.+)", stripped)
0478 | 
0479 |         if slide_match:
0480 |             if current:
0481 |                 slides.append(current)
0482 |             current = {"title": slide_match.group(1).strip(), "bullets": [], "speaker_notes": ""}
0483 |             section = "bullets"
0484 |             continue
0485 |         if current is None:
0486 |             continue
0487 |         if stripped.upper().startswith("CONTENT:"):
0488 |             section = "bullets"
0489 |             continue
0490 |         if stripped.upper().startswith("SPEAKER_NOTES:") or stripped.upper().startswith("SPEAKER NOTES:"):
0491 |             section = "notes"
0492 |             rest = re.sub(r"^SPEAKER[_ ]?NOTES:\s*", "", stripped, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
0493 |             if rest:
0494 |                 current["speaker_notes"] = rest
0495 |             continue
0496 |         if re.match(r"^#{3,}\s+", stripped):
0497 |             bullet = re.sub(r"^#{3,}\s*", "", stripped)
0498 |             if bullet:
0499 |                 current["bullets"].append(bullet)
0500 |             continue
0501 |         if section == "bullets":
0502 |             bullet = re.sub(r"^[-*•\d.]+[\s.)]*", "", stripped)
0503 |             if bullet:
0504 |                 current["bullets"].append(bullet)
0505 |         elif section == "notes":
0506 |             if stripped:
0507 |                 if current["speaker_notes"]:
0508 |                     current["speaker_notes"] += " " + stripped
0509 |                 else:
0510 |                     current["speaker_notes"] = stripped
0511 | 
0512 |     if current:
0513 |         slides.append(current)
0514 |     return slides
0515 | 
0516 | 
0517 | def _write_pptx(content: str, topic: str) -> Path:
0518 |     try:
0519 |         from pptx import Presentation
0520 |         from pptx.util import Inches, Pt
0521 |     except ImportError:
0522 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("python-pptx not installed. Run: pip install python-pptx")
0523 | 
0524 |     slides_data = _parse_slides(content)
0525 |     if not slides_data:
0526 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("Could not parse presentation slides from generated content")
0527 | 
0528 |     prs = Presentation()
0529 |     prs.slide_width = Inches(13.333)
0530 |     prs.slide_height = Inches(7.5)
0531 | 
0532 |     title_layout = prs.slide_layouts[0]
0533 |     content_layout = prs.slide_layouts[1]
0534 | 
0535 |     for i, sd in enumerate(slides_data):
0536 |         layout = title_layout if i == 0 else content_layout
0537 |         slide = prs.slides.add_slide(layout)
0538 | 
0539 |         if slide.placeholders:
0540 |             slide.placeholders[0].text = sd["title"]
0541 | 
0542 |         if len(slide.placeholders) > 1 and sd["bullets"]:
0543 |             tf = slide.placeholders[1].text_frame
0544 |             tf.clear()
0545 |             for j, bullet in enumerate(sd["bullets"]):
0546 |                 if j == 0:
0547 |                     tf.paragraphs[0].text = bullet
0548 |                     tf.paragraphs[0].font.size = Pt(18)
0549 |                 else:
0550 |                     p = tf.add_paragraph()
0551 |                     p.text = bullet
0552 |                     p.font.size = Pt(18)
0553 | 
0554 |         if sd["speaker_notes"]:
0555 |             notes_slide = slide.notes_slide
0556 |             notes_slide.notes_text_frame.text = sd["speaker_notes"]
0557 | 
0558 |     name = _safe_filename(topic) + ".pptx"
0559 |     path = _output_dir() / name
0560 |     prs.save(str(path))
0561 |     return path
0562 | 
0563 | 
0564 | _WRITERS: dict[str, Callable[[str, str], Path]] = {
0565 |     "md": _write_md,
0566 |     "txt": _write_txt,
0567 |     "docx": _write_docx,
0568 |     "pdf": _write_pdf,
0569 |     "pptx": _write_pptx,
0570 | }
0571 | 
0572 | 
0573 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0574 | # Param helpers
0575 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0576 | def _get_topic(params: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
0577 |     topic = str(params.get("topic", "")).strip()
0578 |     if not topic:
0579 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("Missing topic parameter")
0580 |     return topic
0581 | 
0582 | 
0583 | def _get_pages(params: dict[str, Any]) -> int:
0584 |     raw = params.get("pages", DEFAULT_PAGES)
0585 |     try:
0586 |         pages = int(raw)
0587 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0588 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("pages must be an integer")
0589 |     return max(1, min(pages, MAX_PAGES))
0590 | 
0591 | 
0592 | def _get_word_count(params: dict[str, Any], pages: int) -> int:
0593 |     raw = params.get("word_count")
0594 |     if raw is not None:
0595 |         try:
0596 |             return max(100, int(raw))
0597 |         except (TypeError, ValueError):
0598 |             raise NotesGeneratorError("word_count must be an integer")
0599 |     return pages * WORDS_PER_PAGE
0600 | 
0601 | 
0602 | def _get_difficulty(params: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
0603 |     d = str(params.get("difficulty", DEFAULT_DIFFICULTY)).strip().lower()
0604 |     if d not in VALID_DIFFICULTIES:
0605 |         raise NotesGeneratorError(
0606 |             f"Invalid difficulty: {d}. Valid: {', '.join(sorted(VALID_DIFFICULTIES))}"
0607 |         )
0608 |     return d
0609 | 
0610 | 
0611 | def _get_audience(params: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
0612 |     a = str(params.get("audience", DEFAULT_AUDIENCE)).strip().lower()
0613 |     if a not in VALID_AUDIENCES:
0614 |         raise NotesGeneratorError(
0615 |             f"Invalid audience: {a}. Valid: {', '.join(sorted(VALID_AUDIENCES))}"
0616 |         )
0617 |     return a
0618 | 
0619 | 
0620 | def _get_format(params: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
0621 |     f = str(params.get("output_format", params.get("format", DEFAULT_FORMAT))).strip().lower()
0622 |     if f not in VALID_FORMATS:
0623 |         raise NotesGeneratorError(
0624 |             f"Invalid output_format: {f}. Valid: {', '.join(sorted(VALID_FORMATS))}"
0625 |         )
0626 |     return f
0627 | 
0628 | 
0629 | def _get_model(params: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[str]:
0630 |     m = params.get("model")
0631 |     if m and isinstance(m, str) and m.strip():
0632 |         return m.strip()
0633 |     return None
0634 | 
0635 | 
0636 | def _write_output(content: str, topic: str, fmt: str) -> tuple[Path, int]:
0637 |     """Write content in the requested format and return (path, word_count)."""
0638 |     writer = _WRITERS.get(fmt)
0639 |     if not writer:
0640 |         raise NotesGeneratorError(f"No writer for format: {fmt}")
0641 |     path = writer(content, topic)
0642 |     wc = len(content.split())
0643 |     return path, wc
0644 |

0646 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0647 | # Action handlers
0648 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0649 | def _action_generate_notes(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0650 |     topic = _get_topic(params)
0651 |     pages = _get_pages(params)
0652 |     word_count = _get_word_count(params, pages)
0653 |     difficulty = _get_difficulty(params)
0654 |     audience = _get_audience(params)
0655 |     fmt = _get_format(params)
0656 |     model = _get_model(params)
0657 |     structure = params.get("structure")
0658 |     academic = bool(params.get("academic_mode", False))
0659 | 
0660 |     prompt = _build_notes_prompt(topic, word_count, difficulty, audience, structure, academic)
0661 | 
0662 |     if fmt == "pptx":
0663 |         slide_count = max(5, pages * 2)
0664 |         prompt = _build_presentation_prompt(topic, slide_count, difficulty, audience)
0665 |         content = _llm_generate(prompt, model=model)
0666 |     else:
0667 |         content = _llm_generate_long(prompt, word_count, model=model)
0668 | 
0669 |     path, wc = _write_output(content, topic, fmt)
0670 |     return {
0671 |         "file_path": str(path),
0672 |         "pages_generated": max(1, math.ceil(wc / WORDS_PER_PAGE)),
0673 |         "word_count": wc,
0674 |         "topic": topic,
0675 |         "format": fmt,
0676 |     }

0796 | def _action_generate_from_structure(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0797 |     topic = _get_topic(params)
0798 |     structure = params.get("structure")
0799 |     if not structure or not isinstance(structure, list):
0800 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("Missing or invalid structure parameter (expected a list)")
0801 |     if not all(isinstance(s, str) and s.strip() for s in structure):
0802 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("All structure items must be non-empty strings")
0803 | 
0804 |     pages = _get_pages(params)
0805 |     word_count = _get_word_count(params, pages)
0806 |     difficulty = _get_difficulty(params)
0807 |     audience = _get_audience(params)
0808 |     fmt = _get_format(params)
0809 |     model = _get_model(params)
0810 | 
0811 |     prompt = _build_notes_prompt(topic, word_count, difficulty, audience, structure)
0812 |     content = _llm_generate_long(prompt, word_count, model=model)
0813 |     path, wc = _write_output(content, topic, fmt)
0814 |     return {
0815 |         "file_path": str(path),
0816 |         "pages_generated": max(1, math.ceil(wc / WORDS_PER_PAGE)),
0817 |         "word_count": wc,
0818 |         "topic": topic,
0819 |         "format": fmt,
0820 |         "structure_sections": len(structure),
0821 |     }

0823 | 
0824 | def _action_generate_from_prompt(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0825 |     prompt_text = str(params.get("prompt", "")).strip()
0826 |     if not prompt_text:
0827 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("Missing prompt parameter")
0828 | 
0829 |     fmt = _get_format(params)
0830 |     model = _get_model(params)
0831 |     topic = str(params.get("topic", "custom_notes")).strip()
0832 |     word_count = int(params.get("word_count", 2000))
0833 | 
0834 |     content = _llm_generate_long(prompt_text, word_count, model=model)
0835 |     path, wc = _write_output(content, topic, fmt)
0836 |     return {

0838 |         "pages_generated": max(1, math.ceil(wc / WORDS_PER_PAGE)),

0841 |         "format": fmt,

0846 | def _action_generate_from_file(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0847 |     source_path = str(params.get("source_path", params.get("path", ""))).strip()
0848 |     if not source_path:
0849 |         raise NotesGeneratorError("Missing source_path parameter")

0851 |     source_content = _read_source_file(source_path)
0852 |     topic = str(params.get("topic", Path(source_path).stem)).strip()
0853 |     pages = _get_pages(params)
0854 |     word_count = _get_word_count(params, pages)
0855 |     difficulty = _get_difficulty(params)
0856 |     audience = _get_audience(params)
0857 |     fmt = _get_format(params)
0858 |     model = _get_model(params)
0859 | 
0860 |     max_source = 12000
0861 |     if len(source_content) > max_source:
0862 |         source_content = source_content[:max_source] + "\n\n[... content truncated ...]"
0863 | 
0864 |     prompt = textwrap.dedent(f"""\
0865 |         Based on the following source material, create comprehensive,
0866 |         well-structured notes on: "{topic}"
0867 | 
0868 |         Requirements:
0869 |         - Target length: approximately {word_count} words
0870 |         - Difficulty: {difficulty}, Audience: {audience}
0871 |         - Expand on the source material with additional explanations
0872 |         - Rewrite in a professional, clear, educational tone
0873 |         - Use Markdown headings and formatting
0874 |         - Include key takeaways per section
0875 |         - Add examples where the source material lacks them
0876 | 
0877 |         SOURCE MATERIAL:
0878 |         ---
0879 |         {source_content}
0880 |         ---
0881 | 
0882 |         Generate comprehensive notes based on this material.
0883 |         Start the content directly.
0884 |     """).strip()
0885 | 
0886 |     content = _llm_generate_long(prompt, word_count, model=model)
0887 |     path, wc = _write_output(content, topic, fmt)
0888 |     return {
0889 |         "file_path": str(path),
0890 |         "pages_generated": max(1, math.ceil(wc / WORDS_PER_PAGE)),

0927 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0928 | # Public entry point
0929 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0930 | def execute(request_json: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0931 |     """Execute a notes-generation action.
0932 | 
0933 |     Args:
0934 |         request_json: A dict with ``"action"`` (str) and ``"parameters"`` (dict).
0935 | 
0936 |     Returns:
0937 |         A JSON-compatible dict with ``"status"`` (``"success"`` | ``"error"``),
0938 |         ``"action"``, and either ``"data"`` or ``"message"``.
0939 |     """
0940 |     if isinstance(request_json, str):
0941 |         request_json = request_json.lstrip("﻿")
0942 |         try:
0943 |             request_json = json.loads(request_json)
0944 |         except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0945 |             return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON: {exc}"}
0946 | 
0947 |     if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0948 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Request must be a JSON object"}
0949 | 
0950 |     action = request_json.get("action", "")
0951 |     if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0952 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Missing or invalid action field"}
0953 | 
0954 |     if action not in _ACTIONS:
0955 |         return {
0956 |             "status": "error",
0957 |             "action": action,
0958 |             "message": f"Unknown action: {action}. Available: {', '.join(sorted(_ACTIONS))}",
0959 |         }
0960 | 
0961 |     parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0962 |     if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0963 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": "parameters must be a JSON object"}
0964 | 
0965 |     required = _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, [])
0966 |     for key in required:
0967 |         value = parameters.get(key)
0968 |         if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
0969 |             return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Missing required parameter: {key}"}
0970 | 
0971 |     try:
0972 |         data = _ACTIONS[action](parameters)
0973 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, "data": data}
0974 |     except NotesGeneratorError as exc:
0975 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": str(exc)}
0976 |     except Exception as exc:
0977 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Unexpected error: {exc}"}

0991 |                 raw = fh.read().decode("utf-8-sig")

0995 |         raw = sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig")

0998 |             "Usage:\n"
0999 |             '  python notes_generator_agent.py request.json\n'

1003 |             '"parameters":{"topic":"Git"}}\' | python notes_generator_agent.py',

1006 |         sys.exit(2)
1007 | 
1008 |     raw = raw.strip().lstrip("﻿")
1009 |     try:
1010 |         request_data = json.loads(raw)
1011 |     except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
1012 |         result = {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}"}
1013 |         print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
1014 |         sys.exit(1)
1015 | 
1016 |     result = execute(request_data)

================================================================================
Module: agents\project_tracker_agent.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
project_tracker_agent.py — Persistent project knowledge-base plugin (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** business analysis,
recommendations, decision making, prioritization, or project management
advice. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Stores / updates / retrieves project data on disk.
    3. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

Dependencies: Python standard library only.

Storage layout::

    data/projects/index.json          — lightweight project index
    data/projects/{project_id}.json   — full project data per project

CLI usage::

    python project_tracker_agent.py request.json
    python project_tracker_agent.py '{"action":"list_projects","parameters":{}}'

0395 |     pid = _require_project_id(params)
0396 |     todo_id = _require_str(params, "todo_id")
0397 |     project = _load_project(pid)
0398 |     idx, todo = _find_item(project["todos"], todo_id, "Todo")
0399 |     for key in ("title", "description"):
0400 |         if key in params:

0402 |             if key == "title" and not val:
0403 |                 raise ProjectTrackerError("Title cannot be empty")
0404 |             todo[key] = val
0405 |     if "tags" in params:
0406 |         todo["tags"] = params["tags"]
0407 |     todo["updated_at"] = _now()
0408 |     project["todos"][idx] = todo
0409 |     _log_activity(project, "update_todo", f"Todo '{todo['title']}' updated")
0410 |     _save_project(project)

0767 | def _action_get_project_dashboard(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0768 |     pid = _require_project_id(params)

0770 |     todos = project.get("todos", [])
0771 |     milestones = project.get("milestones", [])

0774 |         "project_name": project["project_name"],

0778 |         "total_milestones": len(milestones),
0779 |         "completed_milestones": sum(1 for m in milestones if m.get("status") == "completed"),
0780 |         "total_risks": len(risks),
0781 |         "open_risks": sum(1 for r in risks if r.get("status") == "open"),
0782 |         "total_notes": len(project.get("notes", [])),
0783 |         "total_meetings": len(project.get("meetings", [])),
0784 |         "total_decisions": len(project.get("decisions", [])),
0785 |         "total_links": len(project.get("links", [])),
0786 |         "total_files": len(project.get("files", [])),
0787 |         "total_progress_updates": len(project.get("progress_updates", [])),
0788 |         "last_update": project.get("updated_at", ""),
0789 |     }
