0791 | 
0792 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0793 | # Bulk operations
0794 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0795 | def _action_bulk_add_todos(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0796 |     pid = _require_project_id(params)
0797 |     items = params.get("todos")
0798 |     if not items or not isinstance(items, list):
0799 |         raise ProjectTrackerError("Missing or invalid todos parameter (expected a list)")
0800 |     project = _load_project(pid)
0801 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0802 |     for item in items:
0803 |         if not isinstance(item, dict):
0804 |             results.append({"status": "error", "message": "Each todo must be a JSON object"})
0805 |             continue
0806 |         title = str(item.get("title", "")).strip()
0807 |         if not title:
0808 |             results.append({"status": "error", "message": "Title is required"})
0809 |             continue
0810 |         todo = {
0811 |             "id": _new_id(),
0812 |             "title": title,
0813 |             "description": str(item.get("description", "")).strip(),
0814 |             "status": "pending",
0815 |             "created_at": _now(),
0816 |             "updated_at": _now(),
0817 |             "completed_at": None,
0818 |             "tags": item.get("tags", []),
0819 |         }
0820 |         project["todos"].append(todo)
0821 |         results.append({"status": "success", "todo": todo})
0822 |     added = sum(1 for r in results if r["status"] == "success")
0823 |     _log_activity(project, "bulk_add_todos", f"{added} todos added")
0824 |     _save_project(project)
0825 |     return {"added": added, "total": len(results), "results": results}
0826 | 
0827 | 
0828 | def _action_bulk_complete_todos(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0829 |     pid = _require_project_id(params)
0830 |     ids = params.get("todo_ids")
0831 |     if not ids or not isinstance(ids, list):
0832 |         raise ProjectTrackerError("Missing or invalid todo_ids parameter (expected a list)")
0833 |     project = _load_project(pid)
0834 |     now = _now()
0835 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0836 |     for todo_id in ids:
0837 |         try:
0838 |             idx, todo = _find_item(project["todos"], todo_id, "Todo")
0839 |             if todo["status"] == "completed":
0840 |                 results.append({"status": "error", "id": todo_id, "message": "Already completed"})
0841 |                 continue
0842 |             todo["status"] = "completed"
0843 |             todo["completed_at"] = now

0846 |             results.append({"status": "success", "id": todo_id})
0847 |         except ProjectTrackerError as exc:
0848 |             results.append({"status": "error", "id": todo_id, "message": str(exc)})
0849 |     completed = sum(1 for r in results if r["status"] == "success")
0850 |     _log_activity(project, "bulk_complete_todos", f"{completed} todos completed")

0852 |     return {"completed": completed, "total": len(results), "results": results}

1009 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
1010 | # Public entry point
1011 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
1012 | def execute(request_json: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
1013 |     """Execute a project tracker action.
1014 | 
1015 |     Args:
1016 |         request_json: A dict with ``"action"`` (str) and ``"parameters"`` (dict).
1017 | 
1018 |     Returns:
1019 |         A JSON-compatible dict with ``"status"`` (``"success"`` | ``"error"``),
1020 |         ``"action"``, and either ``"data"`` or ``"message"``.
1021 |     """
1022 |     if isinstance(request_json, str):
1023 |         request_json = request_json.lstrip("﻿")
1024 |         try:
1025 |             request_json = json.loads(request_json)
1026 |         except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
1027 |             return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON: {exc}"}
1028 | 
1029 |     if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
1030 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Request must be a JSON object"}
1031 | 
1032 |     action = request_json.get("action", "")
1033 |     if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
1034 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Missing or invalid action field"}
1035 | 
1036 |     if action not in _ACTIONS:
1037 |         return {
1038 |             "status": "error",
1039 |             "action": action,
1040 |             "message": f"Unknown action: {action}. Available: {', '.join(sorted(_ACTIONS))}",
1041 |         }
1042 | 
1043 |     parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
1044 |     if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
1045 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": "parameters must be a JSON object"}
1046 | 
1047 |     required = _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, [])
1048 |     for key in required:
1049 |         value = parameters.get(key)
1050 |         if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
1051 |             return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Missing required parameter: {key}"}
1052 | 
1053 |     try:
1054 |         data = _ACTIONS[action](parameters)
1055 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, "data": data}
1056 |     except ProjectTrackerError as exc:
1057 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": str(exc)}
1058 |     except Exception as exc:
1059 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Unexpected error: {exc}"}

1066 |     """Handle command-line invocation: file arg, inline JSON arg, or piped stdin."""
1067 |     raw: Optional[str] = None
1068 | 
1069 |     if len(sys.argv) > 1:
1070 |         arg = sys.argv[1]
1071 |         if os.path.isfile(arg):
1072 |             with open(arg, "rb") as fh:
1073 |                 raw = fh.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
1074 |         else:
1075 |             raw = arg
1076 |     elif not sys.stdin.isatty():
1077 |         raw = sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
1078 |     else:
1079 |         print(
1080 |             "Usage:\n"
1081 |             '  python project_tracker_agent.py request.json\n'
1082 |             '  python project_tracker_agent.py \'{"action":"list_projects","parameters":{}}\'\n'
1083 |             '  echo \'{"action":"list_projects","parameters":{}}\' '
1084 |             "| python project_tracker_agent.py",
1085 |             file=sys.stderr,
1086 |         )
1087 |         sys.exit(2)
1088 | 
1089 |     raw = raw.strip().lstrip("﻿")
1090 |     try:
1091 |         request_data = json.loads(raw)
1092 |     except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
1093 |         result = {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}"}
1094 |         print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
1095 |         sys.exit(1)
1096 | 
1097 |     result = execute(request_data)
1098 |     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
1099 |     sys.exit(0 if result.get("status") == "success" else 1)

================================================================================
Module: agents\todo_agent.py

Module Docstring:
todo_agent.py — Persistent todo management plugin (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, prioritization,
reasoning, recommendations, scheduling decisions, intent detection,
productivity advice, or task classification. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Stores, updates, retrieves, or deletes todos in a local JSON file.
    3. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

Dependencies: Python standard library only (no third-party packages).

Storage: ``data/todos.json`` (created automatically on first write).

CLI usage::

    python todo_agent.py request.json
    python todo_agent.py '{"action": "list_all_todos", "parameters": {}}'

Classes:
  - TodoAgentError
    Docstring: Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return....

Functions:
  - _now_iso
    Docstring: Return the current UTC time as an ISO-8601 string....
  - _load_todos
    Docstring: Load the todo list from disk, returning an empty list if absent....
  - _save_todos
    Docstring: Persist the todo list to disk atomically (write-then-rename)....
  - _find_todo
    Docstring: Return the index and dict for *todo_id*, or raise....
  - _make_todo
    Docstring: Build a new todo dict with generated id and timestamps....
  - _action_add_todo
  - _action_update_todo
  - _action_complete_todo
  - _action_reopen_todo
  - _action_delete_todo
  - _action_get_todo
  - _action_list_all_todos
  - _action_list_pending_todos
  - _action_list_completed_todos
  - _action_search_todos
  - _action_filter_by_tag
  - _action_clear_completed

  - _action_bulk_delete

    Docstring: Execute a todo management action....
  - _cli_main
    Docstring: Handle command-line invocation: file arg, inline JSON arg, or piped stdin....

0080 | def _load_todos() -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0081 |     """Load the todo list from disk, returning an empty list if absent."""
0082 |     if not _TODOS_FILE.exists():
0083 |         return []
0084 |     try:
0085 |         raw = _TODOS_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
0086 |         data = json.loads(raw)
0087 |         if isinstance(data, dict):
0088 |             return data.get("todos", [])
0089 |         return []
0090 |     except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError) as exc:
0091 |         raise TodoAgentError(f"Failed to read todos file: {exc}")
0092 | 
0093 | 
0094 | def _save_todos(todos: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> None:
0095 |     """Persist the todo list to disk atomically (write-then-rename)."""
0096 |     _DATA_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
0097 |     tmp_path = _TODOS_FILE.with_suffix(".tmp")
0098 |     try:
0099 |         payload = json.dumps({"todos": todos}, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str)
0100 |         tmp_path.write_text(payload, encoding="utf-8")
0101 |         tmp_path.replace(_TODOS_FILE)
0102 |     except OSError as exc:
0103 |         raise TodoAgentError(f"Failed to save todos: {exc}")

0106 | def _find_todo(todos: list[dict[str, Any]], todo_id: str) -> tuple[int, dict[str, Any]]:
0107 |     """Return the index and dict for *todo_id*, or raise."""
0108 |     for i, todo in enumerate(todos):
0109 |         if todo.get("id") == todo_id:
0110 |             return i, todo
0111 |     raise TodoAgentError("Todo not found")

0156 |     if not todo_id:
0157 |         raise TodoAgentError("Missing todo id")
0158 |     todos = _load_todos()

0162 |     for key in ("title", "description", "tags", "metadata"):
0163 |         if key in params:
0164 |             value = params[key]
0165 |             if key == "title":
0166 |                 if not value or not str(value).strip():
0167 |                     raise TodoAgentError("Title cannot be empty")
0168 |                 value = str(value).strip()

0253 | def _action_search_todos(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0254 |     query = params.get("query", "")
0255 |     if not query or not str(query).strip():
0256 |         raise TodoAgentError("Missing query parameter")
0257 |     query_lower = str(query).strip().lower()
0258 |     todos = _load_todos()
0259 |     matches = []
0260 |     for todo in todos:
0261 |         title = todo.get("title", "").lower()
0262 |         description = todo.get("description", "").lower()
0263 |         tags = [t.lower() for t in todo.get("tags", [])]
0264 |         if (
0265 |             query_lower in title
0266 |             or query_lower in description
0267 |             or any(query_lower in tag for tag in tags)
0268 |         ):
0269 |             matches.append(todo)
0270 |     return {"count": len(matches), "todos": matches}
0271 | 
0272 | 
0273 | def _action_filter_by_tag(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0274 |     tag = params.get("tag", "")
0275 |     if not tag or not str(tag).strip():
0276 |         raise TodoAgentError("Missing tag parameter")
0277 |     tag_lower = str(tag).strip().lower()
0278 |     todos = _load_todos()
0279 |     matches = [
0280 |         t for t in todos
0281 |         if tag_lower in [tg.lower() for tg in t.get("tags", [])]
0282 |     ]
0283 |     return {"count": len(matches), "todos": matches}
0284 |

0286 | def _action_clear_completed(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:

0303 | def _action_bulk_add(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0304 |     items = params.get("todos")
0305 |     if not items or not isinstance(items, list):
0306 |         raise TodoAgentError("Missing or invalid todos parameter (expected a list)")
0307 | 
0308 |     todos = _load_todos()
0309 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0310 |     for item in items:
0311 |         if not isinstance(item, dict):
0312 |             results.append({"status": "error", "message": "Each todo must be a JSON object"})
0313 |             continue
0314 |         title = item.get("title", "")
0315 |         if not title or not str(title).strip():
0316 |             results.append({"status": "error", "message": "Title is required"})
0317 |             continue
0318 |         todo = _make_todo(
0319 |             title=str(title).strip(),
0320 |             description=str(item.get("description", "")).strip(),
0321 |             tags=item.get("tags"),
0322 |             metadata=item.get("metadata"),
0323 |         )
0324 |         todos.append(todo)
0325 |         results.append({"status": "success", "todo": todo})
0326 | 
0327 |     _save_todos(todos)
0328 |     added = sum(1 for r in results if r["status"] == "success")
0329 |     return {"added": added, "total": len(results), "results": results}
0330 | 
0331 | 
0332 | def _action_bulk_complete(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0333 |     ids = params.get("ids")
0334 |     if not ids or not isinstance(ids, list):
0335 |         raise TodoAgentError("Missing or invalid ids parameter (expected a list)")
0336 | 
0337 |     todos = _load_todos()
0338 |     now = _now_iso()
0339 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0340 |     for todo_id in ids:
0341 |         try:
0342 |             idx, todo = _find_todo(todos, todo_id)
0343 |             if todo["status"] == "completed":
0344 |                 results.append({"status": "error", "id": todo_id, "message": "Already completed"})
0345 |                 continue
0346 |             todo["status"] = "completed"
0347 |             todo["completed_at"] = now
0348 |             todo["updated_at"] = now
0349 |             todos[idx] = todo
0350 |             results.append({"status": "success", "id": todo_id})
0351 |         except TodoAgentError as exc:
0352 |             results.append({"status": "error", "id": todo_id, "message": str(exc)})
0353 | 
0354 |     _save_todos(todos)
0355 |     completed = sum(1 for r in results if r["status"] == "success")
0356 |     return {"completed": completed, "total": len(results), "results": results}
0357 | 
0358 | 
0359 | def _action_bulk_delete(params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0360 |     ids = params.get("ids")
0361 |     if not ids or not isinstance(ids, list):
0362 |         raise TodoAgentError("Missing or invalid ids parameter (expected a list)")
0363 | 
0364 |     todos = _load_todos()
0365 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0366 |     ids_to_remove: set[str] = set()
0367 |     for todo_id in ids:
0368 |         try:
0369 |             _find_todo(todos, todo_id)
0370 |             ids_to_remove.add(todo_id)
0371 |             results.append({"status": "success", "id": todo_id})
0372 |         except TodoAgentError as exc:
0373 |             results.append({"status": "error", "id": todo_id, "message": str(exc)})
0374 | 
0375 |     todos = [t for t in todos if t.get("id") not in ids_to_remove]
0376 |     _save_todos(todos)
0377 |     deleted = sum(1 for r in results if r["status"] == "success")
0378 |     return {"deleted": deleted, "total": len(results), "results": results}

0423 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0424 | # Public entry point
0425 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0426 | def execute(request_json: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0427 |     """Execute a todo management action.
0428 | 
0429 |     Args:
0430 |         request_json: A dict with ``"action"`` (str) and ``"parameters"`` (dict).
0431 | 
0432 |     Returns:
0433 |         A JSON-compatible dict with ``"status"`` (``"success"`` | ``"error"``),
0434 |         ``"action"``, and either ``"data"`` or ``"message"``.
0435 |     """
0436 |     if isinstance(request_json, str):
0437 |         request_json = request_json.lstrip("﻿")
0438 |         try:
0439 |             request_json = json.loads(request_json)
0440 |         except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0441 |             return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON: {exc}"}
0442 | 
0443 |     if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0444 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Request must be a JSON object"}
0445 | 
0446 |     action = request_json.get("action", "")
0447 |     if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0448 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Missing or invalid action field"}
0449 | 
0450 |     if action not in _ACTIONS:
0451 |         return {
0452 |             "status": "error",
0453 |             "action": action,
0454 |             "message": f"Unknown action: {action}. Available: {', '.join(sorted(_ACTIONS))}",
0455 |         }
0456 | 
0457 |     parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0458 |     if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0459 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": "parameters must be a JSON object"}
0460 | 
0461 |     required = _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, [])
0462 |     for key in required:
0463 |         value = parameters.get(key)
0464 |         if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
0465 |             return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Missing required parameter: {key}"}
0466 | 
0467 |     try:
0468 |         data = _ACTIONS[action](parameters)
0469 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, "data": data}
0470 |     except TodoAgentError as exc:
0471 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": str(exc)}
0472 |     except Exception as exc:
0473 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Unexpected error: {exc}"}
0474 | 
0475 | 
0476 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0477 | # CLI entry point
0478 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0479 | def _cli_main() -> None:
0480 |     """Handle command-line invocation: file arg, inline JSON arg, or piped stdin."""
0481 |     raw: Optional[str] = None
0482 | 
0483 |     if len(sys.argv) > 1:
0484 |         arg = sys.argv[1]
0485 |         if os.path.isfile(arg):
0486 |             with open(arg, "rb") as fh:
0487 |                 raw = fh.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
0488 |         else:
0489 |             raw = arg
0490 |     elif not sys.stdin.isatty():
0491 |         raw = sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
0492 |     else:
0493 |         print(
0494 |             "Usage:\n"
0495 |             '  python todo_agent.py request.json\n'
0496 |             '  python todo_agent.py \'{"action":"add_todo","parameters":{"title":"Buy milk"}}\'\n'
0497 |             '  echo \'{"action":"list_all_todos","parameters":{}}\' | python todo_agent.py',
0498 |             file=sys.stderr,
0499 |         )
0500 |         sys.exit(2)
0501 | 
0502 |     raw = raw.strip().lstrip("﻿")
0503 |     try:
0504 |         request_data = json.loads(raw)
0505 |     except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0506 |         result = {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}"}
0507 |         print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
0508 |         sys.exit(1)
0509 | 
0510 |     result = execute(request_data)
0511 |     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
0512 |     sys.exit(0 if result.get("status") == "success" else 1)
0513 | 
0514 | 
0515 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0516 |     _cli_main()

================================================================================
Module: agents\weather_agent.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
weather_agent.py — Weather retrieval plugin using Open-Meteo (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, reasoning,
recommendations, summarization, or decision making, and makes no predictions
beyond the data Open-Meteo returns. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Calls the Open-Meteo Geocoding and Forecast APIs.
    3. Retrieves the requested weather information.
    4. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

APIs (no key required):
    * Geocoding: https://geocoding-api.open-meteo.com/v1/search
    * Forecast:  https://api.open-meteo.com/v1/forecast

Dependencies (install once)::

    pip install requests python-dotenv

Optional environment overrides (read from ``.env`` via python-dotenv):
    * ``OPEN_METEO_TIMEOUT``  - per-request timeout in seconds (default 15)
    * ``OPEN_METEO_RETRIES``  - retry attempts on network/5xx errors (default 3)
    * ``OPEN_METEO_BACKOFF``  - base backoff seconds between retries (default 0.5)

CLI usage::

    python weather_agent.py request.json
    python weather_agent.py '{"action": "current_weather", "parameters": {"location": "Bangalore"}}'

Classes:
  - WeatherAgentError
    Docstring: Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return....

Functions:
  - _env_number
    Docstring: Read a numeric environment override, falling back on bad/missing values....
  - _get_session
    Docstring: Return a cached :class:`requests.Session` (Open-Meteo needs no auth)....
  - _get_json
    Docstring: GET ``url`` with retry/backoff and return the parsed JSON payload....
  - _require
    Docstring: Return ``parameters[key]`` or raise if missing/blank....
  - _require_list
    Docstring: Return a validated non-empty list of non-blank strings....
  - _get_int
    Docstring: Parse and clamp an integer parameter....
  - _get_coord
    Docstring: Parse and range-check a latitude/longitude parameter....
  - _describe
    Docstring: Map a WMO weather code to its standard description (``""`` if unknown)....
  - _safe_index
    Docstring: Return ``sequence[index]`` if valid, else ``None``....
  - _map_location
    Docstring: Map a raw geocoding result to a stable metadata dict....
  - _build_current
    Docstring: Build the standard current-weather dict from a forecast payload....
  - _build_daily
    Docstring: Build a list of standard daily-forecast dicts from a forecast payload....
  - _build_hourly
    Docstring: Build a list of hourly dicts (up to ``hours``) from a forecast payload....
  - _resolve_location
    Docstring: Geocode a location name and return the top match....
  - _geocode
    Docstring: Return geocoding matches for ``location`` (newest API order preserved)....
  - _fetch_forecast
    Docstring: Fetch a forecast payload for the requested sections....
  - _current_data
    Docstring: Current weather for a named location....
  - _daily_data
    Docstring: Daily forecast for a named location....
  - _hourly_data
    Docstring: Hourly forecast (up to ``hours``) for a named location....
  - _today_data
    Docstring: Current conditions plus today's daily forecast for a named location....
  - _tomorrow_data
    Docstring: Tomorrow's daily forecast for a named location....
  - _next_days_data
    Docstring: The next ``days`` days (starting tomorrow) for a named location....
  - _multi_current
    Docstring: Current weather for each location; per-location errors are inlined....
  - _action_current_weather
    Docstring: Current weather for a single location....
  - _action_weather_today
    Docstring: Current conditions plus today's daily forecast....
  - _action_hourly_forecast
    Docstring: Hourly forecast for the next ``hours`` hours....
  - _action_daily_forecast
    Docstring: Daily forecast for the next ``days`` days....
  - _action_weather_tomorrow
    Docstring: Tomorrow's daily forecast....
  - _action_weather_next_days
    Docstring: The next ``days`` days (starting tomorrow)....
  - _action_weather_multiple_locations
    Docstring: Current weather for multiple locations, grouped by location....
  - _action_compare_locations
    Docstring: Current weather for multiple locations side by side (no ranking)....
  - _action_search_location
    Docstring: Geocode a location name to coordinates and metadata....
  - _action_weather_by_coordinates
    Docstring: Current weather for explicit latitude/longitude coordinates....
  - _dispatch_bulk
    Docstring: Execute one sub-request inside ``weather_bulk_request``....
  - _action_weather_bulk_request
    Docstring: Run several weather sub-requests in a single call....
  - _error
    Docstring: Build a structured error response....
  - execute
    Docstring: Single public entry point — route a JSON request to an Open-Meteo call....
  - _read_stdin
    Docstring: Read stdin as bytes and decode with ``utf-8-sig`` to strip any BOM....
  - _print_usage
    Docstring: Print CLI usage to stderr (shown when run on a TTY with no input)....
  - _main
    Docstring: Run a single request from the command line and print the JSON result....

0146 |     80: "Slight rain showers",
0147 |     81: "Moderate rain showers",
0148 |     82: "Violent rain showers",
0149 |     85: "Slight snow showers",
0150 |     86: "Heavy snow showers",
0151 |     95: "Thunderstorm",
0152 |     96: "Thunderstorm with slight hail",
0153 |     99: "Thunderstorm with heavy hail",
0154 | }
0155 | 
0156 | 
0157 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0158 | # Exceptions
0159 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0160 | class WeatherAgentError(Exception):
0161 |     """Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return.
0162 | 
0163 |     Covers parameter validation, location-not-found, network failures, and
0164 |     Open-Meteo error responses. These map to a structured ``status: error``
0165 |     response instead of crashing the tool.
0166 |     """
0167 | 
0168 | 
0169 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0170 | # HTTP layer (with retry/backoff)
0171 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0172 | _SESSION: Optional[requests.Session] = None
0173 | 
0174 | 
0175 | def _get_session() -> requests.Session:
0176 |     """Return a cached :class:`requests.Session` (Open-Meteo needs no auth)."""
0177 |     global _SESSION
0178 |     if _SESSION is None:
0179 |         _SESSION = requests.Session()
0180 |     return _SESSION
0181 | 
0182 | 
0183 | def _get_json(url: str, params: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0184 |     """GET ``url`` with retry/backoff and return the parsed JSON payload.
0185 | 
0186 |     Retries on network errors and HTTP 5xx responses (transient); 4xx errors
0187 |     are surfaced immediately using Open-Meteo's ``reason`` field when present.
0188 | 
0189 |     Raises:
0190 |         WeatherAgentError: On exhausted retries, a 4xx/5xx error, or bad JSON.
0191 |     """
0192 |     clean_params = {key: value for key, value in params.items() if value is not None}
0193 |     session = _get_session()
0194 |     last_error: str = "unknown error"
0195 | 
0196 |     for attempt in range(MAX_RETRIES):
0197 |         try:
0198 |             response = session.get(url, params=clean_params, timeout=REQUEST_TIMEOUT)
0199 |         except requests.RequestException as exc:
0200 |             last_error = f"network error ({exc})"
0201 |         else:
0202 |             if response.status_code >= 500:
0203 |                 last_error = f"server error (HTTP {response.status_code})"
0204 |             elif response.status_code != 200:
0205 |                 # Client error — do not retry; surface the API's reason.
0206 |                 reason = None
0207 |                 try:
0208 |                     reason = response.json().get("reason")
0209 |                 except ValueError:
0210 |                     reason = None
0211 |                 raise WeatherAgentError(
0212 |                     reason or f"Open-Meteo request failed (HTTP {response.status_code})"
0213 |                 )
0214 |             else:
0215 |                 try:
0216 |                     return response.json()
0217 |                 except ValueError:
0218 |                     raise WeatherAgentError("Open-Meteo returned a non-JSON response")
0219 | 
0220 |         # Backoff before the next attempt (skip after the final attempt).
0221 |         if attempt < MAX_RETRIES - 1:
0222 |             time.sleep(RETRY_BACKOFF * (2 ** attempt))
0223 | 
0224 |     raise WeatherAgentError(
0225 |         f"Open-Meteo request failed after {MAX_RETRIES} attempts: {last_error}"
0226 |     )
0227 | 
0228 | 
0229 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0230 | # Parameter helpers
0231 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0232 | def _require(parameters: dict[str, Any], key: str) -> Any:
0233 |     """Return ``parameters[key]`` or raise if missing/blank."""
0234 |     value = parameters.get(key)
0235 |     if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
0236 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Missing {key} parameter")
0237 |     return value
0238 | 
0239 | 
0240 | def _require_list(parameters: dict[str, Any], key: str) -> list[str]:
0241 |     """Return a validated non-empty list of non-blank strings."""
0242 |     value = parameters.get(key)
0243 |     if value is None:
0244 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Missing {key} parameter")
0245 |     if not isinstance(value, list) or not value:
0246 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be a non-empty list")
0247 |     if not all(isinstance(item, str) and item.strip() for item in value):
0248 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must contain non-empty strings")
0249 |     return value
0250 | 
0251 | 
0252 | def _get_int(
0253 |     parameters: dict[str, Any],
0254 |     key: str,
0255 |     default: int,
0256 |     minimum: int = 1,
0257 |     maximum: Optional[int] = None,
0258 | ) -> int:
0259 |     """Parse and clamp an integer parameter."""
0260 |     raw = parameters.get(key, default)
0261 |     try:
0262 |         value = int(raw)
0263 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0264 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be an integer")
0265 |     if value < minimum:
0266 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be >= {minimum}")
0267 |     if maximum is not None:
0268 |         value = min(value, maximum)
0269 |     return value
0270 | 
0271 | 
0272 | def _get_coord(parameters: dict[str, Any], key: str, low: float, high: float) -> float:
0273 |     """Parse and range-check a latitude/longitude parameter."""
0274 |     value = parameters.get(key)
0275 |     if value is None:
0276 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Missing {key} parameter")
0277 |     try:
0278 |         coord = float(value)
0279 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0280 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be a number")
0281 |     if not low <= coord <= high:
0282 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be between {low} and {high}")
0283 |     return coord
0284 | 
0285 | 
0286 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0287 | # Data shaping (pure mapping — no interpretation)
0288 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0289 | def _describe(code: Any) -> str:
0290 |     """Map a WMO weather code to its standard description (``""`` if unknown)."""
0291 |     if code is None:
0292 |         return ""
0293 |     try:
0294 |         return _WMO_CODES.get(int(code), "Unknown")
0295 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0296 |         return "Unknown"
0297 | 
0298 | 
0299 | def _safe_index(sequence: Any, index: int) -> Any:
0300 |     """Return ``sequence[index]`` if valid, else ``None``."""
0301 |     if isinstance(sequence, list) and 0 <= index < len(sequence):
0302 |         return sequence[index]
0303 |     return None
0304 | 
0305 | 
0306 | def _map_location(result: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0307 |     """Map a raw geocoding result to a stable metadata dict."""
0308 |     return {
0309 |         "id": result.get("id"),
0310 |         "name": result.get("name", ""),
0311 |         "latitude": result.get("latitude"),
0312 |         "longitude": result.get("longitude"),
0313 |         "country": result.get("country", ""),
0314 |         "country_code": result.get("country_code", ""),
0315 |         "admin1": result.get("admin1", ""),
0316 |         "timezone": result.get("timezone", ""),
0317 |         "population": result.get("population"),
0318 |         "elevation": result.get("elevation"),
0319 |         "feature_code": result.get("feature_code", ""),
0320 |     }
0321 | 
0322 | 
0323 | def _build_current(
0324 |     name: str, latitude: float, longitude: float, forecast: dict[str, Any]
0325 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
0326 |     """Build the standard current-weather dict from a forecast payload."""
0327 |     current = forecast.get("current", {}) or {}
0328 |     code = current.get("weather_code")
0329 |     return {
0330 |         "location": name,
0331 |         "latitude": latitude,
0332 |         "longitude": longitude,
0333 |         "temperature": current.get("temperature_2m"),
0334 |         "feels_like": current.get("apparent_temperature"),
0335 |         "humidity": current.get("relative_humidity_2m"),
0336 |         "wind_speed": current.get("wind_speed_10m"),
0337 |         "wind_direction": current.get("wind_direction_10m"),
0338 |         "weather_code": code,
0339 |         "weather_description": _describe(code),
0340 |         "is_day": bool(current.get("is_day")),
0341 |         "time": current.get("time", ""),
0342 |     }
0343 | 
0344 | 
0345 | def _build_daily(forecast: dict[str, Any]) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0346 |     """Build a list of standard daily-forecast dicts from a forecast payload."""
0347 |     daily = forecast.get("daily", {}) or {}
0348 |     dates = daily.get("time", []) or []
0349 |     out: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0350 |     for i, date in enumerate(dates):
0351 |         code = _safe_index(daily.get("weather_code"), i)
0352 |         out.append(
0353 |             {
0354 |                 "date": date,
0355 |                 "temp_max": _safe_index(daily.get("temperature_2m_max"), i),
0356 |                 "temp_min": _safe_index(daily.get("temperature_2m_min"), i),
0357 |                 "precipitation_probability": _safe_index(
0358 |                     daily.get("precipitation_probability_max"), i
0359 |                 ),
0360 |                 "weather_code": code,
0361 |                 "weather_description": _describe(code),
0362 |             }
0363 |         )
0364 |     return out
0365 | 
0366 | 
0367 | def _build_hourly(forecast: dict[str, Any], hours: int) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0368 |     """Build a list of hourly dicts (up to ``hours``) from a forecast payload."""
0369 |     hourly = forecast.get("hourly", {}) or {}
0370 |     times = hourly.get("time", []) or []
0371 |     out: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0372 |     for i, timestamp in enumerate(times[:hours]):
0373 |         code = _safe_index(hourly.get("weather_code"), i)
0374 |         out.append(
0375 |             {
0376 |                 "time": timestamp,
0377 |                 "temperature": _safe_index(hourly.get("temperature_2m"), i),
0378 |                 "feels_like": _safe_index(hourly.get("apparent_temperature"), i),
0379 |                 "humidity": _safe_index(hourly.get("relative_humidity_2m"), i),
0380 |                 "precipitation_probability": _safe_index(
0381 |                     hourly.get("precipitation_probability"), i
0382 |                 ),
0383 |                 "weather_code": code,
0384 |                 "weather_description": _describe(code),
0385 |                 "wind_speed": _safe_index(hourly.get("wind_speed_10m"), i),
0386 |                 "wind_direction": _safe_index(hourly.get("wind_direction_10m"), i),
0387 |             }
0388 |         )
0389 |     return out
0390 | 
0391 | 
0392 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0393 | # Open-Meteo fetch helpers
0394 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0395 | def _resolve_location(location: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0396 |     """Geocode a location name and return the top match.
0397 | 
0398 |     Raises:
0399 |         WeatherAgentError: No matching location was found.
0400 |     """
0401 |     results = _geocode(location)
0402 |     return results[0]
0403 | 
0404 | 
0405 | def _geocode(location: str) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0406 |     """Return geocoding matches for ``location`` (newest API order preserved).
0407 | 
0408 |     Raises:
0409 |         WeatherAgentError: No matching location was found.
0410 |     """
0411 |     payload = _get_json(
0412 |         GEOCODING_URL,
0413 |         {"name": location, "count": GEOCODE_RESULTS, "language": "en", "format": "json"},
0414 |     )
0415 |     results = payload.get("results") or []
0416 |     if not results:
0417 |         raise WeatherAgentError(f"Location not found: {location}")
0418 |     return results
0419 | 
0420 | 
0421 | def _fetch_forecast(
0422 |     latitude: float,
0423 |     longitude: float,
0424 |     current: bool = False,
0425 |     hourly: bool = False,
0426 |     daily: bool = False,
0427 |     forecast_days: Optional[int] = None,
0428 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
0429 |     """Fetch a forecast payload for the requested sections."""
0430 |     params: dict[str, Any] = {
0431 |         "latitude": latitude,
0432 |         "longitude": longitude,
0433 |         "timezone": "auto",
0434 |     }
0435 |     if current:
0436 |         params["current"] = ",".join(CURRENT_FIELDS)
0437 |     if hourly:
0438 |         params["hourly"] = ",".join(HOURLY_FIELDS)
0439 |     if daily:
0440 |         params["daily"] = ",".join(DAILY_FIELDS)
0441 |     if forecast_days is not None:
0442 |         params["forecast_days"] = max(1, min(forecast_days, MAX_FORECAST_DAYS))
0443 |     return _get_json(FORECAST_URL, params)
0444 | 
0445 | 
0446 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0447 | # Core data builders (resolve -> fetch -> shape). Reused by handlers and bulk.
0448 | # Each raises WeatherAgentError on failure.
0449 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0450 | def _current_data(location: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0451 |     """Current weather for a named location."""
0452 |     loc = _resolve_location(location)
0453 |     forecast = _fetch_forecast(loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], current=True)
0454 |     return _build_current(loc["name"], loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], forecast)
0455 | 
0456 | 
0457 | def _daily_data(location: str, days: int) -> dict[str, Any]:
0458 |     """Daily forecast for a named location."""
0459 |     loc = _resolve_location(location)
0460 |     forecast = _fetch_forecast(
0461 |         loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], daily=True, forecast_days=days
0462 |     )
0463 |     daily = _build_daily(forecast)
0464 |     return {
0465 |         "location": loc["name"],
0466 |         "latitude": loc["latitude"],
0467 |         "longitude": loc["longitude"],
0468 |         "count": len(daily),
0469 |         "daily": daily,
0470 |     }
0471 | 
0472 | 
0473 | def _hourly_data(location: str, hours: int) -> dict[str, Any]:
0474 |     """Hourly forecast (up to ``hours``) for a named location."""
0475 |     loc = _resolve_location(location)
0476 |     days_needed = min(MAX_FORECAST_DAYS, max(1, math.ceil(hours / 24)))
0477 |     forecast = _fetch_forecast(
0478 |         loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], hourly=True, forecast_days=days_needed
0479 |     )
0480 |     hourly = _build_hourly(forecast, hours)
0481 |     return {
0482 |         "location": loc["name"],
0483 |         "latitude": loc["latitude"],
0484 |         "longitude": loc["longitude"],
0485 |         "count": len(hourly),
0486 |         "hourly": hourly,
0487 |     }
0488 | 
0489 | 
0490 | def _today_data(location: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0491 |     """Current conditions plus today's daily forecast for a named location."""
0492 |     loc = _resolve_location(location)
0493 |     forecast = _fetch_forecast(
0494 |         loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], current=True, daily=True, forecast_days=1
0495 |     )
0496 |     daily = _build_daily(forecast)
0497 |     return {
0498 |         "location": loc["name"],
0499 |         "latitude": loc["latitude"],
0500 |         "longitude": loc["longitude"],
0501 |         "current": _build_current(
0502 |             loc["name"], loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], forecast
0503 |         ),
0504 |         "today": daily[0] if daily else None,
0505 |     }
0506 | 
0507 | 
0508 | def _tomorrow_data(location: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0509 |     """Tomorrow's daily forecast for a named location."""
0510 |     loc = _resolve_location(location)
0511 |     forecast = _fetch_forecast(
0512 |         loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], daily=True, forecast_days=2
0513 |     )
0514 |     daily = _build_daily(forecast)
0515 |     return {
0516 |         "location": loc["name"],
0517 |         "latitude": loc["latitude"],
0518 |         "longitude": loc["longitude"],
0519 |         "tomorrow": daily[1] if len(daily) > 1 else None,
0520 |     }
0521 | 
0522 | 
0523 | def _next_days_data(location: str, days: int) -> dict[str, Any]:
0524 |     """The next ``days`` days (starting tomorrow) for a named location."""
0525 |     loc = _resolve_location(location)
0526 |     forecast = _fetch_forecast(
0527 |         loc["latitude"], loc["longitude"], daily=True, forecast_days=days + 1
0528 |     )
0529 |     daily = _build_daily(forecast)
0530 |     upcoming = daily[1 : days + 1]
0531 |     return {
0532 |         "location": loc["name"],
0533 |         "latitude": loc["latitude"],
0534 |         "longitude": loc["longitude"],
0535 |         "count": len(upcoming),
0536 |         "days": upcoming,
0537 |     }
0538 | 
0539 | 
0540 | def _multi_current(locations: list[str]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0541 |     """Current weather for each location; per-location errors are inlined."""
0542 |     results: dict[str, Any] = {}
0543 |     for location in locations:
0544 |         try:
0545 |             results[location] = _current_data(location)
0546 |         except WeatherAgentError as exc:
0547 |             results[location] = {"error": str(exc)}
0548 |     return results
0549 | 
0550 | 
0551 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0552 | # Action handlers — each returns a response fragment merged into the base
0553 | # success envelope. None interpret, rank, recommend, or summarize.
0554 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0555 | def _action_current_weather(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0556 |     """Current weather for a single location."""
0557 |     return {"data": _current_data(_require(parameters, "location"))}
0558 | 
0559 | 
0560 | def _action_weather_today(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0561 |     """Current conditions plus today's daily forecast."""
0562 |     return {"data": _today_data(_require(parameters, "location"))}
0563 | 
0564 | 
0565 | def _action_hourly_forecast(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0566 |     """Hourly forecast for the next ``hours`` hours."""
0567 |     location = _require(parameters, "location")
0568 |     hours = _get_int(parameters, "hours", DEFAULT_HOURS, maximum=MAX_FORECAST_DAYS * 24)
0569 |     return {"data": _hourly_data(location, hours)}
0570 | 
0571 | 
0572 | def _action_daily_forecast(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0573 |     """Daily forecast for the next ``days`` days."""
0574 |     location = _require(parameters, "location")
0575 |     days = _get_int(parameters, "days", DEFAULT_FORECAST_DAYS, maximum=MAX_FORECAST_DAYS)
0576 |     return {"data": _daily_data(location, days)}
0577 | 
0578 | 
0579 | def _action_weather_tomorrow(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0580 |     """Tomorrow's daily forecast."""
0581 |     return {"data": _tomorrow_data(_require(parameters, "location"))}
0582 | 
0583 | 
0584 | def _action_weather_next_days(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0585 |     """The next ``days`` days (starting tomorrow)."""
0586 |     location = _require(parameters, "location")
0587 |     days = _get_int(
0588 |         parameters, "days", DEFAULT_NEXT_DAYS, maximum=MAX_FORECAST_DAYS - 1
0589 |     )
0590 |     return {"data": _next_days_data(location, days)}
0591 | 
0592 | 
0593 | def _action_weather_multiple_locations(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0594 |     """Current weather for multiple locations, grouped by location."""
0595 |     locations = _require_list(parameters, "locations")
0596 |     return {"results": _multi_current(locations)}
0597 | 
0598 | 
0599 | def _action_compare_locations(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0600 |     """Current weather for multiple locations side by side (no ranking)."""
0601 |     locations = _require_list(parameters, "locations")
0602 |     return {"results": _multi_current(locations)}
0603 | 
0604 | 
0605 | def _action_search_location(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0606 |     """Geocode a location name to coordinates and metadata."""
0607 |     location = _require(parameters, "location")
0608 |     results = _geocode(location)
0609 |     mapped = [_map_location(item) for item in results]
0610 |     return {"data": {"query": location, "count": len(mapped), "results": mapped}}
0611 | 
0612 | 
0613 | def _action_weather_by_coordinates(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0614 |     """Current weather for explicit latitude/longitude coordinates."""
0615 |     latitude = _get_coord(parameters, "latitude", -90.0, 90.0)
0616 |     longitude = _get_coord(parameters, "longitude", -180.0, 180.0)
0617 |     forecast = _fetch_forecast(latitude, longitude, current=True)
0618 |     name = f"{latitude},{longitude}"
0619 |     return {"data": _build_current(name, latitude, longitude, forecast)}
0620 | 
0621 | 
0622 | def _dispatch_bulk(item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0623 |     """Execute one sub-request inside ``weather_bulk_request``."""
0624 |     request_type = str(item.get("type") or "current").lower()
0625 |     location = _require(item, "location")
0626 | 
0627 |     if request_type == "current":
0628 |         return _current_data(location)
0629 |     if request_type in ("forecast", "daily"):
0630 |         days = _get_int(item, "days", DEFAULT_FORECAST_DAYS, maximum=MAX_FORECAST_DAYS)
0631 |         return _daily_data(location, days)
0632 |     if request_type == "hourly":
0633 |         hours = _get_int(item, "hours", DEFAULT_HOURS, maximum=MAX_FORECAST_DAYS * 24)
0634 |         return _hourly_data(location, hours)
0635 |     if request_type == "today":
0636 |         return _today_data(location)
0637 |     if request_type == "tomorrow":
0638 |         return _tomorrow_data(location)
0639 |     raise WeatherAgentError(f"Unsupported bulk request type: {request_type}")
0640 | 
0641 | 
0642 | def _action_weather_bulk_request(parameters: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0643 |     """Run several weather sub-requests in a single call."""
0644 |     requests_list = parameters.get("requests")
0645 |     if not isinstance(requests_list, list) or not requests_list:
0646 |         raise WeatherAgentError("Parameter 'requests' must be a non-empty list")
0647 | 
0648 |     results: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0649 |     for index, item in enumerate(requests_list):
0650 |         if not isinstance(item, dict):
0651 |             results.append(
0652 |                 {"status": "error", "message": f"Request #{index} must be an object"}
0653 |             )
0654 |             continue
0655 |         entry: dict[str, Any] = {
0656 |             "location": item.get("location"),
0657 |             "type": str(item.get("type") or "current").lower(),
0658 |         }
0659 |         try:
0660 |             entry["status"] = "success"
0661 |             entry["data"] = _dispatch_bulk(item)
0662 |         except WeatherAgentError as exc:
0663 |             entry["status"] = "error"
0664 |             entry["message"] = str(exc)
0665 |         results.append(entry)
0666 |     return {"results": results}
0667 | 
0668 | 
0669 | # Required parameters per action, validated before any network call. Handlers
0670 | # re-validate (and do deeper checks) so they remain safe if called directly.
0671 | _REQUIRED_PARAMS: dict[str, list[str]] = {
0672 |     "current_weather": ["location"],
0673 |     "weather_today": ["location"],
0674 |     "hourly_forecast": ["location"],
0675 |     "daily_forecast": ["location"],
0676 |     "weather_tomorrow": ["location"],
0677 |     "weather_next_days": ["location"],
0678 |     "weather_multiple_locations": ["locations"],
0679 |     "compare_locations": ["locations"],
0680 |     "search_location": ["location"],
0681 |     "weather_by_coordinates": ["latitude", "longitude"],
0682 |     "weather_bulk_request": ["requests"],
0683 | }
0684 | 
0685 | 
0686 | # Action registry: maps an action name to its handler.
0687 | _ACTIONS: dict[str, Callable[[dict[str, Any]], dict[str, Any]]] = {
0688 |     "current_weather": _action_current_weather,
0689 |     "weather_today": _action_weather_today,
0690 |     "hourly_forecast": _action_hourly_forecast,
0691 |     "daily_forecast": _action_daily_forecast,
0692 |     "weather_tomorrow": _action_weather_tomorrow,
0693 |     "weather_next_days": _action_weather_next_days,
0694 |     "weather_multiple_locations": _action_weather_multiple_locations,
0695 |     "compare_locations": _action_compare_locations,
0696 |     "search_location": _action_search_location,
0697 |     "weather_by_coordinates": _action_weather_by_coordinates,
0698 |     "weather_bulk_request": _action_weather_bulk_request,
0699 | }
0700 | 
0701 | 
0702 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0703 | # Response builder
0704 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0705 | def _error(action: Optional[str], message: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
0706 |     """Build a structured error response."""
0707 |     return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": message}
0708 | 
0709 | 
0710 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0711 | # Public interface
0712 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0713 | def execute(request_json: dict) -> dict:
0714 |     """Single public entry point — route a JSON request to an Open-Meteo call.
0715 | 
0716 |     Validates input, dispatches to the matching handler, and always returns a
0717 |     JSON-compatible ``dict``. It never raises; every error becomes a
0718 |     ``{"status": "error", ...}`` response.
0719 | 
0720 |     Args:
0721 |         request_json: A request dict (a JSON string is also accepted and parsed)
0722 |             of the form ``{"action": <str>, "parameters": <dict>}``.
0723 | 
0724 |     Returns:
0725 |         On success a ``{"status": "success", "action": <str>, ...}`` envelope
0726 |         whose remaining keys depend on the action (``data`` or ``results``).
0727 |         On failure, ``{"status": "error", "action": <str|None>, "message": ...}``.
0728 |     """
0729 |     action: Optional[str] = None
0730 |     try:
0731 |         # Accept a raw JSON string for convenience, though dict is the contract.
0732 |         # ``lstrip`` drops a leading BOM that some shells (PowerShell) prepend.
0733 |         if isinstance(request_json, str):
0734 |             try:
0735 |                 request_json = json.loads(request_json.lstrip("\ufeff"))
0736 |             except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0737 |                 return _error(None, f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}")
0738 | 
0739 |         if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0740 |             return _error(None, "Request must be a JSON object (dict)")
0741 | 
0742 |         action = request_json.get("action")
0743 |         if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0744 |             return _error(action, "Missing or invalid 'action' field")
0745 | 
0746 |         handler = _ACTIONS.get(action)
0747 |         if handler is None:
0748 |             return _error(action, "Unsupported action")
0749 | 
0750 |         parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0751 |         if parameters is None:
0752 |             parameters = {}
0753 |         if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0754 |             return _error(action, "'parameters' must be a JSON object")
0755 | 
0756 |         # Validate required parameters before any network call (router step 3).
0757 |         for required_key in _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, []):
0758 |             _require(parameters, required_key)
0759 | 
0760 |         result = handler(parameters)
0761 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, **result}
0762 | 
0763 |     except WeatherAgentError as exc:
0764 |         return _error(action, str(exc))
0765 |     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - tool must never crash the Brain.
0766 |         return _error(action, f"Unexpected error: {exc}")
0767 | 
0768 | 
0769 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0770 | # CLI shim — accept a JSON request from a file, an argument, or stdin.
0771 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0772 | def _read_stdin() -> str:
0773 |     """Read stdin as bytes and decode with ``utf-8-sig`` to strip any BOM."""
0774 |     return sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig", errors="replace")
0775 | 
0776 | 
0777 | def _print_usage() -> None:
0778 |     """Print CLI usage to stderr (shown when run on a TTY with no input)."""
0779 |     sys.stderr.write(
0780 |         "weather_agent - Weather retrieval tool using Open-Meteo (JSON in/out)\n\n"
0781 |         "Provide a JSON request one of these ways:\n\n"
0782 |         "  1) From a file (most reliable on Windows/PowerShell):\n"
0783 |         "       python weather_agent.py request.json\n\n"
0784 |         "  2) Piped via stdin:\n"
0785 |         "       '{\"action\":\"current_weather\",\"parameters\":{\"location\":\"Bangalore\"}}'"
0786 |         " | python weather_agent.py\n\n"
0787 |         "  3) As one argument with escaped quotes (PowerShell):\n"
0788 |         "       python weather_agent.py '{\\\"action\\\":\\\"current_weather\\\","
0789 |         "\\\"parameters\\\":{\\\"location\\\":\\\"Bangalore\\\"}}'\n\n"
0790 |         "Actions: " + ", ".join(sorted(_ACTIONS)) + "\n"
0791 |     )
0792 | 
0793 | 
0794 | def _main(argv: list[str]) -> int:
0795 |     """Run a single request from the command line and print the JSON result.
0796 | 
0797 |     Input source (first match wins):
0798 |         1. ``argv[1]`` naming an existing file -> read JSON from that file.
0799 |         2. ``argv[1]`` otherwise -> treat it as a JSON string.
0800 |         3. Piped stdin -> read the request from stdin.
0801 |         4. Interactive terminal with no input -> print usage and exit.
0802 |     """
0803 |     if len(argv) > 1:
0804 |         arg = argv[1]
0805 |         if os.path.isfile(arg):
0806 |             with open(arg, "r", encoding="utf-8-sig") as handle:
0807 |                 raw = handle.read()
0808 |         else:
0809 |             raw = arg
0810 |     elif not sys.stdin.isatty():
0811 |         raw = _read_stdin()
0812 |     else:
0813 |         _print_usage()
0814 |         return 2
0815 | 
0816 |     if not raw or not raw.strip():
0817 |         print(json.dumps(_error(None, "No JSON request provided")))
0818 |         return 1
0819 | 
0820 |     response = execute(raw)
0821 |     print(json.dumps(response, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
0822 |     return 0 if response.get("status") == "success" else 1
0823 | 
0824 | 
0825 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0826 |     raise SystemExit(_main(sys.argv))
0827 | 


================================================================================
Module: agents\youtube_agent.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
youtube_agent.py — YouTube search and playback plugin (TOOL ONLY).

This module is a *pure tool*. It performs **no** analysis, summarization,
recommendations, reasoning, intent detection, or decision making. It only:

    1. Receives a JSON-compatible ``dict`` request.
    2. Searches YouTube or retrieves video/channel/playlist metadata via yt-dlp.
    3. Optionally opens URLs in the default browser.
    4. Returns a JSON-compatible ``dict`` response.

All intelligence belongs to the calling "Brain Agent". The single public
entry point is :func:`execute`.

Dependencies (install once)::

    pip install yt-dlp

No API keys required.

CLI usage::

    python youtube_agent.py request.json
    python youtube_agent.py '{"action": "search_videos", "parameters": {"query": "Python tutorial", "limit": 5}}'

Classes:
  - YouTubeAgentError
    Docstring: Raised for any handled error whose message is safe to return....

0091 | def _clamp_limit(params: dict[str, Any], key: str = "limit") -> int:
0092 |     """Parse and clamp a limit parameter."""
0093 |     raw = params.get(key, DEFAULT_LIMIT)
0094 |     try:
0095 |         n = int(raw)
0096 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0097 |         raise YouTubeAgentError(f"Parameter '{key}' must be an integer")
0098 |     if n < 1:
0099 |         n = 1
0100 |     if n > MAX_LIMIT:
0101 |         n = MAX_LIMIT
0102 |     return n

0104 | 
0105 | def _format_duration(seconds: Any) -> str:
0106 |     """Convert numeric seconds to HH:MM:SS or MM:SS string."""
0107 |     if seconds is None:
0108 |         return ""
0109 |     try:
0110 |         total = int(seconds)
0111 |     except (TypeError, ValueError):
0112 |         return str(seconds)
0113 |     hours, remainder = divmod(total, 3600)
0114 |     minutes, secs = divmod(remainder, 60)
0115 |     if hours:
0116 |         return f"{hours}:{minutes:02d}:{secs:02d}"
0117 |     return f"{minutes}:{secs:02d}"
0118 | 
0119 | 
0120 | def _format_date(raw: Any) -> str:
0121 |     """Convert YYYYMMDD to YYYY-MM-DD, or return as-is."""
0122 |     if not raw or not isinstance(raw, str):
0123 |         return str(raw) if raw else ""
0124 |     if len(raw) == 8 and raw.isdigit():
0125 |         return f"{raw[:4]}-{raw[4:6]}-{raw[6:]}"
0126 |     return raw
0127 |

0129 | def _best_thumbnail(entry: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
0130 |     """Pick the best thumbnail URL from an entry."""
0131 |     thumb = entry.get("thumbnail")
0132 |     if thumb:
0133 |         return thumb
0134 |     thumbnails = entry.get("thumbnails")
0135 |     if thumbnails and isinstance(thumbnails, list):
0136 |         best = max(thumbnails, key=lambda t: t.get("width", 0) * t.get("height", 0))
0137 |         return best.get("url", "")
0138 |     vid = entry.get("id", "")
0139 |     if vid:
0140 |         return f"https://i.ytimg.com/vi/{vid}/hqdefault.jpg"
0141 |     return ""
0142 |

0144 | def _parse_entry(entry: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:

0150 |         "channel": entry.get("channel") or entry.get("uploader", ""),
0151 |         "channel_url": entry.get("channel_url") or entry.get("uploader_url", ""),
0152 |         "duration": _format_duration(entry.get("duration")),
0153 |         "duration_seconds": entry.get("duration"),
0154 |         "view_count": entry.get("view_count"),
0155 |         "published": _format_date(entry.get("upload_date")),
0156 |         "url": entry.get("url") or entry.get("webpage_url") or f"{YOUTUBE_BASE}/watch?v={vid}",
0157 |         "thumbnail": _best_thumbnail(entry),
0158 |     }

0161 | def _extract(url: str, opts: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0162 |     """Run yt-dlp extraction with the given options."""
0163 |     try:
0164 |         with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(opts) as ydl:
0165 |             result = ydl.extract_info(url, download=False)
0166 |     except yt_dlp.utils.DownloadError as exc:
0167 |         msg = str(exc)
0168 |         if "HTTP Error 404" in msg or "not found" in msg.lower():
0169 |             raise YouTubeAgentError("Video/page not found")
0170 |         raise YouTubeAgentError(f"yt-dlp extraction failed: {msg}")
0171 |     except Exception as exc:
0172 |         raise YouTubeAgentError(f"yt-dlp error: {exc}")
0173 |     if result is None:
0174 |         raise YouTubeAgentError("No results returned")
0175 |     return result

0179 |     """Search YouTube and return normalised video entries."""

0182 |     entries = result.get("entries") or []
0183 |     return [_parse_entry(e) for e in entries if e]

0190 |         return url

0377 |     "search_and_play": _action_search_and_play,
0378 |     "open_channel": _action_open_channel,
0379 |     "get_channel_videos": _action_get_channel_videos,
0380 |     "get_trending": _action_get_trending,
0381 |     "open_playlist": _action_open_playlist,
0382 |     "get_playlist_videos": _action_get_playlist_videos,
0383 |     "open_url": _action_open_url,
0384 |     "search_bundle": _action_search_bundle,
0385 | }
0386 | 
0387 | 
0388 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0389 | # Public entry point
0390 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0391 | def execute(request_json: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0392 |     """Execute a YouTube search or playback action.
0393 | 
0394 |     Args:
0395 |         request_json: A dict with ``"action"`` (str) and ``"parameters"`` (dict).
0396 | 
0397 |     Returns:
0398 |         A JSON-compatible dict with ``"status"`` (``"success"`` | ``"error"``),
0399 |         ``"action"``, and either ``"data"`` or ``"message"``.
0400 |     """
0401 |     if isinstance(request_json, str):
0402 |         request_json = request_json.lstrip("﻿")
0403 |         try:
0404 |             request_json = json.loads(request_json)
0405 |         except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0406 |             return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON: {exc}"}
0407 | 
0408 |     if not isinstance(request_json, dict):
0409 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Request must be a JSON object"}
0410 | 
0411 |     action = request_json.get("action", "")
0412 |     if not action or not isinstance(action, str):
0413 |         return {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": "Missing or invalid action field"}
0414 | 
0415 |     if action not in _ACTIONS:
0416 |         return {
0417 |             "status": "error",
0418 |             "action": action,
0419 |             "message": f"Unknown action: {action}. Available: {', '.join(sorted(_ACTIONS))}",
0420 |         }
0421 | 
0422 |     parameters = request_json.get("parameters", {})
0423 |     if not isinstance(parameters, dict):
0424 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": "parameters must be a JSON object"}
0425 | 
0426 |     required = _REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(action, [])
0427 |     for key in required:
0428 |         value = parameters.get(key)
0429 |         if value is None or (isinstance(value, str) and not value.strip()):
0430 |             return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Missing required parameter: {key}"}
0431 | 
0432 |     try:
0433 |         data = _ACTIONS[action](parameters)
0434 |         return {"status": "success", "action": action, "data": data}
0435 |     except YouTubeAgentError as exc:
0436 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": str(exc)}
0437 |     except Exception as exc:
0438 |         return {"status": "error", "action": action, "message": f"Unexpected error: {exc}"}
0439 | 
0440 | 
0441 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0442 | # CLI entry point
0443 | # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
0444 | def _cli_main() -> None:
0445 |     """Handle command-line invocation: file arg, inline JSON arg, or piped stdin."""
0446 |     raw: Optional[str] = None
0447 | 
0448 |     if len(sys.argv) > 1:
0449 |         arg = sys.argv[1]
0450 |         if os.path.isfile(arg):
0451 |             with open(arg, "rb") as fh:
0452 |                 raw = fh.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
0453 |         else:
0454 |             raw = arg
0455 |     elif not sys.stdin.isatty():
0456 |         raw = sys.stdin.buffer.read().decode("utf-8-sig")
0457 |     else:
0458 |         print(
0459 |             "Usage:\n"
0460 |             '  python youtube_agent.py request.json\n'
0461 |             '  python youtube_agent.py \'{"action":"search_videos","parameters":{"query":"Python"}}\'\n'
0462 |             '  echo \'{"action":"search_videos","parameters":{"query":"AI"}}\' '
0463 |             "| python youtube_agent.py",
0464 |             file=sys.stderr,
0465 |         )
0466 |         sys.exit(2)
0467 | 
0468 |     raw = raw.strip().lstrip("﻿")
0469 |     try:
0470 |         request_data = json.loads(raw)
0471 |     except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
0472 |         result = {"status": "error", "action": "unknown", "message": f"Invalid JSON input: {exc}"}
0473 |         print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
0474 |         sys.exit(1)
0475 | 
0476 |     result = execute(request_data)
0477 |     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
0478 |     sys.exit(0 if result.get("status") == "success" else 1)
0479 | 
0480 | 
0481 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0482 |     _cli_main()
0483 | 


================================================================================
Module: brain\agent_loader.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
Dynamic agent loader — imports agent modules from agents/ at runtime.

Agents are loaded on first use and cached. The loader reads file paths from
the agent registry (Phase 0) so no agent names are hardcoded.

Classes:
  - AgentLoader
    Docstring: Thread-safe, lazy-loading agent module cache....

----------------------------------------
Source Code Dump
----------------------------------------
0001 | """Dynamic agent loader — imports agent modules from agents/ at runtime.
0002 | 
0003 | Agents are loaded on first use and cached. The loader reads file paths from
0004 | the agent registry (Phase 0) so no agent names are hardcoded.
0005 | """
0006 | 
0007 | from __future__ import annotations
0008 | 
0009 | import importlib.util
0010 | import sys
0011 | import threading
0012 | from pathlib import Path
0013 | from types import ModuleType
0014 | from typing import Any, Callable, Optional
0015 | 
0016 | from brain.agent_registry_manager import AgentRegistryManager
0017 | from brain.utils.config import AGENTS_DIR
0018 | from brain.utils.logger import log_brain
0019 | 
0020 | 
0021 | class AgentLoader:
0022 |     """Thread-safe, lazy-loading agent module cache."""
0023 | 
0024 |     def __init__(self, registry: AgentRegistryManager) -> None:
0025 |         self._registry = registry
0026 |         self._cache: dict[str, ModuleType] = {}
0027 |         self._lock = threading.Lock()
0028 | 
0029 |     def _import_module(self, agent_name: str) -> ModuleType:
0030 |         """Import an agent .py file by name, using the registry for the filename."""
0031 |         filename = self._registry.get_agent_file(agent_name)
0032 |         if filename is None:
0033 |             raise ImportError(f"Agent '{agent_name}' not found in registry")
0034 | 
0035 |         module_path = AGENTS_DIR / filename
0036 |         if not module_path.is_file():
0037 |             raise ImportError(f"Agent file not found: {module_path}")
0038 | 
0039 |         spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(agent_name, str(module_path))
0040 |         if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
0041 |             raise ImportError(f"Cannot create import spec for {module_path}")
0042 | 
0043 |         module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
0044 |         sys.modules[agent_name] = module
0045 |         spec.loader.exec_module(module)
0046 |         return module
0047 | 
0048 |     def get_module(self, agent_name: str) -> ModuleType:
0049 |         """Return the cached module for *agent_name*, importing on first call."""
0050 |         if agent_name in self._cache:
0051 |             return self._cache[agent_name]
0052 | 
0053 |         with self._lock:
0054 |             if agent_name in self._cache:
0055 |                 return self._cache[agent_name]
0056 | 
0057 |             module = self._import_module(agent_name)
0058 |             self._cache[agent_name] = module
0059 |             log_brain("agent_loaded", agent=agent_name)
0060 |             return module
0061 | 
0062 |     def get_execute_fn(self, agent_name: str) -> Callable[[dict[str, Any]], dict[str, Any]]:
0063 |         """Return the execute() callable for *agent_name*."""
0064 |         module = self.get_module(agent_name)
0065 |         entrypoint = self._registry.get_agent_entrypoint(agent_name)
0066 |         fn = getattr(module, entrypoint, None)
0067 |         if fn is None or not callable(fn):
0068 |             raise AttributeError(
0069 |                 f"Agent '{agent_name}' has no callable '{entrypoint}'"
0070 |             )
0071 |         return fn
0072 | 
0073 |     def preload_all(self) -> dict[str, Optional[str]]:
0074 |         """Import every registered agent up front. Returns {name: error|None}."""
0075 |         results: dict[str, Optional[str]] = {}
0076 |         for agent_name in self._registry.list_agents():
0077 |             try:
0078 |                 self.get_module(agent_name)
0079 |                 results[agent_name] = None
0080 |             except Exception as exc:
0081 |                 results[agent_name] = str(exc)
0082 |                 log_brain("agent_load_failed", agent=agent_name, error=str(exc))
0083 |         return results
0084 | 
0085 |     def is_loaded(self, agent_name: str) -> bool:
0086 |         return agent_name in self._cache
0087 | 
0088 |     def clear_cache(self) -> None:
0089 |         with self._lock:
0090 |             self._cache.clear()
0091 |

Reads and indexes the Phase 0 registry files.

0021 | class AgentRegistryManager:
0022 |     """In-memory index over the Phase 0 registry files."""
0023 | 
0024 |     def __init__(self) -> None:
0025 |         self._agents: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
0026 |         self._actions: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}

0032 | 
0033 |     def load(self) -> None:
0034 |         """Load all registry files into memory."""
0035 |         self._load_agent_registry()
0036 |         self._load_action_registry()
0037 |         self._load_planner_context()
0038 |         self._load_capabilities()

0046 |     def _load_agent_registry(self) -> None:
0047 |         raw = json.loads(AGENT_REGISTRY_PATH.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
0048 |         for agent in raw.get("agents", []):
0049 |             name = agent["name"]
0050 |             self._agents[name] = agent
0051 |             action_names: set[str] = set()
0052 |             params_map: dict[str, list[str]] = {}
0053 |             for action in agent.get("actions", []):
0054 |                 action_names.add(action["name"])
0055 |                 params_map[action["name"]] = action.get("required_params", [])
0056 |             self._agent_actions[name] = action_names
0057 |             self._required_params[name] = params_map
0058 | 
0059 |     def _load_action_registry(self) -> None:
0060 |         raw = json.loads(ACTION_REGISTRY_PATH.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
0061 |         for action in raw.get("actions", []):
0062 |             key = f"{action['agent']}.{action['action']}"
0063 |             self._actions[key] = action
0064 | 
0065 |     def _load_planner_context(self) -> None:
0066 |         self._planner_context = json.loads(
0067 |             PLANNER_CONTEXT_PATH.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
0068 |         )
0069 | 
0070 |     def _load_capabilities(self) -> None:

0072 |             CAPABILITIES_PATH.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
0073 |         )
0074 | 
0075 |     def reload(self) -> None:

0077 |         self._agents.clear()
0078 |         self._actions.clear()
0079 |         self._agent_actions.clear()
0080 |         self._required_params.clear()
0081 |         self.load()

0085 |     def agent_exists(self, agent_name: str) -> bool:
0086 |         return agent_name in self._agents
0087 | 
0088 |     def action_exists(self, agent_name: str, action_name: str) -> bool:
0089 |         return action_name in self._agent_actions.get(agent_name, set())
0090 | 
0091 |     def get_required_params(self, agent_name: str, action_name: str) -> list[str]:
0092 |         return self._required_params.get(agent_name, {}).get(action_name, [])
0093 | 
0094 |     def get_agent_info(self, agent_name: str) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
0095 |         return self._agents.get(agent_name)
0096 | 
0097 |     def get_agent_file(self, agent_name: str) -> Optional[str]:
0098 |         info = self._agents.get(agent_name)
0099 |         return info["file"] if info else None
0100 | 
0101 |     def get_agent_entrypoint(self, agent_name: str) -> str:
0102 |         info = self._agents.get(agent_name)
0103 |         return info.get("entrypoint", "execute") if info else "execute"
0104 | 
0105 |     def list_agents(self) -> list[str]:
0106 |         return list(self._agents.keys())
0107 | 
0108 |     def list_actions(self, agent_name: str) -> list[str]:
0109 |         return sorted(self._agent_actions.get(agent_name, set()))

0111 |     def get_planner_context(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
0112 |         return self._planner_context

0114 |     def get_planner_context_compact(self) -> str:
0115 |         """Return a compact JSON string for embedding in the planner prompt."""
0116 |         agents = self._planner_context.get("agents", [])
0117 |         compact: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0118 |         for agent in agents:
0119 |             entry: dict[str, Any] = {
0120 |                 "agent": agent["agent"],
0121 |                 "purpose": agent.get("purpose", ""),
0122 |                 "keywords": agent.get("keywords", []),
0123 |                 "actions": [],
0124 |             }
0125 |             for action in agent.get("actions", []):
0126 |                 a: dict[str, Any] = {"name": action["name"]}
0127 |                 if action.get("required_params"):
0128 |                     a["required_params"] = action["required_params"]
0129 |                 if action.get("optional_params"):
0130 |                     a["optional_params"] = action["optional_params"]
0131 |                 entry["actions"].append(a)
0132 |             compact.append(entry)
0133 |         return json.dumps(compact, ensure_ascii=False)
0134 | 
0135 |     def validate_task(
0136 |         self, agent_name: str, action_name: str, parameters: dict[str, Any]
0137 |     ) -> list[str]:
0138 |         """Return a list of validation errors (empty = valid)."""
0139 |         errors: list[str] = []
0140 | 
0141 |         if not self.agent_exists(agent_name):
0142 |             errors.append(f"Unknown agent: {agent_name}")
0143 |             return errors
0144 | 
0145 |         if not self.action_exists(agent_name, action_name):
0146 |             errors.append(
0147 |                 f"Unknown action '{action_name}' for agent '{agent_name}'"
0148 |             )
0149 |             return errors
0150 | 
0151 |         required = self.get_required_params(agent_name, action_name)
0152 |         for param in required:
0153 |             if param not in parameters:
0154 |                 errors.append(
0155 |                     f"Missing required parameter '{param}' for "

0157 |                 )
0158 | 
0159 |         return errors

================================================================================
Module: brain\brain.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
Brain — the central orchestrator of the MAYA AI assistant.

Flow:
    command  →  Memory(context)  →  Planner  →  WorkQueue  →  Executor
            →  Memory(record)   →  ResponseGenerator  →  text

Usage:
    from brain import Brain

    brain = Brain()
    response = brain.process("Check my unread emails")

Classes:
  - Brain
    Docstring: Top-level MAYA Brain. Call :meth:`process` with a user command....

0001 | """Brain — the central orchestrator of the MAYA AI assistant.
0002 | 
0003 | Flow:
0004 |     command  →  Memory(context)  →  Planner  →  WorkQueue  →  Executor
0005 |             →  Memory(record)   →  ResponseGenerator  →  text
0006 | 
0007 | Usage:
0008 |     from brain import Brain
0009 | 
0010 |     brain = Brain()
0011 |     response = brain.process("Check my unread emails")
0012 | """

0047 |         self._planner = Planner(self._registry)

0063 |

0065 |             load_results = self._loader.preload_all()
0066 |             loaded = sum(1 for v in load_results.values() if v is None)
0067 |             failed = sum(1 for v in load_results.values() if v is not None)
0068 |             log_brain("agents_preloaded", loaded=loaded, failed=failed)
0069 | 
0070 |         log_brain(
0071 |             "brain_initialized",

0075 |             max_retries=max_retries,
0076 |             memory_enabled=enable_memory,
0077 |         )
