0079 |     def process(
0080 |         self,
0081 |         command: str,
0082 |         conversation_context: Optional[str] = None,
0083 |     ) -> str:
0084 |         """Process a user voice command end-to-end and return a spoken response.
0085 | 
0086 |         This is the single entry point the voice layer calls.
0087 |         """
0088 |         request_start = time.perf_counter()
0089 |         log_brain("request_start", command=command)
0090 | 
0091 |         try:
0092 |             # Record user message and build memory context
0093 |             if self._memory:
0094 |                 self._memory.add_user_message(command)
0095 |                 if conversation_context is None:
0096 |                     conversation_context = self._memory.get_context_for_planner(command)
0097 | 
0098 |             plan = self._planner.plan(command, conversation_context)
0099 | 
0100 |             if not plan.requires_agents:
0101 |                 response = self._response_gen.generate_direct(
0102 |                     command, plan.direct_response, conversation_context
0103 |                 )
0104 |                 duration_ms = (time.perf_counter() - request_start) * 1000
0105 | 
0106 |                 if self._memory:
0107 |                     self._memory.add_assistant_message(response)
0108 |                     self._memory.record_planner_execution(
0109 |                         command, plan.model_dump(), [], response, duration_ms,
0110 |                     )
0111 |                     self._memory.save_state()
0112 | 
0113 |                 log_brain(
0114 |                     "request_complete",
0115 |                     path="direct",
0116 |                     duration_ms=round(duration_ms, 2),
0117 |                 )
0118 |                 return response
0119 | 
0120 |             queue = WorkQueue()
0121 |             results = self._executor.execute_plan(plan, queue)
0122 | 
0123 |             # Record agent executions in memory
0124 |             if self._memory:
0125 |                 for r in results:
0126 |                     summary = ""
0127 |                     if r.output and isinstance(r.output, dict):
0128 |                         summary = r.output.get("message", str(r.output)[:200])
0129 |                     self._memory.record_agent_execution(
0130 |                         agent=r.agent,
0131 |                         action=r.action,
0132 |                         parameters={},
0133 |                         status=r.status.value,
0134 |                         result_summary=summary,
0135 |                         duration_ms=r.duration_ms,
0136 |                     )
0137 | 
0138 |             response = self._response_gen.generate(
0139 |                 command, results, conversation_context
0140 |             )
0141 | 
0142 |             duration_ms = (time.perf_counter() - request_start) * 1000
0143 | 
0144 |             if self._memory:
0145 |                 self._memory.add_assistant_message(response)
0146 |                 self._memory.record_planner_execution(
0147 |                     command,
0148 |                     plan.model_dump(),
0149 |                     [r.model_dump() for r in results],
0150 |                     response,
0151 |                     duration_ms,
0152 |                 )
0153 |                 self._memory.save_state()
0154 | 
0155 |             log_brain(
0156 |                 "request_complete",
0157 |                 path="agent",
0158 |                 task_count=len(results),
0159 |                 summary=queue.get_status_summary(),
0160 |                 duration_ms=round(duration_ms, 2),
0161 |             )
0162 |             return response
0163 | 
0164 |         except Exception as exc:
0165 |             duration_ms = (time.perf_counter() - request_start) * 1000
0166 |             log_brain(
0167 |                 "request_error",
0168 |                 command=command,
0169 |                 error=str(exc),
0170 |                 traceback=traceback.format_exc(),
0171 |                 duration_ms=round(duration_ms, 2),
0172 |             )
0173 |             return (
0174 |                 "I ran into a problem processing your request. "
0175 |                 "Could you try again?"
0176 |             )
0177 | 
0178 |     def process_raw(
0179 |         self,
0180 |         command: str,
0181 |         conversation_context: Optional[str] = None,
0182 |     ) -> dict[str, Any]:
0183 |         """Process a command and return structured output (for debugging/tests).
0184 | 
0185 |         Returns a dict with plan, results, response, and timing.
0186 |         """
0187 |         request_start = time.perf_counter()
0188 | 
0189 |         try:
0190 |             if self._memory:
0191 |                 self._memory.add_user_message(command)
0192 |                 if conversation_context is None:
0193 |                     conversation_context = self._memory.get_context_for_planner(command)
0194 | 
0195 |             plan = self._planner.plan(command, conversation_context)
0196 | 
0197 |             if not plan.requires_agents:
0198 |                 response = self._response_gen.generate_direct(
0199 |                     command, plan.direct_response, conversation_context
0200 |                 )
0201 |                 if self._memory:
0202 |                     self._memory.add_assistant_message(response)
0203 |                 return {
0204 |                     "status": "success",
0205 |                     "path": "direct",
0206 |                     "plan": plan.model_dump(),
0207 |                     "results": [],
0208 |                     "response": response,
0209 |                     "duration_ms": round(
0210 |                         (time.perf_counter() - request_start) * 1000, 2
0211 |                     ),

Module Docstring:
Agent executor — runs tasks with timeouts, retries, and result capture.

Supports both parallel (ThreadPoolExecutor) and sequential execution.
Each task is isolated: a failure never crashes the executor.

0065 |     def _run_sequential(self, queue: WorkQueue) -> None:
0066 |         """Execute tasks one at a time, respecting dependency order.
0067 | 
0068 |         Uses a single-thread pool to enforce per-task timeouts without
0069 |         spawning a new pool per call.
0070 |         """
0071 |         with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as timeout_pool:
0072 |             while not queue.is_complete():
0073 |                 ready = queue.get_ready_tasks()

0075 |                     if queue.has_blocked_tasks():
0076 |                         log_brain("deadlock_detected")
0077 |                     break

0079 |                 for task in ready:
0080 |                     result = self._execute_single(task, queue, timeout_pool)
0081 |                     if result.status == TaskStatus.COMPLETED:
0082 |                         queue.mark_completed(task.id, result)
0083 |                     else:
0084 |                         queue.mark_failed(task.id, result)

0086 |     def _run_parallel(self, queue: WorkQueue) -> None:
0087 |         """Execute independent tasks concurrently via ThreadPoolExecutor."""
0088 |         with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=self._max_workers) as pool:
0089 |             while not queue.is_complete():
0090 |                 ready = queue.get_ready_tasks()
0091 |                 if not ready:
0092 |                     if queue.has_blocked_tasks():
0093 |                         log_brain("deadlock_detected")
0094 |                     break

0097 |                 for task in ready:
0098 |                     future = pool.submit(self._execute_single, task, queue, None)
0099 |                     futures[future] = task
0100 | 
0101 |                 for future in as_completed(futures):
0102 |                     task = futures[future]
0103 |                     try:
0104 |                         result = future.result(timeout=self._task_timeout + 5)
0105 |                     except Exception as exc:
0106 |                         result = TaskResult(
0107 |                             task_id=task.id,

================================================================================
Module: brain\planner.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
LLM-based planner — converts user commands into validated execution plans.

Flow:
    1. Build a prompt with the user command + registry context.
    2. Call the planner LLM (Ollama).
    3. Parse and validate the JSON plan via Pydantic.
    4. Validate agents/actions/params against the registry.
    5. On failure: retry (up to PLANNER_MAX_RETRIES), then local fallback.

Classes:
  - Planner
    Docstring: Converts user commands into validated ExecutionPlans....

Functions:
  - _build_prompt
    Docstring: Assemble the user-facing prompt sent to the planner LLM....
  - _extract_json
    Docstring: Pull a JSON object from LLM output that may include markdown fences....
  - _call_ollama
    Docstring: Send a chat request to Ollama and return the assistant content....

0002 | 
0003 | Flow:
0004 |     1. Build a prompt with the user command + registry context.
0005 |     2. Call the planner LLM (Ollama).
0006 |     3. Parse and validate the JSON plan via Pydantic.
0007 |     4. Validate agents/actions/params against the registry.
0008 |     5. On failure: retry (up to PLANNER_MAX_RETRIES), then local fallback.
0009 | """

0034 | _SYSTEM_PROMPT = textwrap.dedent("""\
0035 | You are the MAYA AI planner. Your job is to convert a user command into a
0036 | JSON execution plan.
0037 | 
0038 | RULES — follow exactly:
0039 | 1. Output ONLY valid JSON. No markdown fences, no explanation, no commentary.
0040 | 2. If the command can be answered without any agent (greetings, general
0041 |    knowledge, opinions, conversation), return:
0042 |    {"requires_agents": false, "tasks": [], "direct_response": "<your answer>"}
0043 | 3. If agents are needed, return:
0044 |    {"requires_agents": true, "parallel": <true|false>, "tasks": [...]}
0045 | 4. Each task must have: "id", "agent", "action", "parameters".
0046 | 5. Use ONLY agents and actions from the AGENT REGISTRY below.
0047 | 6. If a task depends on another task's output, add "depends_on": ["task_id"].
0048 | 7. Set "parallel": true only when tasks are independent.
0049 | 8. Task IDs must be unique strings like "task_1", "task_2", etc.
0050 | 9. Parameters must satisfy the required_params for each action.
0051 | 10. Do NOT invent agents or actions that are not in the registry.
0052 | """)

0055 | def _build_prompt(
0056 |     command: str,
0057 |     registry_context: str,
0058 |     conversation_context: Optional[str] = None,
0059 | ) -> str:
0060 |     """Assemble the user-facing prompt sent to the planner LLM."""
0061 |     parts: list[str] = []
0062 | 
0063 |     parts.append("AGENT REGISTRY:\n")
0064 |     parts.append(registry_context)
0065 |     parts.append("\n")
0066 | 
0067 |     if conversation_context:
0068 |         parts.append("RECENT CONVERSATION:\n")
0069 |         parts.append(conversation_context)
0070 |         parts.append("\n")
0071 |

0073 |     parts.append("Respond with JSON only.")

0078 | def _extract_json(raw: str) -> str:
0079 |     """Pull a JSON object from LLM output that may include markdown fences."""
0080 |     raw = raw.strip()
0081 | 
0082 |     fence = re.search(r"```(?:json)?\s*\n?(.*?)```", raw, re.DOTALL)
0083 |     if fence:
0084 |         raw = fence.group(1).strip()
0085 | 
0086 |     start = raw.find("{")
0087 |     if start == -1:
0088 |         return raw
0089 | 
0090 |     decoder = json.JSONDecoder()
0091 |     try:
0092 |         _, end_idx = decoder.raw_decode(raw, start)
0093 |         return raw[start:end_idx]
0094 |     except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
0095 |         pass
0096 | 
0097 |     depth = 0
0098 |     end = start
0099 |     for i in range(start, len(raw)):
0100 |         if raw[i] == "{":
0101 |             depth += 1
0102 |         elif raw[i] == "}":
0103 |             depth -= 1
0104 |             if depth == 0:
0105 |                 end = i + 1
0106 |                 break
0107 |     return raw[start:end]
0108 |

0118 | 
0119 |     Requests JSON format from Ollama so the model is constrained to
0120 |     produce valid JSON, reducing parse failures with smaller models.
0121 |     """
0122 |     client = ollama.Client(host=OLLAMA_BASE_URL)
0123 |     response = client.chat(
0124 |         model=model,
0125 |         messages=[
0126 |             {"role": "system", "content": _SYSTEM_PROMPT},
0127 |             {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
0128 |         ],
0129 |         format="json",
0130 |         options={"temperature": temperature, "num_ctx": num_ctx},
0131 |     )
0132 |     return response.message.content or ""

Module: brain\queue_manager.py

Module Docstring:
Work queue with dependency resolution and state tracking.

Manages task lifecycle: PENDING → RUNNING → COMPLETED/FAILED/CANCELLED.
Resolves inter-task dependencies before yielding ready tasks.

Classes:
  - WorkQueue
    Docstring: Thread-safe work queue with dependency-aware scheduling....

----------------------------------------
Source Code Dump
----------------------------------------
0001 | """Work queue with dependency resolution and state tracking.
0002 | 
0003 | Manages task lifecycle: PENDING → RUNNING → COMPLETED/FAILED/CANCELLED.
0004 | Resolves inter-task dependencies before yielding ready tasks.
0005 | """
0006 | 
0007 | from __future__ import annotations
0008 | 
0009 | import threading
0010 | from typing import Any, Optional
0011 | 
0012 | from brain.schemas.plan_schema import (
0013 |     ExecutionPlan,
0014 |     PlanTask,
0015 |     TaskResult,
0016 |     TaskStatus,
0017 | )
0018 | from brain.utils.logger import log_brain
0019 | 
0020 | 
0021 | class WorkQueue:
0022 |     """Thread-safe work queue with dependency-aware scheduling."""
0023 | 
0024 |     def __init__(self) -> None:
0025 |         self._tasks: dict[str, PlanTask] = {}
0026 |         self._status: dict[str, TaskStatus] = {}
0027 |         self._results: dict[str, TaskResult] = {}
0028 |         self._lock = threading.Lock()
0029 | 
0030 |     def load_plan(self, plan: ExecutionPlan) -> None:
0031 |         """Populate the queue from an execution plan."""
0032 |         with self._lock:
0033 |             self._tasks.clear()
0034 |             self._status.clear()
0035 |             self._results.clear()
0036 |             for task in plan.tasks:
0037 |                 self._tasks[task.id] = task
0038 |                 self._status[task.id] = TaskStatus.PENDING
0039 | 
0040 |         log_brain("queue_loaded", task_count=len(plan.tasks))
0041 | 
0042 |     def get_ready_tasks(self) -> list[PlanTask]:
0043 |         """Return all PENDING tasks whose dependencies are COMPLETED."""
0044 |         with self._lock:
0045 |             return self._get_ready_tasks_unlocked()
0046 | 
0047 |     def _get_ready_tasks_unlocked(self) -> list[PlanTask]:
0048 |         ready: list[PlanTask] = []
0049 |         for task_id, task in self._tasks.items():
0050 |             if self._status[task_id] != TaskStatus.PENDING:
0051 |                 continue
0052 |             deps_met = all(
0053 |                 self._status.get(dep) == TaskStatus.COMPLETED
0054 |                 for dep in task.depends_on
0055 |             )
0056 |             if deps_met:
0057 |                 ready.append(task)
0058 |         return ready
0059 | 
0060 |     def mark_running(self, task_id: str) -> None:
0061 |         with self._lock:
0062 |             self._status[task_id] = TaskStatus.RUNNING
0063 | 
0064 |     def mark_completed(self, task_id: str, result: TaskResult) -> None:
0065 |         with self._lock:
0066 |             self._status[task_id] = TaskStatus.COMPLETED
0067 |             self._results[task_id] = result
0068 | 
0069 |     def mark_failed(self, task_id: str, result: TaskResult) -> None:
0070 |         with self._lock:
0071 |             self._status[task_id] = TaskStatus.FAILED
0072 |             self._results[task_id] = result
0073 |             self._cancel_dependents(task_id)
0074 | 
0075 |     def _cancel_dependents(self, failed_id: str) -> None:
0076 |         """Cancel all tasks that transitively depend on a failed task."""
0077 |         for task_id, task in self._tasks.items():
0078 |             if self._status[task_id] != TaskStatus.PENDING:
0079 |                 continue
0080 |             if failed_id in task.depends_on:
0081 |                 self._status[task_id] = TaskStatus.CANCELLED
0082 |                 self._results[task_id] = TaskResult(
0083 |                     task_id=task_id,
0084 |                     agent=task.agent,
0085 |                     action=task.action,
0086 |                     status=TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
0087 |                     error=f"Cancelled: dependency '{failed_id}' failed",
0088 |                 )
0089 |                 log_brain("task_cancelled", task_id=task_id, reason=failed_id)
0090 |                 self._cancel_dependents(task_id)
0091 | 
0092 |     def is_complete(self) -> bool:
0093 |         """True when no tasks are PENDING or RUNNING."""
0094 |         with self._lock:
0095 |             return all(
0096 |                 s in (TaskStatus.COMPLETED, TaskStatus.FAILED, TaskStatus.CANCELLED)
0097 |                 for s in self._status.values()
0098 |             )
0099 | 
0100 |     def has_blocked_tasks(self) -> bool:
0101 |         """True when there are PENDING tasks but none are ready (deadlock)."""
0102 |         with self._lock:
0103 |             has_pending = any(
0104 |                 s == TaskStatus.PENDING for s in self._status.values()
0105 |             )
0106 |             if not has_pending:
0107 |                 return False
0108 |             ready = self._get_ready_tasks_unlocked()
0109 |             return len(ready) == 0
0110 | 
0111 |     def get_all_results(self) -> list[TaskResult]:
0112 |         with self._lock:
0113 |             return list(self._results.values())
0114 | 
0115 |     def get_result(self, task_id: str) -> Optional[TaskResult]:
0116 |         with self._lock:
0117 |             return self._results.get(task_id)
0118 | 
0119 |     def get_status_summary(self) -> dict[str, int]:
0120 |         with self._lock:
0121 |             summary: dict[str, int] = {}
0122 |             for status in self._status.values():
0123 |                 summary[status.value] = summary.get(status.value, 0) + 1
0124 |             return summary
0125 | 
0126 |     @property
0127 |     def task_count(self) -> int:
0128 |         return len(self._tasks)
0129 |

Module Docstring:
Response generator — converts task results into natural conversation.

Uses the large response model (gpt-oss:120b) with cloud-first + local fallback.
For the no-agent path, passes through the planner's direct_response.

Classes:
  - ResponseGenerator
    Docstring: Generates natural-language responses from task results....

Functions:
  - _build_prompt
    Docstring: Assemble the prompt for the response generator LLM....

0001 | """Response generator — converts task results into natural conversation.
0002 | 
0003 | Uses the large response model (gpt-oss:120b) with cloud-first + local fallback.
0004 | For the no-agent path, passes through the planner's direct_response.
0005 | """
0006 | 
0007 | from __future__ import annotations
0008 | 
0009 | import json
0010 | import textwrap
0011 | import traceback
0012 | from typing import Any, Optional
0013 | 
0014 | import ollama
0015 | 
0016 | from brain.schemas.plan_schema import TaskResult, TaskStatus
0017 | from brain.utils.config import (
0018 |     OLLAMA_BASE_URL,
0019 |     RESPONSE_LOCAL_FALLBACK,
0020 |     RESPONSE_MAX_RETRIES,
0021 |     RESPONSE_MODEL,
0022 |     RESPONSE_NUM_CTX,
0023 |     RESPONSE_TEMPERATURE,
0024 | )
0025 | from brain.utils.logger import log_brain
0026 | 
0027 | 
0028 | import os
0029 | _PERSONA = os.getenv("MAYA_PERSONA", "helpful, professional, and friendly")
0030 | 
0031 | _SYSTEM_PROMPT = textwrap.dedent(f"""\
0032 | You are MAYA, an AI voice assistant. Your personality is: {_PERSONA}
0033 | Always stay strictly in character and adjust your tone and vocabulary to match.
0034 | 
0035 | You are responding to a user who spoke a voice command. Your response will be
0036 | read aloud via text-to-speech.
0037 | 
0038 | RULES:
0039 | 1. Be concise but informative — this is spoken output, not a document.
0040 | 2. Summarise data naturally; do not dump raw JSON.
0041 | 3. If some tasks failed, mention it briefly and focus on what succeeded.
0042 | 4. Use a warm, conversational tone.
0043 | 5. Do NOT use markdown formatting, bullet lists, or code blocks.
0044 | 6. Do NOT mention internal details (task IDs, agent names, JSON).
0045 | 7. If there are no results, say so honestly.
0046 | 8. Keep your response under 200 words unless the data warrants more.
0047 | """)
0048 | 
0049 | 
0050 | def _build_prompt(
0051 |     command: str,
0052 |     results: list[TaskResult],
0053 |     conversation_context: Optional[str] = None,
0054 | ) -> str:
0055 |     """Assemble the prompt for the response generator LLM."""
0056 |     parts: list[str] = []
0057 | 
0058 |     if conversation_context:
0059 |         parts.append(f"RECENT CONVERSATION:\n{conversation_context}\n")
0060 | 
0061 |     parts.append(f"USER SAID: {command}\n")
0062 | 
0063 |     if results:
0064 |         parts.append("TASK RESULTS:\n")
0065 |         for r in results:
0066 |             entry: dict[str, Any] = {
0067 |                 "agent": r.agent,
0068 |                 "action": r.action,
0069 |                 "status": r.status.value,
0070 |             }
0071 |             if r.status == TaskStatus.COMPLETED and r.output is not None:
0072 |                 output = r.output
0073 |                 output_str = json.dumps(output, ensure_ascii=False, default=str)
0074 |                 if len(output_str) > 4000:
0075 |                     output_str = output_str[:4000] + "... [truncated]"
0076 |                 entry["output"] = output_str
0077 |             elif r.error:
0078 |                 entry["error"] = r.error
0079 |             parts.append(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
0080 |             parts.append("\n")
0081 | 
0082 |     parts.append(
0083 |         "\nGenerate a natural, spoken response for MAYA to say aloud."
0084 |     )
0085 |     return "\n".join(parts)
0086 | 
0087 | 
0088 | def _call_ollama(
0089 |     prompt: str,
0090 |     model: str,
0091 |     *,
0092 |     temperature: float = RESPONSE_TEMPERATURE,
0093 |     num_ctx: int = RESPONSE_NUM_CTX,
0094 | ) -> str:
0095 |     client = ollama.Client(host=OLLAMA_BASE_URL)
0096 |     response = client.chat(
0097 |         model=model,
0098 |         messages=[
0099 |             {"role": "system", "content": _SYSTEM_PROMPT},
0100 |             {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
0101 |         ],
0102 |         options={"temperature": temperature, "num_ctx": num_ctx},
0103 |     )
0104 |     return response.message.content or ""
0105 | 
0106 | 
0107 | class ResponseGenerator:
0108 |     """Generates natural-language responses from task results."""
0109 | 
0110 |     def generate(
0111 |         self,
0112 |         command: str,
0113 |         results: list[TaskResult],
0114 |         conversation_context: Optional[str] = None,
0115 |     ) -> str:
0116 |         """Build a spoken response for the user.
0117 | 
0118 |         Tries the primary response model, then falls back to local.
0119 |         """
0120 |         prompt = _build_prompt(command, results, conversation_context)
0121 | 
0122 |         log_brain("response_start", model=RESPONSE_MODEL, command=command)
0123 | 
0124 |         response = self._try_model(RESPONSE_MODEL, prompt)
0125 |         if response is not None:
0126 |             return response
0127 | 
0128 |         if RESPONSE_LOCAL_FALLBACK != RESPONSE_MODEL:
0129 |             log_brain("response_fallback", model=RESPONSE_LOCAL_FALLBACK)
0130 |             response = self._try_model(RESPONSE_LOCAL_FALLBACK, prompt)
0131 |             if response is not None:
0132 |                 return response
0133 | 
0134 |         log_brain("response_all_failed")
0135 |         return self._build_fallback_response(results)
0136 | 
0137 |     def generate_direct(
0138 |         self,
0139 |         command: str,
0140 |         direct_response: Optional[str] = None,
0141 |         conversation_context: Optional[str] = None,
0142 |     ) -> str:
0143 |         """Handle the no-agent path. If the planner supplied a direct_response,
0144 |         use it. Otherwise, run the response model on the command alone."""
0145 |         if direct_response:
0146 |             return direct_response
0147 | 
0148 |         prompt_parts: list[str] = []
0149 |         if conversation_context:
0150 |             prompt_parts.append(f"RECENT CONVERSATION:\n{conversation_context}\n")
0151 |         prompt_parts.append(f"USER SAID: {command}\n")
0152 |         prompt_parts.append("Respond naturally as MAYA, a helpful AI assistant.")
0153 | 
0154 |         prompt = "\n".join(prompt_parts)
0155 | 
0156 |         log_brain("direct_response_start", model=RESPONSE_MODEL)
0157 | 
0158 |         response = self._try_model(RESPONSE_MODEL, prompt)
0159 |         if response is not None:
0160 |             return response
0161 | 
0162 |         if RESPONSE_LOCAL_FALLBACK != RESPONSE_MODEL:
0163 |             response = self._try_model(RESPONSE_LOCAL_FALLBACK, prompt)
0164 |             if response is not None:
0165 |                 return response
0166 | 
0167 |         return direct_response or "I'm here, but I'm having trouble responding right now."
0168 | 
0169 |     def _try_model(self, model: str, prompt: str) -> Optional[str]:
0170 |         """Attempt generation with *model*, returning None on exhausted retries."""
0171 |         for attempt in range(RESPONSE_MAX_RETRIES + 1):
0172 |             try:
0173 |                 text = _call_ollama(prompt, model)
0174 |                 if text.strip():
0175 |                     log_brain(
0176 |                         "response_success",
0177 |                         model=model,
0178 |                         attempt=attempt,
0179 |                         length=len(text),
0180 |                     )
0181 |                     return text.strip()
0182 |             except Exception as exc:
0183 |                 log_brain(
0184 |                     "response_attempt_failed",
0185 |                     model=model,
0186 |                     attempt=attempt,
0187 |                     error=str(exc),
0188 |                     traceback=traceback.format_exc(),
0189 |                 )
0190 |         return None
0191 | 
0192 |     def _build_fallback_response(self, results: list[TaskResult]) -> str:
0193 |         """Deterministic fallback when all LLM attempts fail."""
0194 |         completed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.COMPLETED]
0195 |         failed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.FAILED]
0196 | 
0197 |         if not completed and not failed:
0198 |             return "I processed your request but have no results to share."
0199 | 
0200 |         parts: list[str] = []
0201 |         if completed:
0202 |             parts.append(
0203 |                 f"I completed {len(completed)} "
0204 |                 f"{'task' if len(completed) == 1 else 'tasks'} successfully."
0205 |             )
0206 |         if failed:
0207 |             parts.append(
0208 |                 f"{len(failed)} {'task' if len(failed) == 1 else 'tasks'} failed."
0209 |             )
0210 |         return " ".join(parts)
0211 |

Source Code Dump
----------------------------------------
0001 | """Pydantic models for execution plans and task results."""
0002 | 
0003 | from __future__ import annotations
0004 | 
0005 | from enum import Enum
0006 | from typing import Any, Optional
0007 | 
0008 | from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, model_validator
0009 | 
0010 | 
0011 | class TaskStatus(str, Enum):
0012 |     PENDING = "pending"
0013 |     RUNNING = "running"
0014 |     COMPLETED = "completed"
0015 |     FAILED = "failed"
0016 |     CANCELLED = "cancelled"
0017 | 
0018 | 
0019 | class PlanTask(BaseModel):
0020 |     """A single task within an execution plan."""
0021 | 
0022 |     id: str = Field(..., min_length=1)
0023 |     agent: str = Field(..., min_length=1)
0024 |     action: str = Field(..., min_length=1)
0025 |     parameters: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
0026 |     depends_on: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
0027 | 
0028 | 
0029 | class ExecutionPlan(BaseModel):
0030 |     """The full plan output by the planner LLM."""
0031 | 
0032 |     requires_agents: bool = True
0033 |     parallel: bool = False
0034 |     tasks: list[PlanTask] = Field(default_factory=list)
0035 |     direct_response: Optional[str] = None
0036 | 
0037 |     @model_validator(mode="after")
0038 |     def _validate_plan(self) -> "ExecutionPlan":
0039 |         if self.requires_agents and not self.tasks:
0040 |             raise ValueError("requires_agents=true but no tasks provided")
0041 | 
0042 |         task_ids = {t.id for t in self.tasks}
0043 |         for task in self.tasks:
0044 |             for dep in task.depends_on:
0045 |                 if dep not in task_ids:
0046 |                     raise ValueError(
0047 |                         f"Task '{task.id}' depends on unknown task '{dep}'"
0048 |                     )
0049 |             if task.id in task.depends_on:
0050 |                 raise ValueError(f"Task '{task.id}' depends on itself")
0051 | 
0052 |         return self
0053 | 
0054 | 
0055 | class TaskResult(BaseModel):
0056 |     """Result of executing a single task."""
0057 | 
0058 |     task_id: str
0059 |     agent: str
0060 |     action: str
0061 |     status: TaskStatus
0062 |     output: Any = None
0063 |     error: Optional[str] = None
0064 |     duration_ms: float = 0.0
0065 |     retries_used: int = 0
0066 |

0022 | def _ensure_logs_dir() -> None:
0023 |     LOGS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
0024 | 
0025 | 
0026 | def _append(filename: str, record: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
0027 |     """Append a single JSON record to a .jsonl file (thread-safe)."""
0028 |     _ensure_logs_dir()
0029 |     record["timestamp"] = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc).isoformat()
0030 |     line = json.dumps(record, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) + "\n"
0031 |     with _lock:
0032 |         with open(LOGS_DIR / filename, "a", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
0033 |             fh.write(line)
0034 | 
0035 | 
0036 | def log_brain(event: str, **kwargs: Any) -> None:
0037 |     """Log a brain-level event."""
0038 |     _append("brain.jsonl", {"event": event, **kwargs})
0039 | 
0040 | 
0041 | def log_planner(event: str, **kwargs: Any) -> None:
0042 |     """Log a planner-level event."""
0043 |     _append("planner.jsonl", {"event": event, **kwargs})

0020 | 
0021 |     def _get_file(self) -> Path:
0022 |         if self._file is None:
0023 |             ensure_dirs()
0024 |             month = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m")
0025 |             self._file = AGENT_HISTORY_DIR / f"agent_history_{month}.jsonl"
0026 |         return self._file
0027 | 
0028 |     def record(
0029 |         self,
0030 |         agent: str,
0031 |         action: str,
0032 |         parameters: dict[str, Any],
0033 |         status: str = "success",
0034 |         result_summary: str = "",
0035 |         duration_ms: float = 0.0,
0036 |         chat_id: Optional[str] = None,
0037 |     ) -> None:
0038 |         entry = AgentHistoryEntry(
0039 |             agent=agent,
0040 |             action=action,
0041 |             parameters=parameters,
0042 |             status=status,
0043 |             result_summary=result_summary,
0044 |             duration_ms=duration_ms,
0045 |             chat_id=chat_id,
0046 |         )
0047 |         self._recent.append(entry)
0048 |         if len(self._recent) > AGENT_HISTORY_LIMIT * 2:
0049 |             self._recent = self._recent[-AGENT_HISTORY_LIMIT:]
0050 | 
0051 |         line = json.dumps(entry.model_dump(mode="json"), ensure_ascii=False, default=str)
0052 |         path = self._get_file()
0053 |         with open(path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
0054 |             fh.write(line + "\n")
0055 | 
0056 |     def get_recent(self, limit: int = AGENT_HISTORY_LIMIT) -> list[AgentHistoryEntry]:
0057 |         return list(self._recent[-limit:])
0058 | 
0059 |     def get_by_agent(self, agent: str, limit: int = 10) -> list[AgentHistoryEntry]:
0060 |         return [e for e in reversed(self._recent) if e.agent == agent][:limit]
0061 | 
0062 |     def get_recent_as_text(self, limit: int = 10) -> str:
0063 |         entries = self.get_recent(limit)
0064 |         lines: list[str] = []
0065 |         for e in entries:
0066 |             lines.append(
0067 |                 f"[{e.timestamp.strftime('%H:%M')}] {e.agent}.{e.action} → {e.status}"
0068 |             )
0069 |             if e.result_summary:
0070 |                 lines.append(f"  {e.result_summary[:100]}")
0071 |         return "\n".join(lines)
0072 | 
0073 |     def load_recent_from_disk(self, limit: int = AGENT_HISTORY_LIMIT) -> None:
0074 |         """Load recent entries from the current month's file."""
0075 |         path = self._get_file()
0076 |         if not path.exists():
0077 |             return
0078 |         lines = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip().split("\n")
0079 |         entries: list[AgentHistoryEntry] = []
0080 |         for line in lines[-limit:]:
0081 |             if line.strip():
0082 |                 try:
0083 |                     data = json.loads(line)
0084 |                     entries.append(AgentHistoryEntry.model_validate(data))
0085 |                 except Exception:
0086 |                     continue
0087 |         self._recent = entries
0088 | 
0089 |     def get_stats(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
0090 |         agents: dict[str, int] = {}
0091 |         for e in self._recent:
0092 |             agents[e.agent] = agents.get(e.agent, 0) + 1
0093 |         return {
0094 |             "total_recent": len(self._recent),
0095 |             "agents": agents,
0096 |         }

0035 |         )

0037 |     def rotate(self) -> tuple[Optional[ChatSummary], str]:
0038 |         """Rotate the active chat.
0039 | 
0040 |         Returns (summary_of_old_chat, new_chat_id).
0041 |         """
0042 |         old_chat = self._active_chat.chat
0043 |         summary: Optional[ChatSummary] = None
0044 | 
0045 |         if old_chat and old_chat.messages:
0046 |             self._archive_chat(old_chat.chat_id)
0047 | 
0048 |             summary = self._summarizer.summarize_chat(
0049 |                 old_chat.chat_id, old_chat.messages
0050 |             )
0051 | 
0052 |         self._active_chat.clear()
0053 |         new_id = self._active_chat.create_new()
0054 | 
0055 |         return summary, new_id
0056 | 
0057 |     def check_and_rotate(self) -> Optional[tuple[ChatSummary, str]]:
0058 |         """Rotate if thresholds exceeded. Returns None if no rotation needed."""
0059 |         if not self.needs_rotation():
0060 |             return None
0061 |         summary, new_id = self.rotate()
0062 |         return (summary, new_id) if summary else None

0068 |             return

0027 | You are a conversation summarizer for the MAYA AI assistant.
0028 | 
0029 | Given a conversation, produce a JSON object with EXACTLY these fields:
0030 | {
0031 |     "summary": "<2-4 sentence summary of the conversation>",
0032 |     "key_topics": ["topic1", "topic2"],
0033 |     "important_facts": ["fact1", "fact2"],
0034 |     "projects": ["project names mentioned or worked on"],
0035 |     "decisions": ["decisions made during the conversation"],
0036 |     "todos": ["action items or todos identified"]
0037 | }
0038 | 
0039 | RULES:
0040 | 1. Output ONLY valid JSON. No markdown fences, no explanation.
0041 | 2. Be concise. Each fact/topic should be one clear sentence or phrase.
0042 | 3. Focus on information that would be useful to recall in future conversations.
0043 | 4. Capture user preferences, project details, and recurring patterns.
0044 | 5. If a field has no items, use an empty list [].
0045 | """)
0046 | 
0047 | _MEMORY_EXTRACTION_PROMPT = textwrap.dedent("""\
0048 | You are a memory extraction system for the MAYA AI assistant.
0049 | 
0050 | Given a conversation, extract memories worth keeping long-term.
0051 | Each memory must have a category, content, and importance score (0.0-1.0).
0052 | 
0053 | Categories: projects, people, preferences, goals, facts, skills, recurring_tasks, decisions
0054 | 
0055 | Output a JSON array of memory objects:
0056 | [
0057 |     {
0058 |         "category": "projects",
0059 |         "content": "User is working on Project X using Python",
0060 |         "importance": 0.85,
0061 |         "tags": ["project-x", "python"]
0062 |     }
0063 | ]
0064 | 
0065 | RULES:
0066 | 1. Output ONLY a valid JSON array. No markdown, no explanation.
0067 | 2. Only include memories with importance >= 0.7.
0068 | 3. Be specific — "user prefers dark mode" not "user has preferences".
0069 | 4. Include tags for retrieval.
0070 | 5. If nothing is worth remembering, return [].
0071 | """)

0074 | def _extract_json_object(raw: str) -> str:
0075 |     raw = raw.strip()
0076 |     fence = re.search(r"```(?:json)?\s*\n?(.*?)```", raw, re.DOTALL)
0077 |     if fence:
0078 |         raw = fence.group(1).strip()
0079 |     start = raw.find("{")
0080 |     if start == -1:
0081 |         return raw
0082 | 
0083 |     decoder = json.JSONDecoder()
0084 |     try:
0085 |         _, end_idx = decoder.raw_decode(raw, start)
0086 |         return raw[start:end_idx]
0087 |     except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
0088 |         pass
0089 | 
0090 |     depth = 0
0091 |     for i in range(start, len(raw)):
0092 |         if raw[i] == "{":
0093 |             depth += 1
0094 |         elif raw[i] == "}":
0095 |             depth -= 1
0096 |             if depth == 0:
0097 |                 return raw[start : i + 1]
0098 |     return raw[start:]
0099 | 
0100 | 
0101 | def _extract_json_array(raw: str) -> str:
0102 |     raw = raw.strip()
0103 |     fence = re.search(r"```(?:json)?\s*\n?(.*?)```", raw, re.DOTALL)
0104 |     if fence:
0105 |         raw = fence.group(1).strip()
0106 |     start = raw.find("[")
0107 |     if start == -1:
0108 |         return "[]"
0109 | 
0110 |     decoder = json.JSONDecoder()
0111 |     try:
0112 |         _, end_idx = decoder.raw_decode(raw, start)
0113 |         return raw[start:end_idx]
0114 |     except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
0115 |         pass
0116 | 
0117 |     depth = 0
0118 |     for i in range(start, len(raw)):
0119 |         if raw[i] == "[":
0120 |             depth += 1
0121 |         elif raw[i] == "]":
0122 |             depth -= 1
0123 |             if depth == 0:
0124 |                 return raw[start : i + 1]
0125 |     return raw[start:]
0126 |

0128 | class ChatSummarizer:
0129 |     """Generates chat summaries and extracts long-term memories."""
0130 | 
0131 |     def summarize_chat(
0132 |         self,
0133 |         chat_id: str,
0134 |         messages: list[ChatMessage],
0135 |     ) -> ChatSummary:
0136 |         """Produce a ChatSummary from a list of messages."""
0137 |         conversation_text = self._messages_to_text(messages)
0138 | 
0139 |         try:
0140 |             raw = self._call_llm(
0141 |                 _SUMMARIZER_PROMPT, f"CONVERSATION:\n{conversation_text}"
0142 |             )
0143 |             json_str = _extract_json_object(raw)
0144 |             data = json.loads(json_str)
0145 |         except Exception:
0146 |             data = self._fallback_summary(messages)
0147 | 
0148 |         summary = ChatSummary(
0149 |             chat_id=chat_id,
0150 |             summary=data.get("summary", ""),
0151 |             key_topics=data.get("key_topics", []),
0152 |             important_facts=data.get("important_facts", []),
0153 |             projects=data.get("projects", []),
0154 |             decisions=data.get("decisions", []),
0155 |             todos=data.get("todos", []),
0156 |             message_count=len(messages),
0157 |         )
0158 | 
0159 |         self._save_summary(summary)
0160 |         return summary
0161 | 
0162 |     def extract_memories(
0163 |         self,
0164 |         messages: list[ChatMessage],
0165 |         chat_id: Optional[str] = None,
0166 |     ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0167 |         """Extract long-term memories from conversation messages."""
0168 |         conversation_text = self._messages_to_text(messages)
0169 | 
0170 |         try:
0171 |             raw = self._call_llm(
0172 |                 _MEMORY_EXTRACTION_PROMPT,
0173 |                 f"CONVERSATION:\n{conversation_text}",
0174 |             )
0175 |             json_str = _extract_json_array(raw)
0176 |             memories = json.loads(json_str)
0177 |         except Exception:
0178 |             memories = []
0179 | 
0180 |         for mem in memories:
0181 |             mem["id"] = uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]
0182 |             if chat_id:
0183 |                 mem["source_chat_id"] = chat_id
0184 | 
0185 |         return memories
0186 | 
0187 |     def _call_llm(self, system_prompt: str, user_prompt: str) -> str:
0188 |         client = ollama.Client(host=MEMORY_OLLAMA_BASE_URL)
0189 |         response = client.chat(
0190 |             model=SUMMARIZER_MODEL,
0191 |             messages=[
0192 |                 {"role": "system", "content": system_prompt},
0193 |                 {"role": "user", "content": user_prompt},
0194 |             ],
0195 |             options={
0196 |                 "temperature": SUMMARIZER_TEMPERATURE,
0197 |                 "num_ctx": SUMMARIZER_NUM_CTX,
0198 |             },
0199 |         )
0200 |         return response.message.content or ""
0201 | 
0202 |     def _messages_to_text(self, messages: list[ChatMessage]) -> str:
0203 |         lines: list[str] = []
0204 |         for m in messages:
0205 |             lines.append(f"{m.role.value}: {m.content}")
0206 |         return "\n".join(lines)
0207 | 
0208 |     def _fallback_summary(self, messages: list[ChatMessage]) -> dict[str, Any]:
0209 |         user_msgs = [m.content for m in messages if m.role.value == "user"]
0210 |         topics = list({w for msg in user_msgs[:5] for w in msg.split()[:3]})
0211 |         return {
0212 |             "summary": f"Conversation with {len(messages)} messages.",
0213 |             "key_topics": topics[:5],
0214 |             "important_facts": [],
0215 |             "projects": [],
0216 |             "decisions": [],
0217 |             "todos": [],
0218 |         }
0219 |

0221 |         ensure_dirs()
0222 |         path = CHAT_SUMMARIES_DIR / f"{summary.chat_id}_summary.json"
0223 |         path.write_text(
0224 |             json.dumps(summary.model_dump(mode="json"), indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str),
0225 |             encoding="utf-8",
0226 |         )

Source Code Dump

0001 | """Context builder — assembles an optimized context package for the planner.
0002 | 
0003 | Pulls from: active chat, long-term memory, vector memory, agent history.
0004 | Minimizes token usage while maximizing relevance.
0005 | """
0006 | 
0007 | from __future__ import annotations
0008 | 
0009 | from typing import Any, Optional
0010 | 
0011 | from memory.active_chat import ActiveChat
0012 | from memory.agent_history import AgentHistory
0013 | from memory.config import CONTEXT_MAX_TOKENS, RECENT_MESSAGES_LIMIT
0014 | from memory.long_term_memory import LongTermMemory
0015 | from memory.planner_history import PlannerHistory
0016 | from memory.vector_memory import VectorMemory
0017 | 
0018 | 
0019 | def _estimate_tokens(text: str) -> int:
0020 |     return len(text) // 4 + 1
0021 | 
0022 | 
0023 | def _truncate_to_tokens(text: str, max_tokens: int) -> str:
0024 |     max_chars = max_tokens * 4
0025 |     if len(text) <= max_chars:
0026 |         return text
0027 |     return text[:max_chars] + "\n[...truncated]"
0028 | 
0029 | 
0030 | class ContextBuilder:
0031 |     """Builds an optimized context string for the planner/response generator."""
0032 | 
0033 |     def __init__(
0034 |         self,
0035 |         active_chat: ActiveChat,
0036 |         long_term: LongTermMemory,
0037 |         vector: VectorMemory,
0038 |         agent_history: AgentHistory,
0039 |         planner_history: PlannerHistory,
0040 |     ) -> None:
0041 |         self._active_chat = active_chat
0042 |         self._long_term = long_term
0043 |         self._vector = vector
0044 |         self._agent_history = agent_history
0045 |         self._planner_history = planner_history
0046 | 
0047 |     def build(
0048 |         self,
0049 |         command: str,
0050 |         *,
0051 |         max_tokens: int = CONTEXT_MAX_TOKENS,
0052 |         include_vectors: bool = True,
0053 |     ) -> str:
0054 |         """Build a context string for *command*, staying under *max_tokens*."""
0055 |         sections: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []
0056 |         budget = max_tokens
0057 | 
0058 |         # 1. Recent conversation (highest priority)
0059 |         recent_text = self._active_chat.get_messages_as_text(
0060 |             limit=RECENT_MESSAGES_LIMIT
0061 |         )
0062 |         if recent_text:
0063 |             tokens = _estimate_tokens(recent_text)
0064 |             allocation = min(tokens, budget // 3)
0065 |             recent_text = _truncate_to_tokens(recent_text, allocation)
0066 |             sections.append(("RECENT CONVERSATION", recent_text, _estimate_tokens(recent_text)))
0067 |             budget -= _estimate_tokens(recent_text)
0068 | 
0069 |         # 2. Relevant long-term memories
0070 |         lt_results = self._long_term.search_memories(command, limit=5)
0071 |         if lt_results:
0072 |             lt_lines = [f"- {m.content}" for m in lt_results]
0073 |             lt_text = "\n".join(lt_lines)
0074 |             tokens = _estimate_tokens(lt_text)
0075 |             allocation = min(tokens, budget // 3)
0076 |             lt_text = _truncate_to_tokens(lt_text, allocation)
0077 |             sections.append(("RELEVANT MEMORIES", lt_text, _estimate_tokens(lt_text)))
0078 |             budget -= _estimate_tokens(lt_text)
0079 | 
0080 |         # 3. Vector search for semantic matches
0081 |         if include_vectors and budget > 200:
0082 |             try:
0083 |                 vec_results = self._vector.search(command, top_k=3)
0084 |                 if vec_results:
0085 |                     vec_lines = [f"- {r['text'][:200]}" for r in vec_results if r.get("text")]
0086 |                     if vec_lines:
0087 |                         vec_text = "\n".join(vec_lines)
0088 |                         vec_text = _truncate_to_tokens(vec_text, budget // 3)
0089 |                         sections.append(("RELATED CONTEXT", vec_text, _estimate_tokens(vec_text)))
0090 |                         budget -= _estimate_tokens(vec_text)
0091 |             except Exception:
0092 |                 pass
0093 | 
0094 |         # 4. Recent agent history
0095 |         if budget > 100:
0096 |             history_text = self._agent_history.get_recent_as_text(limit=5)
0097 |             if history_text:
0098 |                 history_text = _truncate_to_tokens(history_text, min(budget // 2, 500))
0099 |                 sections.append(("RECENT ACTIONS", history_text, _estimate_tokens(history_text)))
0100 | 
0101 |         # Assemble
0102 |         parts: list[str] = []
0103 |         for header, content, _ in sections:
0104 |             parts.append(f"--- {header} ---")
0105 |             parts.append(content)
0106 |         return "\n\n".join(parts)
0107 | 
0108 |     def build_compact(self, command: str) -> str:
0109 |         """Minimal context — recent chat + top memories only."""
0110 |         parts: list[str] = []
0111 | 
0112 |         recent = self._active_chat.get_messages_as_text(limit=5)
0113 |         if recent:
0114 |             parts.append(recent)
0115 | 
0116 |         memories = self._long_term.search_memories(command, limit=3)
0117 |         if memories:
0118 |             mem_text = " | ".join(m.content for m in memories)
0119 |             parts.append(f"Memories: {mem_text}")
0120 | 
0121 |         return "\n".join(parts)

0035 |     def load(self) -> None:
0036 |         ensure_dirs()

0039 |                 LONG_TERM_MEMORY_PATH.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
0040 |             )
0041 |             self._store = LongTermMemoryStore.model_validate(data)
0042 |         else:
0043 |             self._store = LongTermMemoryStore()
0044 |             self._save()
0045 | 
0046 |     def _save(self) -> None:
0047 |         ensure_dirs()

0049 |         LONG_TERM_MEMORY_PATH.write_text(
0050 |             json.dumps(
0051 |                 self.store.model_dump(mode="json"),
0052 |                 indent=2,
0053 |                 ensure_ascii=False,
0054 |                 default=str,
0055 |             ),
0056 |             encoding="utf-8",
0057 |         )

0059 |     def add_memory(
0060 |         self,
0061 |         category: str,
0062 |         content: str,
0063 |         importance: float,
0064 |         *,
0065 |         source_chat_id: Optional[str] = None,
0066 |         tags: Optional[list[str]] = None,
0067 |         metadata: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,
0068 |     ) -> Optional[str]:
0069 |         """Add a memory if it meets the importance threshold. Returns the ID or None."""
0070 |         if importance < IMPORTANCE_THRESHOLD:
0071 |             return None
0072 | 
0073 |         cat = MemoryCategory(category)
0074 |         if self._is_duplicate(cat, content):
0075 |             return None
0076 | 
0077 |         entry = MemoryEntry(
0078 |             id=uuid.uuid4().hex[:12],
0079 |             category=cat,
0080 |             content=content,
0081 |             importance=importance,
0082 |             source_chat_id=source_chat_id,
0083 |             tags=tags or [],
0084 |             metadata=metadata or {},
0085 |         )
0086 |         self.store.memories[cat.value].append(entry)
0087 |         self._save()
0088 |         return entry.id
0089 | 
0090 |     def add_memories_batch(self, memories: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> list[str]:
0091 |         """Add multiple memories at once. Returns list of stored IDs."""
0092 |         stored: list[str] = []
0093 |         for mem in memories:
0094 |             mid = self.add_memory(
0095 |                 category=mem.get("category", "facts"),
0096 |                 content=mem.get("content", ""),
0097 |                 importance=mem.get("importance", 0.0),

0099 |                 tags=mem.get("tags", []),

0102 |             if mid:
0103 |                 stored.append(mid)
0104 |         return stored
0105 | 
0106 |     def get_memories(self, category: Optional[str] = None) -> list[MemoryEntry]:
0107 |         if category:
0108 |             return list(self.store.memories.get(category, []))
0109 |         all_memories: list[MemoryEntry] = []
0110 |         for entries in self.store.memories.values():
0111 |             all_memories.extend(entries)
0112 |         return all_memories
0113 | 
0114 |     def search_memories(
0115 |         self,
0116 |         query: str,
0117 |         category: Optional[str] = None,
0118 |         limit: int = 10,
0119 |     ) -> list[MemoryEntry]:
0120 |         """Simple keyword search across memories."""
0121 |         query_lower = query.lower()
0122 |         query_words = set(query_lower.split())
0123 |         candidates = self.get_memories(category)
0124 | 
0125 |         scored: list[tuple[float, MemoryEntry]] = []
0126 |         for mem in candidates:
0127 |             content_lower = mem.content.lower()
0128 |             tag_text = " ".join(mem.tags).lower()
0129 | 
0130 |             if query_lower in content_lower:
0131 |                 score = 1.0
0132 |             else:
0133 |                 matches = sum(1 for w in query_words if w in content_lower or w in tag_text)
0134 |                 score = matches / max(len(query_words), 1)
0135 | 
0136 |             if score > 0:
0137 |                 scored.append((score * mem.importance, mem))
0138 | 
0139 |         scored.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
0140 |         return [mem for _, mem in scored[:limit]]
0141 | 
0142 |     def update_memory(
0143 |         self,
0144 |         memory_id: str,
0145 |         content: Optional[str] = None,
0146 |         importance: Optional[float] = None,
0147 |         tags: Optional[list[str]] = None,
0148 |     ) -> bool:
0149 |         for entries in self.store.memories.values():
0150 |             for entry in entries:
0151 |                 if entry.id == memory_id:
0152 |                     if content is not None:
0153 |                         entry.content = content
0154 |                     if importance is not None:
0155 |                         entry.importance = importance
0156 |                     if tags is not None:
0157 |                         entry.tags = tags
0158 |                     entry.updated_at = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc)
0159 |                     self._save()
0160 |                     return True
0161 |         return False
0162 | 
0163 |     def delete_memory(self, memory_id: str) -> bool:
0164 |         for cat, entries in self.store.memories.items():
0165 |             for i, entry in enumerate(entries):
0166 |                 if entry.id == memory_id:
0167 |                     entries.pop(i)
0168 |                     self._save()
0169 |                     return True
0170 |         return False
0171 | 
0172 |     def get_memory_by_id(self, memory_id: str) -> Optional[MemoryEntry]:
0173 |         for entries in self.store.memories.values():
0174 |             for entry in entries:
0175 |                 if entry.id == memory_id:
0176 |                     return entry
0177 |         return None
0178 | 
0179 |     def get_summary(self) -> dict[str, int]:
0180 |         return {
0181 |             cat: len(entries)
0182 |             for cat, entries in self.store.memories.items()
0183 |         }
0184 | 
0185 |     def get_all_as_text(self, max_per_category: int = 5) -> str:
0186 |         """Compact text representation for context building."""
0187 |         parts: list[str] = []
0188 |         for cat, entries in self.store.memories.items():
0189 |             if not entries:
0190 |                 continue
0191 |             top = sorted(entries, key=lambda e: e.importance, reverse=True)[:max_per_category]
0192 |             parts.append(f"[{cat.upper()}]")
0193 |             for e in top:
0194 |                 parts.append(f"- {e.content}")
0195 |         return "\n".join(parts)
0196 | 
0197 |     def _is_duplicate(self, category: MemoryCategory, content: str) -> bool:

0200 |             if entry.content.lower().strip() == content_lower:
0201 |                 return True
0202 |         return False

0024 |             month = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m")
0025 |             self._file = PLANNER_HISTORY_DIR / f"planner_history_{month}.jsonl"
0026 |         return self._file
0027 | 
0028 |     def record(
0029 |         self,

0050 |         path = self._get_file()

0052 |             fh.write(line + "\n")
0053 | 
0054 |     def get_recent(self, limit: int = 10) -> list[PlannerHistoryEntry]:

0057 |     def get_recent_as_text(self, limit: int = 5) -> str:

0062 |             task_count = len(e.plan_json.get("tasks", []))
0063 |             lines.append(f"  Plan: {task_count} tasks, Response: {e.response[:80]}...")

0065 | 
0066 |     def load_recent_from_disk(self, limit: int = 30) -> None:
0067 |         path = self._get_file()
0068 |         if not path.exists():
0069 |             return
0070 |         lines = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip().split("\n")
0071 |         entries: list[PlannerHistoryEntry] = []
0072 |         for line in lines[-limit:]:
0073 |             if line.strip():
0074 |                 try:
0075 |                     data = json.loads(line)
0076 |                     entries.append(PlannerHistoryEntry.model_validate(data))
0077 |                 except Exception:
0078 |                     continue

0013 | class RecoveryManager:
0014 |     """Manages brain_state.json for crash recovery."""
0015 | 
0016 |     def __init__(self) -> None:
0017 |         self._state: Optional[BrainState] = None
0018 | 
0019 |     @property
0020 |     def state(self) -> BrainState:
0021 |         if self._state is None:
0022 |             self.load()
0023 |         assert self._state is not None
0024 |         return self._state
0025 | 
0026 |     def load(self) -> BrainState:
0027 |         ensure_dirs()
0028 |         if BRAIN_STATE_PATH.exists():
0029 |             try:
0030 |                 data = json.loads(
0031 |                     BRAIN_STATE_PATH.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
0032 |                 )
0033 |                 self._state = BrainState.model_validate(data)
0034 |             except Exception:
0035 |                 self._state = BrainState()
0036 |                 self._save()
0037 |         else:
0038 |             self._state = BrainState()
0039 |             self._save()
0040 |         return self._state
0041 | 
0042 |     def _save(self) -> None:
0043 |         ensure_dirs()
0044 |         self.state.last_updated = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc)
0045 |         BRAIN_STATE_PATH.write_text(
0046 |             json.dumps(
0047 |                 self.state.model_dump(mode="json"),
0048 |                 indent=2,
0049 |                 ensure_ascii=False,
0050 |                 default=str,
0051 |             ),
0052 |             encoding="utf-8",
0053 |         )
0054 |

0056 |         self.state.active_chat_id = chat_id
0057 |         self._save()

0061 |         self._save()

0068 |         self.state.queue_state = queue_state
0069 |         self._save()

0107 |         if project is not None:

0110 |             self.state.unfinished_tasks = unfinished_tasks
0111 |         if queue_state is not None:
0112 |             self.state.queue_state = queue_state

0001 | """Vector memory using ChromaDB for semantic retrieval."""
0002 | 
0003 | from __future__ import annotations
0004 | 
0005 | import uuid
0006 | from datetime import datetime, timezone
0007 | from typing import Any, Optional
0008 | 
0009 | import chromadb
0010 | from chromadb.config import Settings
0011 | 
0012 | from memory.config import (
0013 |     VECTOR_COLLECTION_NAME,
0014 |     VECTOR_TOP_K,
0015 |     VECTORS_DIR,
0016 |     ensure_dirs,
0017 | )
0018 | 
0019 | 
0020 | class VectorMemory:
0021 |     """Wraps ChromaDB for embedding-based memory retrieval."""
0022 | 
0023 |     def __init__(self) -> None:
0024 |         self._client: Optional[chromadb.ClientAPI] = None
0025 |         self._collection: Optional[chromadb.Collection] = None
0026 | 
0027 |     @property
0028 |     def collection(self) -> chromadb.Collection:
0029 |         if self._collection is None:
0030 |             self._init_db()
0031 |         assert self._collection is not None
0032 |         return self._collection
0033 | 
0034 |     def _init_db(self) -> None:
0035 |         ensure_dirs()
0036 |         self._client = chromadb.PersistentClient(
0037 |             path=str(VECTORS_DIR),
0038 |             settings=Settings(anonymized_telemetry=False),
0039 |         )
0040 |         self._collection = self._client.get_or_create_collection(
0041 |             name=VECTOR_COLLECTION_NAME,
0042 |             metadata={"hnsw:space": "cosine"},
0043 |         )
0044 | 
0045 |     def add(
0046 |         self,
0047 |         text: str,
0048 |         *,
0049 |         doc_type: str = "memory",
0050 |         source_id: Optional[str] = None,
0051 |         metadata: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,
0052 |     ) -> str:
0053 |         """Add a text document to the vector store. Returns the document ID."""
0054 |         doc_id = uuid.uuid4().hex[:16]
0055 |         meta: dict[str, Any] = {
0056 |             "type": doc_type,
0057 |             "created_at": datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc).isoformat(),
0058 |         }
0059 |         if source_id:
0060 |             meta["source_id"] = source_id
0061 |         if metadata:
0062 |             for k, v in metadata.items():
0063 |                 if isinstance(v, (str, int, float, bool)):
0064 |                     meta[k] = v
0065 | 
0066 |         self.collection.add(
0067 |             ids=[doc_id],
0068 |             documents=[text],
0069 |             metadatas=[meta],
0070 |         )
0071 |         return doc_id
0072 | 
0073 |     def add_batch(
0074 |         self,
0075 |         texts: list[str],
0076 |         *,
0077 |         doc_type: str = "memory",
0078 |         metadatas: Optional[list[dict[str, Any]]] = None,
0079 |     ) -> list[str]:
0080 |         """Add multiple documents at once."""
0081 |         if not texts:
0082 |             return []
0083 |         ids = [uuid.uuid4().hex[:16] for _ in texts]
0084 |         now = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc).isoformat()
0085 | 
0086 |         metas: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0087 |         for i, text in enumerate(texts):
0088 |             meta: dict[str, Any] = {"type": doc_type, "created_at": now}
0089 |             if metadatas and i < len(metadatas):
0090 |                 for k, v in metadatas[i].items():
0091 |                     if isinstance(v, (str, int, float, bool)):
0092 |                         meta[k] = v
0093 |             metas.append(meta)
0094 | 
0095 |         self.collection.add(ids=ids, documents=texts, metadatas=metas)
0096 |         return ids
0097 | 
0098 |     def search(
0099 |         self,
0100 |         query: str,
0101 |         top_k: int = VECTOR_TOP_K,
0102 |         doc_type: Optional[str] = None,
0103 |     ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
0104 |         """Semantic search. Returns list of {id, text, score, metadata}."""
0105 |         where = {"type": doc_type} if doc_type else None
0106 | 
0107 |         results = self.collection.query(
0108 |             query_texts=[query],
0109 |             n_results=top_k,
0110 |             where=where,
0111 |         )
0112 | 
0113 |         out: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
0114 |         if not results or not results["ids"]:
0115 |             return out
0116 | 
0117 |         ids = results["ids"][0]
0118 |         docs = results["documents"][0] if results["documents"] else []
0119 |         distances = results["distances"][0] if results["distances"] else []
0120 |         metas = results["metadatas"][0] if results["metadatas"] else []
0121 | 
0122 |         for i, doc_id in enumerate(ids):
0123 |             out.append({
0124 |                 "id": doc_id,
0125 |                 "text": docs[i] if i < len(docs) else "",
0126 |                 "score": 1.0 - (distances[i] if i < len(distances) else 0.0),
0127 |                 "metadata": metas[i] if i < len(metas) else {},
0128 |             })
0129 |         return out
0130 | 
0131 |     def delete(self, doc_id: str) -> None:
0132 |         self.collection.delete(ids=[doc_id])
0133 | 
0134 |     def count(self) -> int:
0135 |         return self.collection.count()
0136 | 
0137 |     def clear(self) -> None:
0138 |         if self._client:
0139 |             self._client.delete_collection(VECTOR_COLLECTION_NAME)
0140 |             self._collection = None
0141 |             self._init_db()
0142 |

0579 | # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
0580 | # Runner
0581 | # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
0582 | 
0583 | def _run_all() -> int:
0584 |     """Run all test_* functions, report results."""
0585 |     tests = [
0586 |         (name, func)
0587 |         for name, func in sorted(globals().items())
0588 |         if name.startswith("test_") and callable(func)
0589 |     ]
0590 | 
0591 |     passed = failed = 0
0592 |     for name, func in tests:
0593 |         try:
0594 |             func()
0595 |             print(f"  PASS  {name}")
0596 |             passed += 1
0597 |         except AssertionError as exc:
0598 |             print(f"  FAIL  {name}: {exc}")
0599 |             failed += 1
0600 |         except Exception as exc:
0601 |             print(f"  ERROR {name}: {exc}")
0602 |             failed += 1
0603 | 
0604 |     print(f"\n{passed} passed, {failed} failed out of {len(tests)} tests")
0605 |     return 0 if failed == 0 else 1
0606 | 
0607 | 
0608 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0609 |     raise SystemExit(_run_all())
0610 |

Tests for the Memory Layer.

Runs without Ollama — LLM calls in the summarizer are mocked.
ChromaDB uses an ephemeral/temp directory.

0801 | def _run_all() -> int:
0802 |     tests = [
0803 |         (name, func)
0804 |         for name, func in sorted(globals().items())
0805 |         if name.startswith("test_") and callable(func)
0806 |     ]
0807 | 
0808 |     passed = failed = 0
0809 |     for name, func in tests:
0810 |         try:
0811 |             func()
0812 |             print(f"  PASS  {name}")
0813 |             passed += 1
0814 |         except AssertionError as exc:
0815 |             print(f"  FAIL  {name}: {exc}")
0816 |             failed += 1
0817 |         except Exception as exc:
0818 |             print(f"  ERROR {name}: {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}")
0819 |             failed += 1
0820 | 
0821 |     print(f"\n{passed} passed, {failed} failed out of {len(tests)} tests")
0822 |     _cleanup()
0823 |     return 0 if failed == 0 else 1

0001 | """JSONL logging for voice events."""
0002 | 
0003 | from __future__ import annotations
0004 | 
0005 | import json
0006 | import threading
0007 | from datetime import datetime, timezone
0008 | from typing import Any
0009 | 
0010 | from voice.config import VOICE_LOGS_DIR
0011 | 
0012 | _lock = threading.Lock()
0013 | 
0014 | 
0015 | def log_voice(event: str, **kwargs: Any) -> None:
0016 |     VOICE_LOGS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
0017 |     record = {
0018 |         "event": event,
0019 |         "timestamp": datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc).isoformat(),
0020 |         **kwargs,
0021 |     }
0022 |     line = json.dumps(record, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) + "\n"
0023 |     with _lock:
0024 |         with open(VOICE_LOGS_DIR / "voice.jsonl", "a", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
0025 |             fh.write(line)
0026 | 


================================================================================
Module: voice\voice_orchestrator.py
================================================================================

Module Docstring:
Voice orchestrator — JARVIS-style always-on listening adapted for MAYA.

Flow:
    1. Always-on mic via speech_recognition.listen()
    2. Fast transcribe (base.en) → check for wake word "Maya"
    3. If no wake word → ignore, keep listening
    4. If wake word found → accurate transcribe (small.en)
    5. Strip wake word from command
    6. If bare wake word (no command) → greet + listen once for follow-up
    7. Speak filler (async) → process command with Brain (mic blocked — TTS is blocking)
    8. Speak final response (blocking — mic stays off until done)
    9. Back to step 1

3-min conversation window: after the first wake word, subsequent commands
don't need the wake word. After 3 min of no commands → require wake word again.

Usage:
    from voice.voice_orchestrator import VoiceOrchestrator
    orch = VoiceOrchestrator()
    orch.run()

Classes:
  - VoiceOrchestrator

Functions:
  - _ensure_loaded
  - _to_numpy
  - _transcribe_fast
    Docstring: Fast wake-word check with base.en model....
  - _transcribe_accurate
    Docstring: Accurate command transcription with small.en model....
  - _is_wakeish
  - has_wake
  - strip_wake
  - _is_real_command
  - pick_filler

0132 |     if _wake_model is not None:
0133 |         return
0134 |     import speech_recognition as sr
0135 |     from faster_whisper import WhisperModel
0136 |     _sr = sr
0137 |     _recog = sr.Recognizer()
0138 |     _recog.dynamic_energy_threshold = True
0139 |     _recog.pause_threshold = END_SILENCE
0140 |     manual = os.getenv("JARVIS_MIC_THRESHOLD")
0141 |     if manual:
0142 |         _recog.energy_threshold = float(manual)
0143 |     print(f"[maya] loading wake model ({WAKE_MODEL_NAME})...")
0144 |     _wake_model = WhisperModel(WAKE_MODEL_NAME, device="auto", compute_type="int8")
0145 | 
0146 | 
0147 | def _to_numpy(audio) -> np.ndarray:
0148 |     raw = audio.get_raw_data(convert_rate=16000, convert_width=2)
0149 |     return np.frombuffer(raw, dtype=np.int16)
0150 | 
0151 | 
0152 | def _transcribe_fast(audio) -> str:
0153 |     """Fast wake-word check with base.en model."""
0154 |     samples = _to_numpy(audio).astype(np.float32) / 32768.0
0155 |     segments, _ = _wake_model.transcribe(
0156 |         samples, beam_size=1, language="en", vad_filter=True,
0157 |         condition_on_previous_text=False, without_timestamps=True)
0158 |     return " ".join(s.text for s in segments).strip().lower()
0159 | 
0160 | 
0161 | def _transcribe_accurate(audio) -> str:
0162 |     """Accurate command transcription with small.en model."""
0163 |     import voice_text
0164 |     return voice_text.transcribe_local(_to_numpy(audio), 16000)
0165 | 
0166 | 
0167 | def _is_wakeish(token: str) -> bool:
0168 |     t = re.sub(r"[^a-z]", "", token.lower())
0169 |     if len(t) < 3:
0170 |         return False
0171 |     if any(t == w or (len(w) >= 4 and (t in w or w in t)) for w in WAKE_WORDS):
0172 |         return True
0173 |     return any(difflib.SequenceMatcher(None, t, w).ratio() >= 0.76 for w in WAKE_WORDS)
0174 | 
0175 | 
0176 | def has_wake(text: str) -> bool:
0177 |     low = text.lower()
0178 |     if any(w in low for w in WAKE_WORDS):
0179 |         return True
0180 |     name = NAME.lower()
0181 |     return any(len(re.sub(r"[^a-z]", "", tok)) >= 3
0182 |                and difflib.SequenceMatcher(None, re.sub(r"[^a-z]", "", tok), name).ratio() >= 0.8
0183 |                for tok in low.split())
0184 | 
0185 | 
0186 | def strip_wake(text: str) -> str:
0187 |     t = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", _WAKE_RE.sub(" ", text)).strip(" ,.!?-")
0188 |     t = _LEAD_FILLER.sub("", t)
0189 |     parts = t.split(" ", 1)
0190 |     if parts and _is_wakeish(parts[0]):
0191 |         t = parts[1] if len(parts) > 1 else ""
0192 |     t = _LEAD_FILLER.sub("", t)
0193 |     return t.strip(" ,.!?-")
0194 | 
0195 | 
0196 | def _is_real_command(text: str) -> bool:
0197 |     low = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9' ]", " ", (text or "").lower()).strip()
0198 |     low = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", low)
0199 |     if len(low) < 4 or len(low.split()) < 2:
0200 |         return False
0201 |     return low not in _NOISE_PHRASES
0202 | 
0203 | 
0204 | def pick_filler(text: str) -> str:
0205 |     low = text.lower()
0206 |     for keywords, domain in DOMAIN_KEYWORDS:
0207 |         if any(k in low for k in keywords):
0208 |             return random.choice(CONTEXT_FILLERS[domain])
0209 |     return random.choice(SLOW_FILLERS)
