0212 | # ── The orchestrator ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0213 | class VoiceOrchestrator:
0214 |     def __init__(self) -> None:
0215 |         self._brain: Any = None
0216 |         self._running = False
0217 |         self._bg_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None
0218 |         self._greet_i = 0
0219 |         self._conversation_active = False
0220 |         self._last_activity: float = 0.0
0221 | 
0222 |     def _get_brain(self):
0223 |         if self._brain is None:
0224 |             from brain.brain import Brain
0225 |             self._brain = Brain(enable_memory=True)
0226 |             log_voice("brain_initialized")
0227 |         return self._brain
0228 | 
0229 |     # ── TTS helpers (use maya_tts) ────────────────────────────────────────
0230 | 
0231 |     @staticmethod
0232 |     def say(text: str) -> None:
0233 |         import maya_tts
0234 |         maya_tts.speak(text)
0235 | 
0236 |     @staticmethod
0237 |     def say_async(text: str):
0238 |         import maya_tts
0239 |         return maya_tts.speak_async(text)
0240 | 
0241 |     def greet(self) -> None:
0242 |         self.say(GREETINGS[self._greet_i % len(GREETINGS)])
0243 |         self._greet_i += 1
0244 | 
0245 |     # ── Conversation window ───────────────────────────────────────────────
0246 | 
0247 |     def _start_conversation(self) -> None:
0248 |         self._conversation_active = True
0249 |         self._last_activity = time.monotonic()
0250 | 
0251 |     def _touch(self) -> None:
0252 |         self._last_activity = time.monotonic()
0253 | 
0254 |     def _conversation_timed_out(self) -> bool:
0255 |         if not self._conversation_active:
0256 |             return False
0257 |         return (time.monotonic() - self._last_activity) > CONVERSATION_TIMEOUT
0258 | 
0259 |     def _end_conversation(self) -> None:
0260 |         self._conversation_active = False
0261 |         log_voice("conversation_ended")
0262 | 
0263 |     # ── Main loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0264 | 
0265 |     def run(self) -> None:
0266 |         if not VOICE_MODE_ENABLED:
0267 |             print("[maya] VOICE_MODE_ENABLED=false, exiting.")
0268 |             return
0269 | 
0270 |         self._running = True
0271 |         _ensure_loaded()
0272 | 
0273 |         # Pre-warm TTS + STT in background
0274 |         import maya_tts
0275 |         import voice_text
0276 |         threading.Thread(target=maya_tts.warm, daemon=True).start()
0277 |         threading.Thread(
0278 |             target=lambda: voice_text.transcribe_local(np.zeros(1600, dtype=np.int16), 16000),
0279 |             daemon=True).start()
0280 | 
0281 |         with _sr.Microphone(sample_rate=16000) as src:
0282 |             print("[maya] adjusting for ambient noise (~1s)...")
0283 |             _recog.adjust_for_ambient_noise(src, duration=1.0)
0284 |             _recog.energy_threshold = max(_recog.energy_threshold, 200)
0285 |             print(f"[maya] energy threshold = {_recog.energy_threshold:.0f}")
0286 | 
0287 |             self.say(f"{NAME_CAP} is online. Say my name to activate.")
0288 |             print(f"[maya] listening — say '{NAME}' to activate.\n")
0289 | 
0290 |             while self._running:
0291 |                 try:
0292 |                     self._listen(src)
0293 |                 except KeyboardInterrupt:
0294 |                     break
0295 |                 except Exception as exc:
0296 |                     log_voice("listen_error", error=str(exc))
0297 |                     print(f"[error] {exc}")
0298 |                     time.sleep(0.5)
0299 | 
0300 |         self._shutdown()
0301 | 
0302 |     def run_in_background(self) -> None:
0303 |         if self._bg_thread and self._bg_thread.is_alive():
0304 |             return
0305 |         self._bg_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True)
0306 |         self._bg_thread.start()
0307 | 
0308 |     def stop(self) -> None:
0309 |         self._running = False
0310 |         import maya_tts
0311 |         maya_tts.request_stop()
0312 | 
0313 |     # ── Single listen cycle ───────────────────────────────────────────────
0314 | 
0315 |     def _listen(self, src) -> None:
0316 |         # Check conversation timeout
0317 |         if self._conversation_active and self._conversation_timed_out():
0318 |             print("\n😴 No activity for 3 minutes — going to sleep.")
0319 |             self.say("Going to sleep. Say Maya to wake me up.")
0320 |             self._end_conversation()
0321 |             return
0322 | 
0323 |         # Capture audio
0324 |         try:
0325 |             audio = _recog.listen(src, timeout=10 if self._conversation_active else None,
0326 |                                  phrase_time_limit=15)
0327 |         except Exception:
0328 |             if self._conversation_active and self._conversation_timed_out():
0329 |                 print("\n😴 No activity for 3 minutes — going to sleep.")
0330 |                 self.say("Going to sleep. Say Maya to wake me up.")
0331 |                 self._end_conversation()
0332 |             return
0333 | 
0334 |         # Fast transcription (base.en) — check for wake word
0335 |         gist = _transcribe_fast(audio)
0336 |         if not gist:
0337 |             return
0338 | 
0339 |         # In conversation mode: accept commands without wake word
0340 |         if self._conversation_active:
0341 |             # Check for sleep commands
0342 |             low = gist.lower()
0343 |             if any(p in low for p in SLEEP_PHRASES):
0344 |                 self.say("Going to sleep. Goodbye.")
0345 |                 self._end_conversation()
0346 |                 return
0347 | 
0348 |             # Check for stop words
0349 |             words = low.split()
0350 |             if len(words) <= 3 and any(w in STOP_WORDS for w in words):
0351 |                 self.say("Okay.")
0352 |                 self._end_conversation()
0353 |                 return
0354 | 
0355 |             # In conversation mode — process without requiring wake word
0356 |             if has_wake(gist):
0357 |                 accurate = _transcribe_accurate(audio) or gist
0358 |                 command = strip_wake(accurate)
0359 |             else:
0360 |                 # No wake word but conversation active — treat entire utterance as command
0361 |                 accurate = _transcribe_accurate(audio) or gist
0362 |                 command = accurate.strip()
0363 | 
0364 |             if not _is_real_command(command):
0365 |                 return
0366 | 
0367 |             print(f"[heard] {accurate}")
0368 |             self._touch()
0369 |             self._process(command)
0370 |             return
0371 | 
0372 |         # Not in conversation — require wake word
0373 |         if not has_wake(gist):
0374 |             print(f"\r[idle] {gist[:60]:<60}", end="", flush=True)
0375 |             return
0376 | 
0377 |         # Wake word detected!
0378 |         print(f"\n🟢 Activated!")
0379 |         log_voice("wake_word_detected")
0380 |         self._start_conversation()
0381 | 
0382 |         # Accurate transcription
0383 |         accurate = _transcribe_accurate(audio) or gist
0384 |         command = strip_wake(accurate)
0385 |         print(f"[heard] {accurate}")
0386 | 
0387 |         if not command:
0388 |             # Bare wake word — greet and listen once for follow-up
0389 |             self.greet()
0390 |             try:
0391 |                 follow = _recog.listen(src, timeout=8, phrase_time_limit=15)
0392 |                 command = (_transcribe_accurate(follow) or "").strip()
0393 |             except Exception:
0394 |                 command = ""
0395 |             if command:
0396 |                 print(f"[heard] {command}")
0397 |             if not _is_real_command(command):
0398 |                 print("✅ Ready — listening for command...")
0399 |                 return
0400 | 
0401 |         self._touch()
0402 |         self._process(command)
0403 | 
0404 |     # ── Process a command (mic is blocked — TTS is synchronous) ───────────
0405 | 
0406 |     def _process(self, command: str) -> None:
0407 |         log_voice("command_received", command=command)
0408 | 
0409 |         # Speak context-aware filler async while brain processes
0410 |         filler = pick_filler(command)
0411 |         self.say_async(filler)
0412 | 
0413 |         try:
0414 |             brain = self._get_brain()
0415 |             start = time.perf_counter()
0416 |             response = brain.process(command)
0417 |             duration_ms = (time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000
0418 |             log_voice("brain_response", command=command[:100],
0419 |                       response=(response or "")[:200], duration_ms=round(duration_ms, 2))
0420 |         except Exception as exc:
0421 |             log_voice("brain_error", error=str(exc))
0422 |             response = "I encountered an issue while processing your request."
0423 | 
0424 |         # Stop any ongoing filler speech, then speak the real response
0425 |         import maya_tts
0426 |         maya_tts.request_stop()
0427 |         time.sleep(0.1)
0428 | 
0429 |         if response:
0430 |             print(f"[maya] {response}")
0431 |             self.say(response)  # blocking — mic stays off until done
0432 | 
0433 |         self._touch()
0434 |         print("✅ Ready — listening...")
0435 | 
0436 |     # ── Shutdown ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0437 | 
0438 |     def _shutdown(self) -> None:
0439 |         self._running = False
0440 |         self._end_conversation()
0441 |         log_voice("orchestrator_stop")
0442 |         print("\n[maya] stopped.")
0443 | 
0444 |     # ── Properties ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0445 | 
0446 |     @property
0447 |     def is_running(self) -> bool:
0448 |         return self._running
0449 | 
0450 | 
0451 | # ── CLI entry point ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
0452 | if __name__ == "__main__":
0453 |     orch = VoiceOrchestrator()
0454 |     try:
0455 |         orch.run()
0456 |     except KeyboardInterrupt:
0457 |         orch.stop()
0458 |         print("\nGoodbye.")
